Revākhaṇḍa of the Vāyupurāṇa
RKV adhyāya 
śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ  RKV 
oṃ namaḥ śrīpuruṣottamāya 
oṃ namaḥ śrīnarmadāyai 
oṃ namo hariharahiraṇyagarbhebhyo namo vyāsavālmīkiśukaparāśarebhyo namo gurugobrāhmaṇebhyaḥ 
oṃ majjanmātaṅgagaṇḍacyutamadamadirāmodamattālimālaṃ snānaiḥ siddhāṅganānāṃ kucayugavigalat kuṅkumāsaṅgapiṅgam 
sāyaṃ prātarmunīnāṃ kusumacayasamācchannatīrasthavṛkṣaṃ pāyādvo narmadāmbhaḥ karimakarakarākrāntarahaṃstaraṃgam  RKV 
ubhayataṭapuṇyatīrthā prakṣālitasakalalalokaduritaughā 
devamunimanujavandyā haratu sadā narmadā duritam  RKV 
nāśayatu duritamakhilaṃ bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhavacca bhuvi bhavinām 
sakalapavitri tava sudhā puṇyajalā narmadā bhavati  RKV 
taṭapulinaṃ śivadevā yasyā yatayo 'pi kāmayante vā 
muninivahavihitasevā śivāya mama jāyatāṃ revā  RKV 
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtvā naraṃ caiva narottamam 
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet  RKV 
naimiṣe puṇyanilaye nānāṛṣiniṣevite 
śaunakaḥ satramāsīnaḥ sūta papraccha vistarāt  RKV 
manye 'haṃ dharmanaipuṇyaṃ tvayi sūta sadārcitam 
puṇyāmṛtakathāvaktā vyāsasaśiṣyastvameva hi  RKV 
atastvāṃ paripṛcchāmi dharmatīrthāśrayaṃ kave 
bahūni santi tīrthāni bahuśo me śrutāni ca  RKV 
śrutā divyanadī brāhmī tathā viṣṇunadī mayā 
tṛtīyā na mayā kvāpi śrutā raudrī saridvarā  RKV 
tāṃ vedagarbhāṃ vikhyātāṃ vibudhaughābhivanditām 
vada me tvaṃ mahāprājña tīrthapūgapariṣkṛtām  RKV 
kaṃ deśam āśritā revā kathaṃ śrīrudrasaṃbhavā 
tatsaṃśritāni tīrthāni yāni tāni vadasva me  RKV 
sūta uvāca
sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ kulapate caritraṃ narmadāśritam 
citraṃ pavitraṃ doṣaghnaṃ śrutamuktaṃ ca sattama  RKV 
vedopavedavedāṅgādīnyabhivyasya pūritaḥ 
aṣṭādaśapurāṇānāṃ vaktā satyavatīsutaḥ  RKV 
taṃ namaskṛtya vakṣyāmi purāṇāni yathākramam 
yeṣām abhivyāharaṇād abhivṛddhir vṛṣāyuṣoḥ  RKV 
śrutiḥ smṛtiśca viprāṇāṃ cakṣuṣī parikīrtite 
kāṇastatraikayā hīno dvābhyāmandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  RKV 
śrutismṛtipurāṇāni viduṣāṃ locanatrayam 
yastribhirnayanaiḥ paśyet so 'ṃśo māheśvaro mataḥ  RKV 
ātmano vedavidyā ca īśvareṇa vinirmitā 
śaunakīyā ca paurāṇī dharmaśāstrātmikā ca yā  RKV 
tisro vidyā imā mukhyāḥ sarvaśāstravinirṇaye 
purāṇaṃ pañcamo veda iti brahmānuśāsanam  RKV 
yo na veda purāṇaṃ hi na sa vedātra kiṃcana 
katamaḥ sa hi dharmo 'sti kiṃ vā jñānaṃ tathāvidham  RKV 
anyadvā tatkimatrāha purāṇe yanna dṛśyate 
vedāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ pūrvaṃ purāṇe nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
bibhetyalpaśrutādvedo māmayaṃ pratariṣyati 
itihāsapurāṇaiśca kṛto'yaṃ niścayaḥ purā  RKV 
ātmā purāṇaṃ vedānāṃ pṛthagaṃgāni tāni ṣaṭ 
yacca dṛṣṭaṃ hi vedeṣu taddṛṣṭaṃ smṛtibhiḥ kila  RKV 
ubhābhyāṃ yattu dṛṣṭaṃ hi tatpurāṇeṣu gīyate 
purāṇaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ prathamaṃ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtam  RKV 
anantaraṃ ca vaktrebhyo vedāstasya vinirgatāḥ 
purāṇamekamevāsīd asmin kalpāntare mune  RKV 
trivargasādhanaṃ puṇyaṃ śatakoṭipravistaram 
smṛtvā jagāda ca munīnprati devaścaturmukhaḥ  RKV 
pravṛttiḥ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ purāṇasyābhavattataḥ 
kālenāgrahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā purāṇasya tato muniḥ  RKV 
vyāsarūpaṃ vibhuḥ kṛtvā saṃharetsa yuge yuge 
aṣṭalakṣapramāṇe tu dvāpare dvāpare sadā  RKV 
tadaṣṭādaśadhā kṛtvā bhūloke 'smin prabhāṣyate 
adyāpi devaloke tacchatakoṭipravistaram  RKV 
tathātra caturlakṣaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa niveśitam 
purāṇāni daśāṣṭau ca sāmprataṃ tadihocyate 
nāmatastāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tvamṛṣisattama  RKV 
sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvantarāṇi ca 
vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam  RKV 
brāhmaṃ purāṇaṃ tatrādyaṃ saṃhitāyāṃ vibhūṣitam 
ślokānāṃ daśasāhasraṃ nānāpuṇyakathāyutam  RKV 
pādmaṃ ca pañcapañcāśatsahasrāṇi nigadyate 
tṛtīyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃnāma trayoviṃśatisaṃkhyayā  RKV 
caturthaṃ vāyunā proktaṃ vāyavīyamiti smṛtam 
śivabhaktisamāyogācchaivaṃ taccāparākhyayā  RKV 
caturviṃśatisaṃkhyātaṃ sahasrāṇi tu śaunaka 
caturbhiḥ parvabhiḥ proktaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ pañcamaṃ tathā  RKV 
caturdaśasahasrāṇi tathā pañca śatāni tat 
mārkaṇḍaṃ navasāhasraṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ tatparikīrtitam  RKV 
āgneyaṃ saptamaṃ proktaṃ sahasrāṇi tu ṣoḍaśa 
aṣṭamaṃ nāradīyaṃ tu proktaṃ vai pañcaviṃśatiḥ  RKV 
navamaṃ bhagavannāma bhāgadvayavibhūṣitam 
tadaṣṭādaśasāhasraṃ procyate granthasaṃkhyayā  RKV 
daśamaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ tāvatsaṃkhyam ihocyate 
laiṅgamekādaśaṃ jñeyaṃ tathaikādaśasaṃkhyayā  RKV 
bhāgadvayaṃ viracitaṃ talliṅgamṛṣipuṃgava 
caturviṃśatisāhasraṃ vārāhaṃ dvādaśaṃ viduḥ  RKV 
vibhaktaṃ saptabhiḥ khaṇḍaiḥ skāndaṃ bhāgyavatāṃ vara 
tadekāśītisāhasraṃ saṃkhyayā vai nirūpitam  RKV 
tatastu vāmanaṃ nāma caturdaśatamaṃ smṛtam 
saṃkhyayā daśasāhasraṃ proktaṃ kulapate purā  RKV 
kaurmaṃ pañcadaśaṃ prāhur bhāgadvayavibhūṣitam 
daśasaptasahasrāṇi purā sāṃkhyapate kalau  RKV 
mātsyaṃ matsyena yatproktaṃ manave ṣoḍaśaṃ kramāt 
taccaturdaśasāhasraṃ saṃkhyayā vadatāṃ vara  RKV 
gāruḍaṃ saptadaśamaṃ smṛtaṃ caikonaviṃśatiḥ 
aṣṭādaśaṃ tu brahmāṇḍaṃ bhāgadvayavibhūṣitam  RKV 
tacca dvādaśasāhasraṃ śatamaṣṭasamanvitam 
tathaivopapurāṇāni yāni coktāni vedhasā  RKV 
idaṃ brahmapurāṇasya sulabhaṃ sauramuttamam 
saṃhitādvayasaṃyuktaṃ puṇyaṃ śivakathāśrayam  RKV 
ādyā sanatkumāroktā dvitīyā sūryabhāṣitā 
sanatkumāranāmnā hi tadvikhyātaṃ mahāmune  RKV 
dvitīyaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ ca purāṇe pādmasaṃjñite 
śaukeyaṃ hi tṛtīyaṃ tu purāṇe vaiṣṇave matam  RKV 
bārhaspatyaṃ caturthaṃ ca vāyavyaṃ saṃmataṃ sadā 
daurvāsasaṃ pañcamaṃ ca smṛtaṃ bhāgavate sadā  RKV 
bhaviṣye nāradoktaṃ ca sūribhiḥ kathitaṃ purā 
kāpilaṃ mānavaṃ caiva tathaivośanaseritam  RKV 
brahmāṇḍaṃ vāruṇaṃ cātha kālikādvayameva ca 
māheśvaraṃ tathā sāmbaṃ sauraṃ sarvārthasaṃcayam  RKV 
pārāśaraṃ bhāgavataṃ kaurmaṃ cāṣṭādaśaṃ kramāt 
etānyupapurāṇāni mayoktāni yathākramam  RKV 
purāṇasaṃhitāmetāṃ yaḥ paṭhedvā śṛṇoti ca 
so 'nantapuṇyabhāgī syānmṛto brahmapuraṃ vrajet  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe purāṇasaṃhitāvarṇanām prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
sūta uvāca  RKV 
narmadāyāstu māhātmyaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano 'bravīt 
tatte 'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi yattvayā paripṛcchitam  RKV 
vistaraṃ narmadāyāstu tīrthānāṃ munisattama 
ko 'nyaḥ śakto 'sti vai vaktumṛte brahmāṇamīśvaram  RKV 
etameva purā praśnaṃ pṛṣṭavāñjanamejayaḥ 
vaiśaṃpāyanasaṃjñaṃ tu śiṣyaṃ dvaipāyanasya ha  RKV 
revātīrthāśritaṃ puṇyaṃ tatte vakṣyāmi śaunaka 
purā pārīkṣito rājā yajñādīkṣāsu dīkṣitaḥ  RKV 
saṃbhṛte tu havirdravye vartamāneṣu karmasu 
āsīneṣu dvijāgryeṣu hūyamāne hutāśane  RKV 
vartamānāsu sarvatra tathā dharmakathāsu ca 
śrūyamāṇe tathā śabde janairukte tvaharniśam  RKV 
yajñabhūmau kulapate dīyatāṃ bhujyatām iti 
vividhāṃśca vinodānvai kurvāṇeṣu vinodiṣu  RKV 
evaṃvidhe vartamāne yajñe svargasadaḥsame 
vaiśaṃpāyanam āsīnaṃ papraccha janamejayaḥ  RKV 
janamejaya uvāca
dvaipāyanaprasādena jñānavānasi me mataḥ 
vaiśaṃpāyana tasmāt tvāṃ pṛcchāmi ṛṣisannidhau  RKV 
brūhi me tvaṃ purāvṛttaṃ pitḥṇāṃ tīrthasevanam 
ciraṃ nānāvidhānkleśān prāptāsta iti me śrutam  RKV 
kathaṃ dyūtajitāḥ pārthā mama pūrvapitāmahāḥ 
āsamudrāṃ mahīṃ vipra bhramantastīrthalobhataḥ  RKV 
kena te sahitāstāta bhūmibhāgān anekaśaḥ 
ceruḥ kathaya tatsarvaṃ sarvajño 'si mato mama  RKV 
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca  RKV 
kathayiṣyāmi bhūnātha yatpṛṣṭaṃ tu tvayā 'nagha 
namaskṛtya virūpākṣaṃ vedavyāsaṃ mahākavim  RKV 
pitāmahāstu te pañca pāṇḍavāḥ saha kṛṣṇayā 
uṣitvā brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ kāmyake vana uttame  RKV 
pradhānoddālake tatra kaśyapo 'tha mahāmatiḥ 
vibhāṇḍakaśca rājendra muruścaiva mahāmuniḥ  RKV 
pulastyo lomaśaścaiva tathānye putrapautriṇaḥ 
snātvā niḥśeṣatīrtheṣu gatāste vindhyaparvatam  RKV 
te ca tatrāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvairvṛkṣaiḥ samākulam 
campakaiḥ karṇakāraiśca punnāgairnāgakesaraiḥ  RKV 
bakulaiḥ kovidāraiśca dāḍimairupaśobhitam 
puṣpitairarjunaiścaiva bilvapāṭalaketakaiḥ  RKV 
kadambāmramadhūkaiśca nimbajambīratindukaiḥ 
nālikeraiḥ kapitthaiśca kharjūrapanasaistathā  RKV 
nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāvallībhirāvṛtam 
sapuṣpaṃ phalitaṃ kāntaṃ vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ yathā  RKV 
jalāśrayaistu vipulaiḥ padminīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitam 
sitotpalaiśca saṃchannaṃ nīlapītaiḥ sitāruṇaiḥ  RKV 
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇaṃ cakravākopaśobhitam 
āḍīkākabalākābhiḥ sevitaṃ kokilādibhiḥ  RKV 
siṃhairvyāghrairvarāhaiśca gajaiścaiva mahotkaṭaiḥ 
mahiṣaiśca mahākāyaiḥ kuraṅgaiś citrakaiḥ śaśaiḥ  RKV 
gaṇḍakaiścaiva khaḍgaiśca gomāyusurabhī yutam 
sāraṅgair mallakaiścaiva dvipadaiśca catuṣpadaiḥ  RKV 
tathāca kokilākīrṇaṃ manaḥkāntaṃ suśobhitam 
jīvaṃjīvakasaṃghaiśca nānāpakṣisamāyutam  RKV 
duḥkhaśokavinirmuktaṃ sattvotkaṭamanoramam 
kṣuttṛṣārahitaṃ kāntaṃ sarvavyādhivivarjitam  RKV 
siṃhīstanaṃ pibantyatra kuraṃgāḥ snehasaṃyutam 
mārjāramūṣakau cobhāvavalehata unmukhau  RKV 
pañcāsyāḥ potakebhāśca bhoginastu kalāpinaḥ 
dṛṣṭvā tadvipinaṃ ramyaṃ praviṣṭāḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ  RKV 
mārkaṇḍaṃ dṛṣṭavāṃstatra taruṇādityasannibham 
ṛṣibhiḥ sevyamānaṃ tu nānāśāstraviśāradaiḥ  RKV 
kulīnaiḥ sattvasampannaiḥ śaucācārasamanvitaiḥ 
dhīsaṃgataiḥ kṣamāyuktaistrisaṃdhyaṃ japatatparaiḥ  RKV 
ṛgyajuḥsāmavihitair mantrair homaparāyaṇaiḥ 
kecitpañcāgnimadhyasthāḥ kecidekāntasaṃsthitāḥ  RKV 
ūrdhvabāhunirālambā ādityabhramaṇāḥ pare 
sāyaṃprātarbhujaścānye ekāhārāstathā pare  RKV 
dvādaśāhāttathā cānye anye māsārdhabhojanāḥ 
darśe darśe tathā cānye anye śaivālabhojanāḥ  RKV 
piṇyākamapare 'bhujan kecit pālāśabhojanāḥ 
apare niyatāhārā vāyubhakṣyāmbubhojanāḥ  RKV 
evaṃbhūtais tathā vṛddhaiḥ sevyate munipuṃgavaiḥ 
tato dharmasutaḥ śrīmān āśramaṃ taṃ praviśya saḥ  RKV 
dṛṣṭvā munivaraṃ śāntaṃ dhyāyamānaṃ paraṃ padam 
prādakṣiṇyena sahasā daṇḍavatpatito 'grataḥ  RKV 
bhaktyānupatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā cirādādāya locanam 
ko bhavānityuvācedaṃ dharmaṃ dhīmānapṛcchata  RKV 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā dārakastatsamīpagaḥ 
āhāyaṃ dharmarājaste darśanārthaṃ samāgataḥ  RKV 
tacchrutvādārakeṇoktaṃ vacanaṃ prāha sādaraḥ 
ehyehi vatsavatseti kiṃcit sthānāccalanmuniḥ 
taṃ tu snehādupāghrāya āsane upaveśayat  RKV 
upaviṣṭe sabhāyāṃ tu pūjāṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi 
vanyairdhānyaiḥ phalair mūlai rasaiścaiva pṛthagvidhaiḥ  RKV 
pāṇḍavā brāhmaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ yathāyogyaṃ prapūjitāḥ 
muhūrtādatha viśramya dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ  RKV 
pṛcchati sma muniśreṣṭhaṃ kautūhalasamanvitaḥ 
bhagavansarvalokānāṃ dīrghāyustvaṃ mato mama  RKV 
saptakalpānaśeṣeṇa kathayasva mamānagha 
kalpakṣaye 'pi lokasya sthāvarasyetarasya ca  RKV 
na vinaṣṭo 'si viprendra kathaṃ vā kena hetunā 
gaṅgādyāḥ saritaḥ sarvāḥ samudrāntāśca yā mune  RKV 
tāsāṃ madhye sthitāḥ kāḥ svitkāścaiva pralayaṃ gatāḥ 
kā nu puṇyajalā nityaṃ kānu na kṣayamāgatā  RKV 
etat kathaya me tāta prasannenāntarātmanā 
śrotumicchāmyaśeṣeṇa ṛṣibhiḥ saha bāndhavaiḥ  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhusādhu mahāprājña dharmaputra yudhiṣṭhira 
kathayāmi yathā nyāyaṃ yatpṛcchasi mamānagha  RKV 
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ rudrabhāṣitam 
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  RKV 
aśvamedha sahasreṇa vājapeyaśatena ca 
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti rājannāstyatra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
brahmaghnaśca surāpī ca steyī goghnaśca yo naraḥ 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo rudrasya vacanaṃ yathā  RKV 
gaṅgā tu saritāṃ śreṣṭhā tathā caiva sarasvatī 
kāverī devikā caiva sindhuḥ sālakuṭī tathā  RKV 
sarayūḥ śatarudrā ca mahī carmilayā saha 
godāvarī tathā puṇyā tathaiva yamunā nadī  RKV 
payoṣṇī ca śatadruśca tathā dharmanadī śubhā 
etāścānyāśca saritaḥ sarvapāpaharāḥ smṛtāḥ  RKV 
kiṃ tu te kāraṇaṃ tāta vakṣyāmi nṛpasattama 
samudrāḥ saritaḥ sarvāḥ kalpe kalpe kṣayaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
saptakalpakṣaye kṣīṇe na mṛtā tena narmadā 
narmadaikaiva rājendra paraṃ tiṣṭhet saridvarā  RKV 
toyapūrṇā mahābhāga munisaṃghairabhiṣṭutā 
gaṃgādyāḥ saritaścānyāḥ kalpe kalpe kṣayaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
eṣā devī purā dṛṣṭā tena vakṣyāmi te 'nagha  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe revāmāhātmyavarṇanaṃnāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
saptakalpakṣayā ghorāstvayā dṛṣṭā mahāmune 
na cāpīhāsti bhagavandīrghāyuriha kaścana  RKV 
tvayā hyekārṇave suptaḥ padmanābhaḥ surārihā 
dṛṣṭaḥ sahasracaraṇaḥ sahasranayanodaraḥ  RKV 
tvaṃ kilānugrahāt tasya dahyamāne carācare 
na kṣayaṃ samanuprāpto varadānānmahātmanaḥ  RKV 
kiṃ tvayāścaryabhūtaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ ca bhramatānagha 
etadācakṣva bhagavanparaṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me  RKV 
samprāpte ca mahāghore yugasyānte mahākṣaye 
anāvṛṣṭihate loke purā varṣaśatādhike  RKV 
auṣadhīnāṃ kṣaye ghore devadānavavarjite 
nirvīrye nirvaṣaṭkāre kalinā dūṣite bhṛśam  RKV 
saritsarastaḍāgeṣu palvalopavaneṣu ca 
saṃśuṣkeṣu tadā brahmannirākāre yugakṣaye  RKV 
janaṃ prāpte maharloke brahmakṣatraviśādayaḥ 
ṛṣayaśca mahātmāno divyatejaḥsamanvitāḥ  RKV 
sthitāni kāni bhūtāni gatānyeva mahāmune 
etatsarvaṃ mahābhāga kathayasva pṛthakpṛthak  RKV 
bhūtāni kāni viprendra kathaṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt 
brahmaviṣṇvindrarudrāṇāṃ kāle prāpte sudāruṇe  RKV 
evamuktas tataḥ so 'tha dharmarājena dhīmatā 
mārkaṇḍaḥ pratyuvācedamṛṣisaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇvantu ṛṣayaḥ sarve tvayā saha nareśvara 
mahatpurāṇaṃ pūrvoktaṃ śaṃbhunā vāyudaivate  RKV 
vāyoḥ sakāśātskandena śrutametatpurātanam 
vasiṣṭhaḥ śrutavāṃstasmāt parāśarastataḥ param  RKV 
tasmācca jātūkarṇyena tasmāccaiva maharṣibhiḥ 
evaṃ paramparāproktaṃ śatasaṃkhyair dvijottamaiḥ  RKV 
saṃhitā śatasāhasrī puroktā śaṃbhunā kila 
āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vadārthaṃ tattvataḥ purā  RKV 
yugarūpeṇa sā paścāc caturdhā viniyojitā 
madaprajñānusāreṇa narāṇāṃ tu maharṣibhiḥ  RKV 
ārādhya paśubhartāraṃ mayā pūrvaṃ maheśvaram 
purāṇaṃ śrutametaddhi tatte vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ  RKV 
yacchrutvā mucyate jantuḥ sarvapāpairnareśvara 
mānasaiḥ karmajaiścaiva saptajanmasu saṃcitaiḥ  RKV 
saptakalpakṣayā ghorā mayā dṛṣṭāḥ punaḥpunaḥ 
prasādāddevadevasya viṣṇośca parameṣṭhinaḥ  RKV 
dvādaśādityanirdagdhe jagatyekārṇavīkṛte 
śrānto 'haṃ vibhramaṃs tatra taranbāhubhir arṇavam  RKV 
athāhaṃ salile rājannādityasamarūpiṇam 
purā puruṣamadrākṣamanādinidhanaṃ prabhum  RKV 
śṛṅgaṃ caivādrirājasya bhāsayantaṃ diśo daśa 
dvitīyo 'nyo manurdṛṣṭaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ  RKV 
agādhe bhramate so 'pi tamobhūte mahārṇave 
aviśramanmuhūrtaṃ tu cakrārūḍha iva bhraman  RKV 
athāhaṃ bhayādudvignastaranbāhubhir arṇavam 
tatrastho'haṃ mahāmatsyam apaśyaṃ madasaṃyutam  RKV 
tato 'bravītsa māṃ dṛṣṭvā ehyehīti ca bhārata 
paraṃ pradhānaḥ sarveṣāṃ matsyarūpo maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
tato 'haṃ tvarayā gatvā tanmukhe manujeśvara 
suśrānto vigatajñānaḥ paraṃ nirvedamāgataḥ  RKV 
tato 'drākṣaṃ samudrānte mahadāvartasaṃkulām 
udyattaraṃgasalilāṃ phenapuñjāṭṭahāsinīm  RKV 
nadīṃ kāmagamāṃ puṇyāṃ jhaṣamīnasamākulām 
nadyāstasyāstu madhyasthā pramadā kāmarūpiṇī  RKV 
nīlotpaladalaśyāmā mahatprakṣobhavāhinī 
divyahāṭakacitrāṅgī kanakojjvalaśobhitā  RKV 
dvābhyāṃ saṃgṛhya jānubhyāṃ mahatpotaṃ vyavasthitā 
tāṃ manuḥ pratyuvācedaṃ kā tvaṃ divyavarāṅgane  RKV 
tiṣṭhase kena kāryeṇa tvamatra surasundari 
surāsuragaṇe naṣṭe bhramase līlayārṇave  RKV 
saritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailāḥ kṣayaṃ prāptā hyanekaśaḥ 
tvamekā tu kathaṃ sādhvi tiṣṭhase kāraṇaṃ mahat 
śrotumicchāmyahaṃ devi kathayasva hyaśeṣataḥ  RKV 
abalovāca
īśvarāṅgasamudbhūtā hyamṛtānāma viśrutā 
saritpāpaharā puṇyā māmāśritya bhayaṃ kutaḥ  RKV 
sāhaṃ potamimaṃ tubhyaṃ gṛhītvā hyāgatā dvija 
na hyasya potasya kṣayo yatra tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ  RKV 
tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vismayotphullalocanaḥ 
manunā saha rājendra potārūḍho hyahaṃ tadā  RKV 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇamya śirasā vibhum 
vyāpinaṃ parameśānamastauṣamabhayapradam  RKV 
sadyojātāya devāya vāmadevāya vai namaḥ 
bhave bhave namastubhyaṃ bhaktigamyāya te namaḥ  RKV 
bhūrbhuvāya namastubhyaṃ rāmajyeṣṭhāya vai namaḥ 
namaste bhadrakālāya kalirūpāya vai namaḥ  RKV 
acintyāvyaktarūpāya mahādevāya dhāmane 
vidmahe devadevāya tanno rudra namonamaḥ  RKV 
jagatsṛṣṭivināśānāṃ kāraṇāya namonamaḥ 
evaṃ stuto mahādevaḥ pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭayā mayānagha  RKV 
prasanno māvadat paścādvaraṃ varaya suvrata  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe
narmadāmāhātmye mārkaṇḍeyadharmarājasaṃvāde kalpakṣaye mārkaṇḍeyakṛtapotārdhārohaṇavṛttāntavarṇanaṃnāma tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato 'rṇavātsamuttīrya trikūṭaśikhare sthitam 
mahākanakavarṇābhe nānāvarṇaśilācite  RKV 
mahāśṛṅge samāsīnaṃ rudrakoṭisamanvitam 
mahādevaṃ mahātmānamīśānamajam avyayam  RKV 
sarvabhūtamayaṃ tāta manunā saha suvrata 
bhūyo vavande caraṇau sarvadevanamaskṛtau  RKV 
tatkāle yugasāhasraṃ saha rudreṇa mānada 
tasminnekārṇave ghore sthito 'haṃ kurunaṃdana  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
etacchrutvā tu me tāta paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hṛdi 
jātaṃ tatkathayasveti śṛṇvataḥ saha bāndhavaiḥ  RKV 
kā sā padmapalāśākṣī tamobhūte mahārṇave 
yogivadbhramate nityaṃ rudrajāṃ svāṃ ca yābravīt  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
etameva mayā praśnaṃ purā pṛṣṭo manuḥ svayam 
tadeva te 'dya vakṣyāmi abalāyāḥ samudbhavam  RKV 
vyatītāyāṃ niśāyāṃ tu brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
tataḥ prabhāte vimale sṛjyamāneṣu jantuṣu  RKV 
manuṃ praṇamya śirasā pṛcchāmyetad yudhiṣṭhira 
keyaṃ padmapalāśākṣī śyāmā caṃdranibhānanā  RKV 
ekārṇave bhramatyekā rudrajāsmīti vādinī 
sāvitrī vedamātā ca hyathavā sā sarasvatī  RKV 
mandākinī saricchreṣṭhā lakṣmīrvā kimatho umā 
kālarātrirbhavetsākṣāt prakṛtirvā sukhocitā  RKV 
etadācakṣva bhagavankā sā hyamṛtasaṃbhavā 
caratyekārṇave ghore pranaṣṭoragarākṣase  RKV 
manuruvāca
śṛṇu vatsa yathānyāyamasyā vakṣyāmi saṃbhavam 
yayā rudrasamudbhūtā yā ceyaṃ varavarṇinī  RKV 
purā śivaḥ śāntatanuścacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ 
hitārthaṃ sarvalokānāmumayā saha śaṃkaraḥ  RKV 
ṛkṣaśailaṃ samāruhya tapastepe sudāruṇam 
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvabhūtātmako vaśī  RKV 
tapatastasya devasya svedaḥ samabhavatkila 
taṃ giriṃ plāvayāmāsa sa svedo rudrasaṃbhavaḥ  RKV 
tasmād āsīt samudbhūtā mahāpuṇyā saridvarā 
yā sā tvayārṇave dṛṣṭā padmapatrāyatekṣaṇā  RKV 
strīrūpaṃ samavasthāya rudramārādhayatpurā 
ādye kṛtayuge tasminsamānāmayutaṃ nṛpa  RKV 
tatastuṣṭo mahādeva umayā saha śaṃkaraḥ 
brūhi tvaṃ tu mahābhāge yatte manasi vartate  RKV 
sariduvāca
pralaye samanuprāpte naṣṭe sthāvarajaṃgame 
prasādāttava deveśa akṣayāhaṃ bhave prabho  RKV 
saritsu sāgareṣveva parvateṣu kṣayiṣvapi 
tava prasādāddeveśa puṇyā kṣayyā bhave prabho  RKV 
pāpopapātakairyuktā mahāpātakino 'pi ye 
mucyante sarvapāpebhyo bhaktyā snātvā tu śaṃkara  RKV 
uttare jāhnavīdeśe mahāpātakanāśinī 
bhavāmi dakṣiṇe mārge yadyevaṃ surapūjitā  RKV 
svargādāgamya gaṃgeti yathā khyātā kṣitau vibho 
tathā dakṣiṇagaṅgeti bhaveyaṃ tridaśeśvara  RKV 
pṛthivyāṃ sarvatīrtheṣu snātvā yallabhate phalam 
tatphalaṃ labhate martyo bhaktyā snātvā maheśvara  RKV 
brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpam yadāste saṃcitaṃ kvacit 
māsamātreṇa taddeva kṣayaṃ yātvavagāhanāt  RKV 
yatphalaṃ sarvavedeṣu sarvayajñeṣu śaṃkara 
avagāhena tatsarvaṃ bhavatviti matirmama  RKV 
sarvadānopavāseṣu sarvatīrthāvagāhane 
tatphalaṃ mama toyena jāyatāmiti śaṃkara  RKV 
mama tīre narā ye tu arcayanti maheśvaram 
te gatāstava lokaṃ syur etad eva bhavecchiva  RKV 
mama kūle maheśāna umayā saha daivataiḥ 
vasa nityaṃ jagannātha eṣa eva varo mama  RKV 
sukarmā vā vikarmā vā śānto dānto jitendriyaḥ 
mṛto janturmama jale gacchatād amarāvatīm  RKV 
triṣu lokeṣu vikhyātā mahāpātakanāśinī 
bhavāmi devadeveśa prasanno yadi manyase  RKV 
etāṃścānyānvarāndivyānprārthito nṛpasattama 
narmadayā tataḥ prāha prasanno vṛṣavāhanaḥ  RKV 
śrīmaheśa uvāca
evaṃ bhavatu kalyāṇi yattvayoktamanindite 
nānyā varārhā lokeṣu muktvā tvāṃ kamalekṣaṇe  RKV 
yadaiva mama dehāt tvaṃ samudbhūtā varānane 
tadaiva sarvapāpānāṃ mocinī tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
kalpakṣayakare kāle kāle ghore viśeṣataḥ 
uttaraṃ kūlamāśritya nivasanti ca ye narāḥ  RKV 
api kīṭapataṅgāśca vṛkṣagulmalatādayaḥ 
ā dehapatanāddevi te 'pi yāsyanti sadgatim  RKV 
dakṣiṇaṃ kūlamāśritya ye dvijā dharmavatsalāḥ 
ā mṛtyor nivasiṣyanti te gatāḥ pitṛmandire  RKV 
ahaṃ hi tava vākyena kasmiṃścit kāraṇāntare 
tvattīre nivasiṣyāmi sadaiva hyumayā samam  RKV 
evaṃ devi mahādevi evameva na saṃśayaḥ 
brahmendracandravaruṇaiḥ sādhyaiśca saha viṣṇunā  RKV 
uttare devi te kūle vasiṣyanti mamājñayā 
dakṣiṇe pitṛbhiḥ sārddhaṃ tathānye surasundari  RKV 
vasiṣyanti mayā sārddhameṣa te vara uttamaḥ 
gaccha gaccha mahābhāge martyānpāpādvimocaya  RKV 
sahitā ṛṣisaṃghaiśca tathā siddhasurāsuraiḥ 
evamuktā mahādeva umayā sahito vibhuḥ  RKV 
vandyamāno 'tha manunā mayā cādarśanaṃ gataḥ 
tena caiṣā mahāpuṇyā mahāpātakanāśinī  RKV 
kathitā pṛcchyate yā te mā te bhavatu vismayaḥ 
eṣā gaṃgā mahāpuṇyā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā  RKV 
daśābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ srotaiḥ plāvayantī diśo daśa 
śoṇo mahānadaścaiva narmadā surasā kṛtā  RKV 
mandākinī daśārṇā ca citrakūṭā tathaiva ca 
tamasā vidiśā caiva karabhā yamunā tathā  RKV 
citrotpalā vipāśā ca rañjanā vāluvāhinī 
ṛkṣapādaprasūtāstāḥ sarvā vai rudrasaṃbhavāḥ  RKV 
sarvapāpaharāḥ puṇyāḥ sarvamaṃgaladāḥ śivāḥ 
ityetairnāmabhirdivyaiḥ stūyate vedapāragaiḥ  RKV 
purāṇajñair mahābhāgairājyapaiḥ somapaistathā 
ityetatsarvamākhyātaṃ mahābhāgyaṃ narottama  RKV 
manunoktaṃ purā mahyam amṛtāyāḥ samudbhavam 
puṇyaṃ pavitramatulaṃ rudrodgītamidaṃ śubham  RKV 
ye narāḥ kīrtayiṣyanti bhaktyā śṛṇvanti ye 'pi ca 
prātarutthāya nāmāni daśa pañca ca bhārata  RKV 
te narāḥ sakalaṃ puṇyaṃ labhiṣyantyavagāhajam 
vimānenārkavarṇena ghaṇṭāśataninādinā  RKV 
tyaktvā mānuṣyakaṃ bhāvaṃ yāsyanti paramāṃ gatim  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāpañcadaśanāmavarṇanaṃ nāma caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
āścaryametadakhilaṃ kathitaṃ bho dvijottama 
vismayaṃ paramāpannā ṛṣisaṃghā mayā saha  RKV 
aho bhagavatī puṇyā narmadeyamayonijā 
rudradehādviniṣkrāntā mahāpāpakṣayaṃkarī  RKV 
saptakalpakṣaye prāpte tvayeyaṃ saha suvrata 
na mṛtā ca mahābhāgā kimataḥ puṇyamuttamam  RKV 
ke te kalpāḥ samuddiṣṭāḥ sapta kalpakṣayaṃkarāḥ 
na mṛtā cediyaṃ devī tvaṃ caiva ṛṣipuṃgava  RKV 
apakṣigaṇasaṃghāte jagatyekārṇavīkṛte 
kīdṛgrūpaḥ samabhavanmahādevo yugakṣaye  RKV 
kathaṃ saṃharate viśvaṃ kathaṃ cāste mahārṇave 
kathaṃ ca sṛjate viśvaṃ kathaṃ dhārayate prajāḥ  RKV 
kīdṛgrūpā bhaveddevī sarid ekārṇavīkṛte 
kimarthaṃ narmadā proktā revatī ca kathaṃ smṛtā  RKV 
añjaneti kimarthaṃ vā kimarthaṃ suraseti ca 
mandākinī kimarthaṃ ca śoṇaśceti kathaṃ bhavet  RKV 
trikūṭeti kimarthaṃ vā kimarthaṃ vāluvāhinī 
koṭikoṭyo hi tīrthānāṃ praviṣṭā yā mahārṇavam  RKV 
kiyatyaḥ saritāṃ koṭyo narmadāṃ samupāsate 
yajñopavītairṛṣibhir devatābhis tathaiva ca  RKV 
vibhakteyaṃ kimarthaṃ ca śrūyate munisattama 
vaiṣṇavīti purāṇajñaiḥ kimarthamiha cocyate  RKV 
keṣu sthāneṣu tīrtheṣu pūjanīyā saridvarā 
tīrthāni ca pṛthagbrūhi yatra saṃnihito haraḥ  RKV 
yatpramāṇā ca sā devī yā rudreṇa vinirmitā 
kīdṛśāni ca karmāṇi rudreṇa kathitāni te  RKV 
kathaṃ mlecchasamākīrṇo deśo 'yaṃ dvijasattama 
etadācakṣva māṃ brahmanmārkaṇḍeya mahāmate  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇvantu ṛṣayaḥ sarve tvaṃ ca tāta yudhiṣṭhira 
purāṇaṃ narmadāyāṃ tu kathitaṃ ca triśūlinā  RKV 
vāyoḥ sakāśācca mayā tenāpi ca maheśvarāt 
aśakyatvānmanuṣyāṇāṃ saṃkṣiptam ṛṣibhiḥ purā  RKV 
māyūraṃ prathamaṃ tāta kaurmyam ca tadanantaram 
puram tathā kauśikaṃ ca mātsyaṃ dviradam eva ca  RKV 
vārāhaṃ yanmayā dṛṣṭaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ param 
nyagrodhākhyam ataḥ cāsīd ākāṅkṣaṃ punaruttamam  RKV 
padmaṃ ca tāmasaṃ caiva saṃvartodvartameva ca 
mahāpralayamityāhuḥ purāṇe vedacintakāḥ  RKV 
etatsaṃkṣepataḥ sarvaṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ tairmahātmabhiḥ 
vibhaktaṃ ca caturbhāgair brahmādyaiśca maharṣibhiḥ  RKV 
tadahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi purāṇārthaviśārada 
sapta kalpā mahāghorā yair iyaṃ na mṛtā sarit  RKV 
ā jaṅgamaṃ tamobhūtam aprajñātamalakṣaṇam 
naṣṭacandrārkakiraṇam āsīd bhūtavivarjitam  RKV 
tamaso 'to mahānāmnā puruṣaḥ sa jagadguruḥ 
cacāra tasminnekākī vyaktāvyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ  RKV 
sa cauṃkāramayo 'tīto gāyatrīmasṛjaddvijaḥ 
sa tayā sārddham īśānaścikrīḍa puruṣo virāṭ  RKV 
svadehādasṛjad viśvaṃ pañcabhūtātmasaṃjñitam 
krīḍansamasṛjadviśvaṃ pañcabhūtātmasaṃjñitam  RKV 
krīḍan sṛjad virāṭsaṃjñaḥ sabījaṃ ca hiraṇmayam 
taccāṇḍam abhavad divyaṃ dvādaśādityasannibham  RKV 
tadbhittvā puruṣo jajñe caturvaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ 
so 'sṛjadviśvam evaṃ tu sadevāsuramānuṣam  RKV 
satiryakpaśupakṣīkaṃ svedāṇḍajajarāyujam 
etadaṇḍaṃ purāṇeṣu prathamaṃ parikīrtitam  RKV 
pūrvakalpe nṛpaśreṣṭha krīḍantyā parameṣṭhinā 
umayā saha rudrasya krīḍataścārṇavīkṛtaḥ  RKV 
harṣājjajñe śubhā kanyā umāyāḥ svedasaṃbhavā 
śarvasyoraḥsthalājjajñe umā kucavimardanāt  RKV 
svedādvijajñe mahatī kanyā rājīvalocanā 
dvitīyaḥ saṃbhavo yasyā rudradehād yudhiṣṭhira  RKV 
sā paribhramate lokān sadevāsuramānavān 
trailokyonmādajananī rūpeṇa 'pratimā tadā  RKV 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā devadaityendrā mohitā labhate katham 
mṛgayanti sma tāṃ kanyām itaścetaśca bhārata  RKV 
hāvabhāvavilāsaiśca mohayatyakhilaṃ jagat 
bhramate divyarūpā sā vidyutsaudāminī yathā  RKV 
meghamadhye sthitā bhābhiḥ sarvayoṣidanuttamā 
tato rudraṃ surāḥ sarve daityāśca saha dānavaiḥ  RKV 
varayanti sma tāṃ kanyāṃ kāmenākulitā bhṛśam 
tato 'bravīnmahādevo devadānavayordvayoḥ  RKV 
balena tejasā caiva hyadhiko yo bhaviṣyati 
sa imāṃ prāpsyate kanyāṃ nānyathā vai surottamāḥ  RKV 
tato devāsurāḥ sarve kanyāṃ vai samupāgaman 
ahamenāṃ grahīṣyāmi ahamenāmiti bruvan  RKV 
paśyatāmeva sarveṣāṃ sā kanyāntaradhīyata 
punastāṃ dadṛśuḥ sarve yojanāntaradhiṣṭhitām  RKV 
jagmuste tvaritāḥ sarve yatra sā samadṛśyata 
tribhiścaturbhiśca tathā yojanairdaśabhiḥ punaḥ  RKV 
dhiṣṭhitāṃ samapaśyaṃste sarve mātaṃgagāminīm 
yojanānāṃ śatairbhūyaḥ sahasraiścāpyadhiṣṭhitām  RKV 
tathā śatasahasreṇa laghutvāt samadṛśyata 
agrataḥ pṛṣṭhataścaiva diśāsu vidiśāsu ca  RKV 
tāṃ paśyanti varārohām ekadhā bahudhā punaḥ 
divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu bhrāmitāste tayā purā  RKV 
na cāvāptā tu sā kanyā mahādevāṅgasaṃbhavā 
sahomayā tato devo jahāsoccaiḥ punaḥpunaḥ  RKV 
gaṇāstālakasaṃpātair nṛtyanti ca mudānvitāḥ 
akasmāddṛśyate kanyā śaṃkarasya samīpagā  RKV 
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayāpannā devā yānti parāṅmukhāḥ 
tasyāś cakre tato nāma svayameva pinākadhṛk  RKV 
narma caibhyo dade yasmāt tatkṛtaiś ceṣṭitaiḥ pṛthak 
bhaviṣyasi varārohe saricchreṣṭhā tu narmadā  RKV 
svarūpamāsthito devaḥ prāpa hāsyaṃ yato bhuvi 
narmadā tena cokteyaṃ suśītalajalā śivā  RKV 
saptakalpakṣaye jāte yaduktaṃ śaṃbhunā purā 
na mṛtā tena rājendra narmadā khyātimāgatā  RKV 
tatastāmadadātkanyāṃ śīlavatīṃ suśobhanām 
mahārṇavāya deveśaḥ sarvabhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ  RKV 
tataḥ sā ṛkṣaśailendrāt phenapuñjāṭṭahāsinī 
viveśa narmadā devī samudraṃ saritāṃ patim  RKV 
evaṃ brāhme purā kalpe samudbhūteyamīśvarāt 
mātsye kalpe mayā dṛṣṭā samākhyātā mayā śṛṇu  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
punaryugānte samprāpte tṛtīye nṛpasattama 
dādaśārkavapurbhūtvā bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ  RKV 
saptadvīpasamudrāntāṃ saśailavanakānanām 
nirdagdhāṃ tu mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ kālo bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
tato mahāghano bhūtvā plāvayāmāsa vāriṇā 
kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇavapus tvenāṃ vidyuccandrāyudhāṅkitām  RKV 
plāvayitvā jagatsarvaṃ tasminnekārṇavīkṛte 
suṣvāpa vimale toye jagatsaṃkṣipya māyayā  RKV 
tato 'haṃ bhramamāstu tamobhūte mahārṇave 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu vāyubhūte maheśvare  RKV 
oṃkṛtvā devadeveśaṃ yenedaṃ gahanīkṛtam 
dhyāyamānastato devaṃ rājendra vimale jale  RKV 
tasminmahārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame 
mayūraṃ svarṇapatrāḍhyam apaśyaṃsahasā jale 
vicitracandrakopetaṃ nīlakaṃṭhaṃ sulocanam  RKV 
tato mayūraḥ sa mahārṇavānte vikṣobhayitvā hi mahāsveṇa 
cacāra devastriśikhī śikhaṇḍī trailokyagoptā sa mahānubhāvaḥ  RKV 
śivaśca raudreṇa mayūrarūpiṇā vikṣobhyamāṇe salile 'pi tasmin 
saha bhramantīṃ ca mahārṇavānte sarinmahaughāṃ sumahāndadarśa  RKV 
sa tāṃ mahādevamayūrarūpo dṛṣṭvā bhramantīṃ sahasormijālaiḥ 
kā tvaṃ śubhe śāśvatadehabhūtā kṣayaṃ na yātāsi mahākṣayānte  RKV 
devāsuragaṇe naṣṭe saritsaramahārṇave 
kā tvaṃ bhramasi padmākṣi kva gatāsi ca na kṣayam  RKV 
narmadovāca
tava prasādāddeveśa mṛtyurmama na vidyate 
sṛja deva punarviśvaṃ śarvarī kṣayamāgatā  RKV 
evamukto mahādevo vyadhunotpakṣapañjaram 
tāvatpañjaramadhyānte tasya pakṣādviniḥsṛtāḥ  RKV 
tāvanto devadaityendrāḥ pakṣābhyāṃ tasya jajñire 
teṣāṃ madhye punaḥ sā tu narmadā bhramate sarit  RKV 
tataścānyo mahāśailo dṛśyate bharatarṣabha 
tribhiḥ kūṭaiḥ suvistīrṇaiḥ śṛṅgavāniva govṛṣaḥ  RKV 
trikūṭastu iti khyātaḥ sarvaratnairvibhūṣitaḥ 
tatastasmāttrikūṭācca plāvayantī mahīṃ yayau  RKV 
trikūṭī tena vikhyātā pitḥṇāṃ trāyaṇī parā 
dvitīyācca tato gaṅgā vistīrṇā dharaṇītale  RKV 
tṛtīyaṃ ca tataḥ śṛṅgaṃ saptadhā khaṇḍaśo gatam 
jambūdvīpe tu saṃjātāḥ sapta te kulaparvatāḥ  RKV 
candranakṣatrasahitā grahagrāmanadīnadāḥ 
aṇḍajaṃ svedajaṃ jātamudbhijjaṃ ca jarāyujam  RKV 
evaṃ jagadidaṃ sarvaṃ mayūrādabhavatpurā 
samastaṃ naraśārdūla mahādevasamudbhavam  RKV 
tato nadīḥ samudrāṃśca saṃvibhajya pṛthakpṛthak 
narmadāmāha deveśo gaccha tvaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśam  RKV 
evaṃ sā dakṣiṇā gaṃgā mahāpātakanāśinī 
uttare jāhnavī deśe puṇyā tvaṃ dakṣiṇe śubhā  RKV 
yathā gaṃgā mahāpuṇyā mama mastakasaṃbhavā 
tadviśiṣṭā mahābhāge tvaṃ caiveti na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
tvayā saha bhaviṣyāmi ekenāṃśena suvrate 
mahāpātakayuktānām auṣadhaṃ tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi  RKV 
evamuktā tu devena mahāpātakanāśinī 
dakṣiṇaṃ digvibhāgaṃ tu sā jagāmāśu vikramā  RKV 
ṛkṣaśailendramāsādya candramauler anugrahāt 
vāryaughaiḥ prasthitā yasmānmahādevapraṇoditā  RKV 
mahatā cāpi vegena yasmād eṣā samucchritā 
mahatī tena sā proktā mahādevānmahīpate  RKV 
tapatastasya devasya śūlāgrādbindavo 'patan 
tenaiṣā śoṇasaṃjñā tu daśa sapta ca tāḥ smṛtāḥ  RKV 
sarveṣāṃ narmadā puṇyā rudradehādviniḥsṛtā 
sarvābhyaśca saridbhyaś ca varadānānmahātmanaḥ  RKV 
śaṃkarānuprahād devī mahāpātakanāśinī 
yasmān mahārṇave ghore dṛśyate mahatī ca sā  RKV 
suvyaktāṅgī mahākāyā mahatī tena sā smṛtā 
tasmād vikṣobhyamāṇā hi diggajairambudopamaiḥ  RKV 
kaluṣatvaṃ nayatyeva rasena surasā tathā 
kṛpāṃ karoti sā yasmāllokānāmabhayapradā  RKV 
saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ tena caiṣā kṛpā smṛtā 
purā kṛtayuge puṇye divyamandārabhūṣitā  RKV 
kalpavṛkṣasamākīrṇā rohītakasamākulā 
vahatyeṣā ca mandena tena mandākinī smṛtā  RKV 
bhittvā mahārṇavaṃ kṣipraṃ yasmāllokamihāgatā 
pūjyā suraiśca siddhaiśca tasmādeṣā mahārṇavā  RKV 
vicitrotpalasaṃghātair ṛkṣadvipasamākulā  RKV 
bhittvā śailaṃ ca vipulaṃ prayātyevaṃ mahārṇavam 
bhrāmayantī diśaḥ sarvā raveṇa mahatā purā  RKV 
plāvayantī virājantī tena revā iti smṛtā 
bhāryāputrasuduḥkhāḍhyānnarāñchāpaiḥ samāvṛtān  RKV 
vipāpānkurute yasmādvipāpā tena sā smṛtā 
viṇmūtranicayāṃ ghorāṃ pāṃśuśoṇitakardamām  RKV 
pāśairnityaṃ tu sambādhāṃ yasmānmocayate bhṛśam 
vipāśeti ca sā proktā saṃsārārṇavatāriṇī  RKV 
narmadā vimalāmbhā ca vimalenduśubhānanā 
tamobhūte mahāghore yasmādeṣā mahāprabhā  RKV 
vimalā tena sā proktā vidvadbhirnṛpasattama 
karair indukaraprakhyaiḥ sūryaraśmisamaprabhā  RKV 
kṣarantī modate viśvaṃ karabhā tena cocyate 
yasmād rañjayate lokāndarśanādeva bhārata  RKV 
rañjanād rañjanā proktā dhātvarthe rājasattama 
tṛṇavīrudhagulmādyās tiryañcaḥ pakṣiṇastathā 
tānudbhūtānnayetsvargaṃ tenoktā vāyuvāhinī  RKV 
evaṃ yo vetti nāmāni nirgamaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
sa yāti pāpavirmukto rudralokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe
narmadāmāhātmye sahaitukarevānāmamāhātmyavarṇane mayūrakalpasamudbhavo nāma ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
punarekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṃgame 
salilenāplute loke nirāloke tamodbhave  RKV 
brahmaiko vicaraṃstatra tamībhūte mahārṇave 
divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu khadyota iva rūpavān  RKV 
śete yojanasāhasram aprameyam anuttamam 
dvādaśādityasaṃkāśaṃ sahasracaraṇekṣaṇam  RKV 
prasuptaṃ cārṇave ghore hyapaśyatkūrmarūpiṇam 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayāpanno brahmā bodhayate śanaiḥ  RKV 
stutibhirmaṃgalaiścaiva vedavedāṃgasaṃbhavaiḥ 
vācaspate vibudhyasva mahābhūta namo 'stu te  RKV 
tavodare jagatsarvaṃ tiṣṭhate parameśvara 
tadvimuñca mahāsattva yatpūrvaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ tvayā  RKV 
vyatītā rajanī brāhmī dinaṃ samanuvartate 
nirīkṣya sarvalokeśa yena saṃbhavate jagat  RKV 
sa niśamya vacastasya utthitaḥ parameśvaraḥ 
samudgiran sa lokāṃstrīn grastān kalpakṣaye tadā  RKV 
devadānavagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ 
sacandrārkagrahāḥ sarve śarīrāttasya nirgatāḥ  RKV 
tato hyekārṇavaṃ sarvaṃ vibhajya parameśvaraḥ 
vistīrṇopalatoyaughāṃ saritsaravivardhitām  RKV 
paśyate medinīṃ devaḥ savṛkṣauṣadhipalvalām 
himavantaṃ giriśreṣṭhaṃ śvetaṃ parvatamuttamam  RKV 
śṛṅgavantaṃ mahāśailaṃ ye cānye kulaparvatāḥ 
jaṃbudvīpaṃ kuśaṃ krauñcaṃ sagomedaṃ saśālmalam  RKV 
puṣkarāntāśca ye dvīpā ye ca saptamahārṇavāḥ 
lokālokaṃ mahāśailaṃ sarvaṃ ca purataḥ sthitam  RKV 
catuḥprakṛtisaṃyuktaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṃgamam 
yugānte tu viniṣkrāntam apaśyatsa maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
viprakīrṇaśilājālāmapaśyatsa vasuṃdharām 
kūrmapṛṣṭhopagāṃ devīṃ mahārṇavagatāṃ prabhuḥ  RKV 
tasmin viśīrṇaśailāgre saritsarovivarjite 
nānātaraṃgabhinnoda āvartodvartasaṃkule  RKV 
nānauṣadhiprajvalite nānotpalaśilātale 
nānāvihaṃgasaṃghuṣṭāṃ matsyakūrmasamākulām  RKV 
divyamāyāmayīṃ devīm utkṛṣṭāmbudasannibhām 
nadīmapaśyaddeveśo hyanaupamyajalāśayām  RKV 
madhye tasyāmbudaśyāmāṃ pīnorujaghanastanīm 
vastrairanupamairdivyairnānābharaṇabhūṣitām  RKV 
sanūpuraravoddāmāṃ hārakeyūramaṇḍitām 
tādṛśīṃ narmadāṃ devīṃ svayaṃ strīrūpadhāriṇīm  RKV 
yogamāyāmayaiścitrairbhūṣaṇaiḥ svairvibhūṣitām 
avyaktāṅgīṃ mahābhāgāmapaśyatsa tu narmadām  RKV 
ardhodyatabhujāṃ bālāṃ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇām 
stuvantīṃ devadeveśamutthitāṃ tu jalāttadā  RKV 
vismayāviṣṭahṛdayo hyahamudvīkṣya tāṃ śubhām 
snātvā jale śubhe tasyāḥ stotumabhyudyatastataḥ  RKV 
arcayāmāsa saṃhṛṣṭo mantrairvedāṃgasaṃbhavaiḥ 
sṛṣṭaṃ ca tatpurā rājanpaśyeyaṃ sacarācaram  RKV 
sadevāsuragandharvaṃ sapannagamahoragam 
paśyāmyeṣā mahābhāgā naiva yātā kṣayaṃ purā  RKV 
mahādevaprasādācca taccharīrasamudbhavā 
bhūyo bhūyo mayā dṛṣṭā kathitā te nṛpottama  RKV 
prādurbhāvamimaṃ kaurmyaṃ ye 'dhīyante dvijottamāḥ 
ye 'pi śṛṇvanti vidvāṃso mucyante te 'pi kilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye kūrmakalpasamudbhavo nāma saptamo

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
naṣṭe loke punaścānye salilena samāvṛte 
mahārṇavasya madhyastho bāhubhyāmataraṃ jalam  RKV 
divye varṣaśate pūrṇe śrānto 'haṃ nṛpasattama 
dhyātuṃ samārabhaṃ devaṃ mahadarṇavatāraṇam  RKV 
dhyāyamānastataḥ kāle apaśyaṃ pakṣiṇaṃ param 
hārakundendusaṃkāśaṃ bakaṃ gokṣīrapāṇḍuram  RKV 
tato 'haṃ vismayāviṣṭastaṃ bakaṃ samudīkṣya vai 
asmin mahārṇave ghore kuto 'yaṃ pakṣisaṃbhavaḥ  RKV 
taranbāhubhiraśrāntastaṃ bakaṃ pratyabhāṣiṣi 
pākṣarūpaṃ samāsthāya kastvamekārṇavīkṛte  RKV 
bhramase divyayogātmanmohayanniva māṃ prabho 
etatkathaya me sarvaṃ yo 'si so 'si namo 'stu te  RKV 
so 'bravīnmāṃ mahādevo brahmāhaṃ viṣṇureva ca 
jagatsarvaṃ mayā vatsa saṃhṛtaṃ kiṃ na budhyase  RKV 
tava mātā pitāhaṃ vai viśvasya ca mahāmune 
kāruṇyaṃ mama saṃjātaṃ dṛṣṭvā magnaṃ mahārṇave  RKV 
pakṣirūpaṃ samāsthāya ato 'trāhaṃ samāgataḥ 
kim arthamāturo bhūtvā bhramasītthaṃ mahārṇave  RKV 
śīghraṃ praviśa matpakṣau yena viśramase dvija 
evamuktastatastena devenāhaṃ nareśvara  RKV 
tato 'haṃ tasya pakṣānte pralīnastu bhramañjale 
kāle yugasāhasrānte aśrānto 'rṇavamadhyagaḥ  RKV 
tataḥ śṛṇomi sahasā dikṣu sarvāsu suvrata 
kiṃcinnūpurasaṃmiśram adbhutaṃ śabdamuttamam  RKV 
tadārṇavajalaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ sahasābhavat 
kimetaditi saṃcintya diśaḥ samavalokayam  RKV 
daśa kanyāstato dikṣu āgatāśca mahārṇave 
vastrālaṃkārasahitā digbhyo nūpurabhūṣitāḥ  RKV 
kāciccandrasamābhāsā kācidādityasaprabhā 
kācidaṃjanapuñjābhā kācidraktotpalaprabhā  RKV 
nānārūpadharā saumyā nānābharaṇabhūṣitā 
arghyapādyādibhirmālyairbakamabhyarcya suvratāḥ  RKV 
tatastaṃ parvatākāraṃ guhyaṃ pakṣiṇamavyayam 
praviveśa mahāghoraṃ parvato hyarṇavaṃ svarāṭ  RKV 
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi tāvantyeva śatāni ca 
triṃśadyojanasāhasraṃ yāvadbhūmaṇḍalaṃ tviti  RKV 
tato bhūmaṇḍalaṃ divyaṃ pañcaratnasamākulam 
divyasphaṭikasopānaṃ rukmastaṃbhamanoramam  RKV 
yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu vistarāddviguṇāyatam 
vāpīkūpasamākīrṇaṃ prāsādāṭṭālakāvṛtam  RKV 
kalpavṛkṣasamākīrṇaṃ dhvajaṣaṣṭivibhūṣitam 
tasminpuravare ramye nānāratnopaśobhitam  RKV 
tathānyacca puraṃ ramyaṃ patākojjvalavedikam 
śatayojanavistīrṇaṃ tāvaddviguṇamāyatam  RKV 
puramadhye tatastasminnadī paramaśobhanā 
mahatī puṇyasalilā nānāratnaśilā tathā  RKV 
tasyāstīre mayā dṛṣṭaṃ taḍitsūryasamaprabham 
indranīlamahānīlaiścitaṃ ratnaiḥ samantataḥ  RKV 
kvacidvahnisamākāraṃ kvacidindrāyudhaprabham 
kvaciddhūmraṃ kvacitpītaṃ kvacidraktaṃ kvacitsitam  RKV 
nānāvarṇaiḥ samāyuktaṃ liṅgamadbhutadarśanam 
brahmaviṣṇvindrasādhyaiśca samantātparivāritam  RKV 
nandīśvaragaṇādhyakṣaiścendrādityaiśca tadvṛtam 
paśyāmi liṅgamīśānaṃ mahāliṅgaṃ tameva ca  RKV 
parivārya tatastaṃ tu prasuptāndevadānavān 
nimīlitākṣānpaśyāmi divyābharaṇabhūṣitān  RKV 
tatastāḥ padmapatrākṣyo nāryaḥ paramasaṃmatāḥ 
nadyāstasyā jale snātvā divyapuṣpairmanoramaiḥ  RKV 
dattvārghapādyaṃ vidhivalliṃgasya saha pakṣiṇā 
arcayantīrvarārohā daśa tāḥ pramadottamāḥ  RKV 
tatastvabhyarcya talliṅgaṃ tasminneva purottame 
sarvā adarśanaṃ jagmurvidyuto 'bhragaṇeṣviva  RKV 
na cāsau pakṣirāṭ tasminna striyo na ca devatāḥ 
tadevaikaṃ sthitaṃ liṅgamarcayanvismayānvitaḥ  RKV 
tato'haṃ duḥkhamūḍhātmā rudramāyeti cintayan 
tataḥ kanyāḥ samuttīrya divyāṃbaravibhūṣaṇāḥ  RKV 
bhāsayantyo jagatsarvaṃ vidyuto 'bhragaṇāniva 
padmairhiraṇmayairdivyairarcayitvā śubhānanāḥ  RKV 
viviśustajjalaṃ kṣipraṃ samaṃtād varabhūṣaṇāḥ 
tasminpuravare cānye tāmevāhaṃ punaḥpunaḥ  RKV 
paśyāmi hyamarāṃ kanyām arcayantīṃ maheśvaram 
tato 'haṃ tāṃ varārohāmapṛcchaṃ kamalekṣaṇām  RKV 
kā tvamasminpure devi vasase śivamarcatī 
tāścāgatāḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ kva gatāste gaṇeśvarāḥ  RKV 
namo 'stu te mahābhāge brūhi puṇye maheśvari 
tava prasādādvijñātumetadicchāmi suvrate 
dayāṃ kṛtvā mahādevi kathayasva mamānaghe  RKV 
śryuvāca
vismṛtāhaṃ kathaṃ vipra dṛṣṭvā kalpe purātane 
mā te 'bhūtsmṛtivibhraṃśaḥ sā cāhaṃ kalpavāhinī  RKV 
narmadā nāma vikhyātā rudradehād viniḥsṛtā 
yāstāḥ kanyāstvayā dṛṣṭā hyarcayantyo maheśvaram  RKV 
yābhistviha samānītaḥ pakṣirājasamanvitāḥ 
diśastā viddhi sarveśāḥ sarvāstvaṃ munisattama  RKV 
tiryakpakṣisvarūpeṇa mahāyogī maheśvaraḥ 
ebhiḥ śivapurādvipra ānītaḥ sa maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
saiṣa devo mahādevo liṅgamūrtirvyavasthitaḥ 
arcyate brahmaviṣṇvindraiḥ surāsurajagadguruḥ  RKV 
layamāyāti yasmāddhi jagatsarvaṃ carācaram 
tena liṅgamiti proktaṃ purāṇajñair maharṣibhiḥ  RKV 
tena devagaṇāḥ sarve saṃkṣiptā māyayā purā 
pralīnāścaiva lokeśa na dṛśyante hi sāṃpratam  RKV 
punardṛśyā bhaviṣyanti sṛjamānāḥ svayaṃbhuvā 
sāhaṃ liṅgārcanaparā narmadā nāma nāmataḥ  RKV 
kālaṃ yugasahasrasya rudrasya paricārikā 
asya prasādādamarastathā tvaṃ dvijapuṃgava  RKV 
satyārjavadayāyuktaḥ siddho 'si tvaṃ śivārcanāt 
evamuktvā tu sā devī tatraivāntaradhīyata  RKV 
tāḥ striyaḥ sa ca deveśo bakarūpo maheśvaraḥ 
tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā avatīrya mahānadīm  RKV 
snātvā samarcaya tvaṃ hi vidhinā mantrapūrvakam 
tato 'haṃ sahasā tasmāt samuttīrya jalāśayāt  RKV 
na ca paśyāmi talliṅgaṃ na ca tāṃ nimnagāṃ nṛpa 
tadaiva lokāḥ saṃjātāḥ kṣitiścaiva sakānanā  RKV 
ṛkṣacandrārkavitataṃ tadeva ca nabhastalam 
yathāpūrvam adṛṣṭaṃ tu tathaiva ca punaḥ kṛtam 
nato'haṃ manasā devamapūjayaṃ maheśvaram  RKV 
evaṃ bake purā kalpe mayā dṛṣṭeyam avyayā 
narmadā martyalokasya mahāpātakanāśinī  RKV 
tasmāddharmaparair vipraiḥ kṣatraśūdraviśādibhiḥ 
sadā sevyā mahābhāgā dharmavṛddhyarthakāribhiḥ  RKV 
ye 'pi bhaktayā sakṛttoye narmadāyā maheśvaram 
snātvā te sarvaṃ pāpaṃ nāśayantyasaṃśayam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye bakakalpasamudbhavo nāmāṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
punaryugāntaṃ te cānyaṃ sampravakṣyāmi tacchṛṇu 
sūryairādīpite loke jaṅgame sthāvare purā  RKV 
saritsaraḥsamudreṣu kṣayaṃ yāteṣu sarvaśaḥ 
nirmānuṣavaṣaṭkāre hyamaryādagatiṃ gate  RKV 
nānārūpaistato medhaiḥ śakrāyudhavirājitaiḥ 
sarvamāpūritaṃ vyoma vāryaughaiḥ pūrite tadā  RKV 
tatastvekārṇavībhūte sarvataḥ salilāvṛte 
jagatkṛtvodare sarvaṃ suṣvāpa bhagavānharaḥ  RKV 
prakṛtiṃ svāmavaṣṭabhya yogātmā sa prajāpatiḥ 
śete yugasahasrāntaṃ kālamāviśya sārṇavam  RKV 
tatra suptaṃ mahātmānaṃ brahmalokanivāsinaḥ 
bhṛgvādiṛṣayaḥ sarve ye cānye sanakādayaḥ  RKV 
paryaṅke vimale śubhre nānāstaraṇasaṃstṛte 
śayānaṃ dadṛśurdevaṃ sapatnīkaṃ vṛṣadhvajam  RKV 
viśvarūpā tu sā nārī viśvarūpo maheśvaraḥ 
gāḍhamāliṅgya suptas tāṃ dadṛśe cāhamavyayam  RKV 
pādamūle tatastasya śyāmāṃ tāṃ padmalakṣaṇām 
kanyāṃ paśyāmi suśroṇīṃ caraṇau tasya mṛdgatīm  RKV 
vimalāmbarasaṃvītāṃ vyālayajñopavītinīm 
śyāmāṃ kamalapatrākṣīṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām  RKV 
sakalaṃ yugasāhasraṃ narmadeyaṃ vijānatī 
prasuptaṃ devadeveśamupāste varavarṇinī  RKV 
hṛtairvedaiścaturbhiśca brahmāpyevaṃ maheśvaraḥ 
bhṛgvādyairmānasaiḥ putraiḥ stauti śaṅkaramavyayam  RKV 
bhaktyā paramayā rājaṃstatra śambhum anāmayam 
stuvantastatra deveśaṃ mantrairīśvarasambhavaiḥ  RKV 
prasuptaṃ devamīśānaṃ bodhayansamupasthitaḥ 
uttiṣṭha hara piṅgākṣa mahādeva maheśvara  RKV 
mama vedā hṛtāḥ sarve ato 'haṃ stotumudyataḥ 
vedairvyāptaṃ jagatsarvaṃ divyādivyaṃ carācaram  RKV 
atītaṃ vartamānaṃ ca smarāmi ca sṛjāmyaham 
tairvinā cāhamekastu mūko 'dho jaḍavatsadā  RKV 
gatirvīryaṃ balotsāhau tairvinā na prajāyate 
tairvinā devadeveśa nāhaṃ kiṃcit smarāmi vai  RKV 
tānvedāndevadeveśa śīghraṃ me dātumarhasi 
jaḍāndhabadhiraṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam  RKV 
sthānādi daśa catvāri na śobhante sureśvara 
praṇamāmy alpavīryatvād vedahīnaḥ sureśvara  RKV 
vedebhyaḥ sakalaṃ jātaṃ yatkiṃcitsacarācaram 
tāvacchobhanti śāstrāṇi samastāni jagadguro  RKV 
yāvadvedanidhirayaṃ nopatiṣṭhetsanātanaḥ 
yathoditena sūryeṇa tamo yāti vināśatām  RKV 
evaṃ samastapāpāni yānti vedasya dhāraṇāt 
vede rahasi yatsūkṣmaṃ yattadbrahma sanātanam  RKV 
hṛdisthaṃ deva jānāmi gataṃ tadvedagarjanāt 
vedānuccarato me 'dya tava śaṅkara cāgrataḥ  RKV 
akasmātte gatā vedā na sṛjeyaṃ vibho bhuvam 
te 'pi sarve mahādeva praviṣṭāḥ sammukhārṇavam  RKV 
te yācyamānā deveśa tiṣṭhantu smaraṇe mama 
duhiteyaṃ viśālākṣī sarvaḥ sarvaṃ vijānate  RKV 
jāyatī yugasāhasraṃ nānyā kācidbhavedṛśī 
ṛṣiścāyaṃ mahābhāgo mārkaṇḍo dhīmatāṃ varaḥ  RKV 
kalpe kalpe mahādeva tvāmayaṃ paryupāsate 
jagattrayahitārthāya carate vratamuttamam  RKV 
evamuktastu deveśo brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā 
uvāca ślakṣṇayā vācā narmadāṃ saritāṃ varām  RKV 
kathayasva mahābhāge brahmaṇastvaṃ tu pṛcchataḥ 
kena vedā hṛtāḥ sarve vedhaso jagatīguroḥ  RKV 
evamuktā tu rudreṇa uvāca mṛgalocanā 
brahmaṇo japato vedāṃstvayi supte maheśvara  RKV 
bhavataśchidramāsādya ghore 'sminsalilāvṛte 
pūrvakalpasamudbhūtāvasurau suradurjayau  RKV 
śriyāvṛttau mahādeva tvayā cotpāditau purā 
surāsurasudurjeyau dānavau madhukaiṭabhau  RKV 
tau vāyubhūtau sūkṣmau ca paṭhato 'smātpitāmahāt 
tāvāśu hṛtvā vedāṃśca praviṣṭau ca mahārṇavam  RKV 
etacchrutvā mahātejā hyamṛtāyāstato vacaḥ 
sasmāra sa ca deveśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam  RKV 
sa viveśa mahārāja bhūtalaṃ sasurottamaḥ 
dānavāntakaro devaḥ sarvadaivatapūjitaḥ  RKV 
mīnarūpadharo devo loḍayāmāsa cārṇam 
vedāṃśca dadṛśe tatra pātāle nihitānprabhuḥ  RKV 
tau ca daityau mahāvīryau dṛṣṭavānmadhusūdanaḥ 
mahāvegau mahābāhū sūdayāmāsa tejasā  RKV 
vedāṃstatrāpi toyasthānānināya jagadguruḥ 
caturvaktrāya devāyādadāccakravibhūṣitaḥ  RKV 
tataḥ prahṛṣṭo bhagavān vedāṃllabdhvā pitāmahaḥ 
janayāmāsa nikhilaṃ jagadbhūyaścarācaram  RKV 
sā ca devī nadī puṇyā rudrasya paricārikā 
pāvanī sarvabhūtānāṃ provāha salilaṃ tadā  RKV 
tasyāstīre tato devā ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ 
yajanti tryambakaṃ devaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā  RKV 
ekā mūrtirmaheśasya kāraṇāntaragatā 
traiguṇyā kurute karma brahmacakrīśarūpataḥ  RKV 
eteṣāṃ tu pṛthagbhāvaṃ ye kurvanti sumohitāḥ 
teṣāṃ dharmaḥ kutaḥ siddhirjāyate pāpakarmiṇām  RKV 
evametā mahānadyastisro rudrasamudbhavāḥ 
ekā eva tridhā bhūtā gaṅgā revā sarasvatī  RKV 
gaṅgā tu vaiṣṇavī mūrtiḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśinī 
rudradehasamudbhūtā narmadā caivameva tu  RKV 
brāhmī sarasvatī mūrtistriṣu lokeṣu viśrutā 
divyā kāmagamā devī vāgvibhūtyai tu saṃsthitā  RKV 
narmadā paramā kācinmartyamūrtikalā śivā 
divyā kāmagamā devī sarvatra surapūjitā  RKV 
vyāpinī sarvabhūtānāṃ sūkṣmātsūkṣmatarā smṛtā 
akṣayā hyamṛtā hyeṣā svargasopānamuttamā  RKV 
sṛṣṭā rudreṇa lokānāṃ saṃsārārṇavatāriṇī  RKV 
sīrajalaṃ ye 'pi pibanti loke mucyanti te pāpaviśeṣasaṅghaiḥ 
vrajanti saṃsāramanādibhāvaṃ tyaktvā ciraṃ mokṣapadaṃ viśuddham  RKV 
yathā gaṅgā tathā revā tathā caiva sarasvatī 
samaṃ puṇyaphalaṃ proktaṃ snānadarśanacintanaiḥ  RKV 
varadānānmahābhāgā hyadhikā cocyate budhaiḥ 
kāruṇyāntarabhāvena na mṛtā samupāgatā  RKV 
mucyante darśanāttena pātakaiḥ snānamaṅgalaiḥ 
narmadāyāṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha ye namanti trilocanam  RKV 
umārudrāṅgasambhūtā yena caiṣā mahānadī 
lokānprāpayate svargaṃ tena puṇyatvamāgatā  RKV 
ya evamīśānavarasya dehaṃ vibhajya devīmiha saṃśṛṇoti 
sa yāti rudraṃ mahatāraveṇa gandharvayakṣairiva gīyamānaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye narmadotpattitatsnānaphalādikathanaṃ  
nāma navamo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kasminkalpe mahābhāgā narmadeyaṃ dvijottama 
vibhaktā ṛṣibhiḥ sarvaistapoyuktairmahātmabhiḥ  RKV 
etadvistarataḥ sarvaṃ brūhi me vadatāṃ vara 
kalpānte yadbhavetkaṣṭaṃ lokānāṃ tattvameva ca  RKV 
atīte tu purā kalpe yatheyaṃ vartate 'nagha 
asyāntyasya ca kalpasya vyavasthāṃ kathaya prabho 
evamuktaḥ sabhāmadhye mārkaṇḍo vākyamabravīt  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
vakṣye 'haṃ śrūyatāṃ sarvaiḥ katheyaṃ pūrvataḥ śrutā  RKV 
mahatkatheyaṃ vaiśiṣṭī kalpādasmātparaṃ tu yā 
lokakṣayakaro ghora āsītkālaḥ sudāruṇaḥ  RKV 
tasminnapi mahāghore yatheyaṃ vā mṛtā satī 
parituṣṭairvibhaktā ca śṛṇudhvaṃ tāṃ kathāmimām  RKV 
yugānte samanuprāpte pitāmahadinatraye 
mānasā brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ sākṣādbrahmeva sattamāḥ  RKV 
sanakādyā mahātmāno ye ca vaimānikā gaṇāḥ 
yamendravaruṇādyāśca lokapālā dinatraye  RKV 
kālāpekṣāstu tiṣṭhanti lokavṛttāntatatparāḥ 
tataḥ kalpakṣaye prāpte teṣāṃ jñānamanuttamam  RKV 
sarveṣāṃ naśyate cāyuryugarūpānusārataḥ 
bhūrlokaṃ te parityajya agamaṃśca bhuvaṃ tadā  RKV 
svarlokaṃ ca mahaścaiva janaścaiva tapastadā 
āśrayaṃ satyalokaṃ ca sarvalokamanuttamam  RKV 
kālaṃ yugasahasrāntaṃ putrapautrasamanvitāḥ 
satyaloke ca tiṣṭhanti yāvatsaṃjāyate jagat  RKV 
brahmaputrāśca ye kecitkalpādau na bhavanti ha 
trailokyaṃ te parityajya anādhāraṃ bhavanti ca  RKV 
taiḥ sārdhaṃ ye tu te viprā anye cāpi tapodhanāḥ 
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāśca anye vaimānikā gaṇāḥ  RKV 
ṛṣayaśca mahābhāgā varṇāścānye pṛthagvidhāḥ 
sīdanti bhūmyāṃ sahitā ye cānye talavāsinaḥ  RKV 
anāvṛṣṭirabhūttatra mahatī śatavārṣikī 
lokakṣayakarī raudrā vṛkṣavīrudvināśinī  RKV 
trailokyasaṃkṣobhakarī saptārṇavaviśoṣaṇī 
tato lokāḥ kṣudhāviṣṭā bhramantīva diśo daśa  RKV 
kaṃdairmūlaiḥ phalairvāpi vartayante suduḥkhitāḥ 
saritaḥ sāgarāḥ kūpāḥ sevante pāvanāni ca  RKV 
tatrāpi sarve śuṣyanti saridbhiḥ saha sāgarāḥ 
tato yānyalpasārāṇi sattvāni pṛthivītale  RKV 
tānyevāgre pralīyante bhinnānyurujalena vai 
atha saṃkṣīyamāṇāsu saritsu saha sāgaraiḥ  RKV 
ṛṣīṇāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasraṃ kurukṣetranivāsinām 
ye ca vaikhānasā viprā dantolūkhalinastathā  RKV 
himācalaguhāguhye ye vasanti tapodhanāḥ 
sarve te māmupāgamya kṣuttṛṣārtāstapodhanāḥ  RKV 
ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve sīdayāmo mahāmune 
saritsāgaraśailāntaṃ jagatsaṃśuṣyate dvija  RKV 
kutra yāsyāma sahitā yāvatkālasya paryayaḥ 
dīrghāyurasi viprendra na mṛtastvaṃ yugakṣaye  RKV 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca sarvaṃ tava hṛdi sthitam 
tasmāttvaṃ vetsi sarvaṃ ca kathayasva mahāvrata  RKV 
kīdṛkkālaṃ mahābhāga kṣapiṣyāmo 'tha suvrata 
anāvṛṣṭihataṃ sarvaṃ sīdate sacarācaram  RKV 
paritrāhi mahābhāga na yathā yāma saṃkṣayam 
tataḥ saṃcintya manasā tvaranviprān athābravam  RKV 
kurukṣetraṃ tyajadhvaṃ ca putradārasamanvitāḥ 
tyaktvodīcīṃ diśaṃ sarve yāmo yāmyāmanuttamām  RKV 
nagaragrāmaghoṣāḍhyāṃ purapattanaśobhitām 
gacchāmo narmadātīraṃ bahusiddhaniṣevitam  RKV 
rudrāṅgīṃ tāṃ mahāpuṇyāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm 
paśyāmastāṃ mahābhāgāṃ nyagrodhāvārasaṃkulām  RKV 
māheśvarairbhāgavataiḥ sāṃkhyaiḥ siddhaiḥ susevitām 
anāvṛṣṭibhayādbhītāḥ kūlayorubhayorapi  RKV 
āśrame hyāśramāndivyānkārayāmo jitavratāḥ 
evamuktāstu te sarve sametānucaraiḥ saha  RKV 
narmadātīramāsādya sthitāḥ sarve 'kutobhayāḥ 
kiṃcit pūrvam anusmṛtya purā kalpādibhirbhayam  RKV 
prāptāstu narmadātīramādāveva kalau yuge 
tato varṣaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ divyaṃ revātaṭe 'vasan  RKV 
ṣaḍviṃśacca sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi ca 
tatrāścaryaṃ mayā dṛṣṭamṛṣīṇāṃ vasatāṃ nṛpa  RKV 
anāvṛṣṭihate loke saṃśuṣke sthāvare care 
bhinne yugādikalane hāhābhūte vicetane  RKV 
cāturvarṇe pralīne tu naṣṭe homabalikrame 
niḥsvāhe nirvaṣaṭkāre śaucācāravivarjite  RKV 
iyamekā saricchreṣṭhā ṛṣikoṭiniṣevitā 
nānyā kācittriloke 'pi ramaṇīyā nareśvara  RKV 
yatheyaṃ puṇyasalilā indrasyevāmarāvatī 
devatāyatanaiḥ śubhrairāśramaiśca sukalpitaiḥ  RKV 
śobhate narmadā devī svarge mandākinī yathā 
yāvadvṛkṣā mahāśailā yāvatsāgarasaṃbhavā  RKV 
ubhayoḥ kūlayos tāvan maṇḍitāyatanaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
hūyadbhir agnihotraiśca havirdhūmasamākulā  RKV 
babhūva narmadā devī prāvṛṭkāla iva śarvarī 
devatāyatanairnaikaiḥ pūjāsaṃskāraśobhitā  RKV 
saridbhirbhrājate śreṣṭhā purī śākrī ca bhāskarī 
kecitpañcāgnitapasaḥ kecidapyagnihotriṇaḥ  RKV 
kecid dhūmakamaśnanti tapasyugre vyavasthitāḥ 
ātmayajñaratāḥ kecidapare bhaktibhāginaḥ  RKV 
vaiṣṇavajñānam āsādya kecicchaivaṃ vrataṃ tathā 
ekarātraṃ dvirātraṃ ca kecitṣaṣṭhāhabhojanāḥ  RKV 
cāndrāyaṇavidhānaiśca kṛcchriṇaścātikṛcchriṇaḥ 
evaṃvidhaistapobhiśca narmadātīraśobhitaiḥ  RKV 
yajadbhiḥ śaṃkaraṃ devaṃ keśavaṃ bhāti nityadā 
ekatve ca pṛthaktve ca yajatāṃ ca maheśvaram  RKV 
kalau yuge mahāghore prāptāḥ siddhimanuttamām 
yasya yasya hi yā bhaktirvijñānaṃ yasya yādṛśam  RKV 
yasminyasmiṃśca deve tu tāṃtāmīśo 'dadātprabhuḥ 
svabhāvaikatayā bhaktyā tāmetyāntaḥ pralīyate  RKV 
saṃsāre parivartante ye pṛthagbhājino narāḥ 
ye mahāvṛkṣamīśānaṃ tyaktvā śākhāvalambinaḥ  RKV 
punarāvartamānāste jāyante hi caturyuge 
devānte sthāvarānte ca saṃsāre cābhramankramāt  RKV 
punarjanma punaḥ svarge punarghore ca raurave 
ye punardevamīśānaṃ bhavaṃ bhaktisusaṃsthitāḥ  RKV 
yajanti narmadātīre na punaste bhavanti ca 
ā dehapatanāt kecid upāsantaḥ paraṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
keciddvādaśabhirvarṣaiḥ ṣaḍbharanye tapodhanāḥ 
tribhiḥ saṃvatsaraiḥ kecitkecitsaṃvatsareṇa tu  RKV 
ṣaḍbhirmāsaistu saṃsiddhās tribhir māsais tathāpare 
munayo devamāśritya narmadāṃ ca yaśasvinīm  RKV 
chittvā saṃsāradoṣāṃśca agamanbrahma śāśvatam 
evaṃ kaliyuge ghore śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ  RKV 
narmadātīramāśritya munayo rudramāviśan  RKV 
ye narmadātīramupetya viprāḥ śaive vrate yatnam upaprapannāḥ 
trikālam ambhaḥ pravigāhya bhaktyā devaṃ samabhyarcya śivaṃ vrajanti  RKV 
dhyānārcanairjāpyamahāvrataiśca nārāyaṇaṃ vā satataṃ smaranti 
te dhautapāṇḍurapaṭā iva rājahaṃsāḥ saṃsārasāgarajalasya taranti pāram  RKV 
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyamutkṣipya bhujam ucyate 
idamekaṃ suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā  RKV 
yo vā haraṃ pūjayate jitātmā māsaṃ ca pakṣaṃ ca vasennarendra 
revāṃ samāśritya mahānubhāvaḥ sa devadevo 'tha bhavetpinākī  RKV 
kīṭāḥ pataṃgāśca pipīlikāśca ye vai mriyante 'mbhasi narmadāyāḥ 
te divyarūpāstu kulaprasūtāḥ śataṃ samā dharmaparā bhavanti  RKV 
kālena vṛkṣāḥ prapatanti ye 'pi mahātaraṃgaughanikṛttamūlāḥ 
te narmadāṃbhobhirapāstapāpā dedīpyamānāstridivaṃ prayānti  RKV 
akāmakāmāśca tathā sakāmā revāntam āśritya mriyanti tīre 
jaḍāndhamūkās tridivaṃ prayānti kimatra viprā bhavabhāvayuktāḥ  RKV 
māsopavāsairapi śoṣitāṅgā na tāṃ gatiṃ yānti vimuktadehāḥ 
mriyanti revājalapūtakāyāḥ śivārcane keśavabhāvayuktāḥ  RKV 
nīvāraśyāmākayaveṅgudādyair anyair munīndrā iha vartayanti 
āpritya kūlaṃ tridaśānugītaṃ te narmadāyā na viśanti mṛtyum  RKV 
bhramanti ye tīramupetya devyās trikāladevārcanasatyapūtāḥ 
viṇmūtracarmāsthitiropadhānāḥ kukṣau yuvatyā na vasanti bhūyaḥ  RKV 
kiṃ yajñadānairbahubhiśca teṣāṃ niṣevitaistīrthavaraiḥ samastaiḥ 
revātaṭaṃ dakṣiṇamuttaraṃ vā sevanti te rudracarānupūrvam  RKV 
te vañcitāḥ paṅgujaḍāndhabhūtā lokeṣu martyāḥ paśubhiśca tulyāḥ 
ye nāśritā rudraśarīrabhūtāṃ sopānapaṅktiṃ tridivasya revām  RKV 
yugaṃ kaliṃ ghoramimaṃ ya iccheddraṣṭuṃ kadācinna punar dvijendraḥ 
sa narmadātīramupetya sarvaṃ sampūjayet sarvavimuktasaṃgaḥ  RKV 
vighnair anekair atiyojyamānā ye tīram ujhanti na narmadāyāḥ 
te caiva sarvasya hitārthabhūtā vandyāśca te sarvajanasya mānyāḥ  RKV 
bhṛgvatrigārgeyavaśiṣṭhakaṅkāḥ śataiḥ sametair niyatās tvasaṃkhyaiḥ 
siddhiṃ parāṃ te hi jalaplutāṅgāḥ prāptāstu lokānmarutāṃ na cānye  RKV 
jñānaṃ mahatpuṇyatamaṃ pavitraṃ paṭhantyado nityaviśuddhasattvāḥ 
gatiṃ parāṃ yānti mahānubhāvā rudrasya vākyaṃ hi yathā pramāṇam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye narmadāsnānaphalaśrutikathanaṃ nāma  
daśamo'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
aho mahatpuṇyatamā viśiṣṭā kṣayaṃ na yātā iha yā yugānte 
tasmātsadā sevyatamā munīndrair dhyānārcanasnānaparāyaṇaiśca  RKV 
yāmāśritya gatā mokṣamṛṣayo dharmavatsalāḥ 
ye tvayoktāstu niyamā ṛṣīṇāṃ vedanirmitāḥ  RKV 
mokṣāvāptirbhavedyeṣāṃ niyamaiśca pṛthagvidhaiḥ

bhrājate sā saricchreṣṭhā tārābhir dyaur grahairiva  RKV 
tatra tairbahulaiḥ śubhrair brāhmaṇair vedaparāgaiḥ 
narmadā dharmadā pūrvaṃ saṃvibhaktā yathākramam  RKV 
ṛṣibhir daśakoṭibhir narmadātīravāsibhiḥ 
vibhakteyaṃ vibhaktāṅgī narmadā śarmadā nṛṇām  RKV 
yajñopavītaiśca śubhair akṣasūtraiśca bhārata 
kūladvaye mahāpuṇyā narmadodadhigāminī  RKV 
pṛthagāyatanaiḥ śubhrairliṅgairvālukamṛnmayaiḥ 
bhrājate yā saricchreṣṭhā nakṣatrairiva śarvarī  RKV 
evaṃ ta ṛṣayaḥ sarve tarpayantaḥ surānpitḥn 
nyavasannarmadātīre yāvadābhūtasamplavam  RKV 
kiṃcidgate tatastasminghore varṣaśatādhike 
ardharātre tadā kanyā jalāduttīrya bhārata  RKV 
vidyutpuṃjasamābhāsā vyālayajñopavītinī 
triśūlāgrakarā saumyā tānuvāca ṛṣīṃstadā  RKV 
āgacchadhvaṃ munigaṇā viśadhvaṃ māmayonijām 
sametāḥ putradāraiśca tataḥ siddhimavāpsyatha  RKV 
yasya yasya hi yā vāñchā tasya tāṃ tāṃ dadāmyaham 
viṣṇuṃ brahmāṇamīśānamanyaṃ vā suramuttamam  RKV 
tatra sarvānnayiṣyāmi prasannā varadā hyaham 
prāṇāyāmaparā bhūtvā māṃ viśadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ  RKV 
saha putraiśca dāraiśca tyaktvāśramapadāni ca 
kālakṣepo na kartavyaḥ pralayo 'yamupasthitaḥ  RKV 
saṃhāraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ kalpadāhaḥ sudāruṇaḥ 
ekāham abhavaṃ pūrvaṃ mahāghore janakṣaye  RKV 
śeṣā nadyaḥ samudrāśca sarva eva kṣayaṃgatāḥ 
varadānān maheśasya tenāhaṃ na kṣayaṃ gatā  RKV 
amṛtaḥ śāśvato devaḥ sthāṇurīśaḥ sanātanaḥ 
sa pūjitaḥ prārthito vā kiṃ na dadyād dvijottamāḥ  RKV 
evamuktvā ṛṣīvrevā praviveśa jalaṃ tataḥ 
karāttaśūlā sā devī vyālayajñopavītinī  RKV 
tataste tadvacaḥ śrutvā vismayāpannamānasāḥ 
abhivandya ca māṃ sarve kṣāmayantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ  RKV 
kṣamyatāṃ no yaduktaṃ hi vasatāṃ tava saṃśraye 
gṛhāṃstyaktvā mahābhāgāḥ saśiṣyāḥ sahabāndhavāḥ  RKV 
japtvā caikākṣaraṃ brahma hṛdi dhyātvā maheśvaram 
snātvā ca mantrapūtābhiratha cādbhir jitavratāḥ  RKV 
viviśurnarmadātoyaṃ sapakṣā iva parvatāḥ 
dyotayanto diśaḥ sarvāḥ kuśahastāḥ sahāgrayaḥ  RKV 
gateṣu teṣu rājendra ahamekaḥ sthitastadā 
amareśaṃ samāsādya pūjayannarmadāṃ nadīm  RKV 
anubhūtāḥ saptakalpā māyūrādyā mayā nṛpa 
prasādād vedhasaḥ sarve revayā saha bhārata  RKV 
janmato'dya dinaṃ yāvanna jāne 'syāḥ purāsthitim  RKV 
iyaṃ hi śāṃkarī śaktiḥ kalā śambhorilāhvayā 
narmadā duritadhvaṃsakāriṇī bhavatāriṇī  RKV 
yadāhamapi nābhūvaṃ purākalpeṣu pāṇḍava 
caturdaśasu kalpeṣu teṣviyaṃ sukhasaṃsthitā  RKV 
caturdaśa purā kalpā na mṛtā yeṣu narmadā 
tānahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi devī prāha yathā mama  RKV 
kāpilaṃ prathamaṃ viddhi prājāpatyaṃ dvitīyakam 
brāhmaṃ saumyaṃ ca sāvitraṃ bārhaspatyaṃ prabhāsakam  RKV 
māhendram agnikalpaṃ ca jayantaṃ mārutaṃ tathā 
vaiṣṇavaṃ bahurūpaṃ ca jyautiṣaṃ ca caturdaśam  RKV 
ete kalpā mayā khyātā na mṛtā yeṣu narmadā 
māyūraṃ pañcadaśamaṃ kaurmaṃ caivātra ṣoḍaśam  RKV 
bakaṃ mātsyaṃ ca pādmaṃ ca vaṭakalpaṃ ca bhārata 
ekaviṃśatimaṃ caitaṃ vārāhaṃ sāṃpratīnakam  RKV 
ime sapta mayā sākaṃ revayā pariśīlitāḥ 
ekaviṃśatikalpāstu narmadāyāḥ śivāṅgataḥ  RKV 
saṃjātāyā nṛpaśreṣṭha mayā dṛṣṭā hyanekaśaḥ 
kathitā nṛpatiśreṣṭha bhūyaḥ kiṃ kathayāmi te  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmya ekaviṃśatikalpakathānakavarṇanaṃ nāma  
trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca

gatāstu paramaṃ lokaṃ tataḥ kiṃ jātamadbhutam  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tatasteṣu prayāteṣu narmadātīravāsiṣu 
babhūva raudrasaṃhāraḥ sarvabhūtakṣayaṃkaraḥ  RKV 
kailāsaśikharasthaṃ tu mahādevaṃ sanātanam 
brahmādyāḥ prāstuvan devam ṛgyajuḥsāmabhiḥ śivam  RKV 
saṃhara tvaṃ jagad deva sadevāsuramānuṣam 
prāpto yugasahasrāntaḥ kālaḥ saṃharaṇakṣamaḥ  RKV 
madrūpaṃ tu samāsthāya tvayā caitadvinirmitam 
vaiṣṇavīṃ mūrtimāsthāya tvayaitatparipālitam  RKV 
ekā mūrtistridhā jātā brāhmī śaivī ca vaiṣṇavī 
sṛṣṭisaṃhārarakṣārthaṃ bhavedevaṃ maheśvara  RKV 
etacchrutvā vacastathyaṃ viṣṇośca parameṣṭhinaḥ 
sagaṇaḥ saparīvāraḥ saha tābhyāṃ sahomayā  RKV 
samalokānvibhidyemānbhagavānnīlalohitaḥ 
bhūrādyabrahmalokāntaṃ bhittvāṇḍaṃ parataḥ param  RKV 
śaivaṃ padam ajaṃ divyam āviśat saha tairvibhuḥ 
na tatra vāyur nākāśaṃ nāgnistatra na bhūtalam  RKV 
yatra saṃtiṣṭhe deva umayā saha śaṅkaraḥ 
na sūryo na grahāstatra na ṛkṣāṇi diśastathā  RKV 
na lokapālā na sukhaṃ na ca duḥkhaṃ nṛpottama  RKV 
brāhmaṃ padaṃ yatkavayo vadanti śaivaṃ padaṃ yatkavayo vadanti 
kṣetrajñamīśaṃ pravadanti cānye sāṃkhyāśca gāyanti kilādimokṣam  RKV 
yadbrahma ādyaṃ pravadanti kecidyaṃ sarvamīśānamajaṃ purāṇam 
tam ekarūpaṃ tam anekarūpam arūpam ādyaṃ param avyayākhyam  RKV 
avarṇamapyartham anāmagotraṃ turyaṃ padaṃ yatkavayo vadanti 
dhyānārthavijñānamayaṃ susūkṣmam ātmastham īśānavaraṃ vareṇyam  RKV 
tatastrayaste bhagavantamīśaṃ samprāpya saṃkṣipya bhavantyarthakam 
pṛthaksvarūpaistu punasta eva jagat samastaṃ paripālayanti  RKV 
saṃhāraṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ rudratve kurute prabhuḥ 
viṣṇutve pālayellokānbrahmatve sṛṣṭikārakaḥ  RKV 
prakṛtyā saha saṃyuktaḥ kālo bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ 
viśvarūpā mahābhāgā tasya pārśve vyavasthitā  RKV 
yāmāhuḥ prakṛtiṃ tajjñāḥ padārthānāṃ vicakṣaṇāḥ 
puruṣatve prakṛtitve ca kāraṇaṃ parameśvaraḥ  RKV 
tasmād etajjagatsarvaṃ carācaram 
tasminneva layaṃ yāti yugānte samupasthite  RKV 
bhagaliṅgāṅkitaṃ sarvaṃ vyāptaṃ vai parameṣṭhinā 
bhagarūpo bhavedviṣṇurliṅgarūpo maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
bhāti sarveṣu lokeṣu gīyate bhūrbhuvādiṣu 
praviṣṭaḥ sarvabhūteṣu tena viṣṇurbhagaḥ smṛtaḥ  RKV 
viśanādviṣṇurityuktaḥ sarvadevamayo mahān 
bhāsanādgamanāccaiva bhagasaṃjñā prakīrtitā  RKV 
brahmādistambaparyantaṃ yasminneti layaṃ jagat 
ekabhāvaṃ samāpannaṃ liṅgaṃ tasmād vidurbudhāḥ  RKV 
mahādevastato devīmāha pārśve sthitāṃ tadā 
saṃharasva jagatsarvaṃ mā vilambasva śobhane  RKV 
tyaja saumyamidaṃ rūpaṃ sitacandrāṃśunirmalam 
rudraṃ rūpaṃ samāsthāya saṃharasva carācaram  RKV 
raudrairbhūtagaṇairghorairdevi tvaṃ parivāritā 
jīvalokamimaṃ sarvaṃ bhakṣayasvāmbujekṣaṇe  RKV 
tato 'haṃ mardayiṣyāmi plāvayiṣye tathā jagat 
kṛtvā caikārṇavaṃ bhūyaḥ sukhaṃ svapsye tvayā saha  RKV 
śrīdevyuvāca
nāhaṃ deva jagaccaitatsaṃharāmi mahādyute 
ambā bhūtvā viceṣṭaṃ na bhakṣayāmi bhṛśāturam  RKV 
strīsvabhāvena kāruṇyaṃ karoti hṛdayaṃ mama 
kathaṃ vai nirdahiṣyāmi jagad etajjagatpate  RKV 
tasmāt tvaṃ svayamevedaṃ jagatsaṃhara śaṅkara 
athaivamuktastāṃ devīṃ dhūrjaṭirnīlalohitaḥ  RKV 
kruddho nirbhartsayāmāsa huṅkāreṇa maheśvarīm 
oṃ huṃphaṭ tvaṃ sa ityāha kopāviṣṭair athekṣaṇaiḥ  RKV 
huṃkāritā viśālākṣī pīnorujaghanasthalā 
tatkṣaṇāccābhavadraudrā kālarātrīva bhārata  RKV 
huṃkurvatī mahānādairnādayantī diśo daśa

vidyutsampātaduṣprekṣyā vidyutsaṃghātacañcalā

muktakeśī viśālākṣī kṛśagrīvā kṛśodarī

vṛścikairagnipuñjābhair gonasaiśca vibhūṣitā 
trailokyaṃ pūrayāmāsa vistāreṇocchrayeṇa ca  RKV 
bhāsurāṅgā tu saṃvṛttā kṛṣṇasarpaikakuṇḍalā 
citradaṇḍodyatakarā vyāghracarmopasevitā  RKV 
vyavardhata mahāraudrā jagatsaṃhārakāriṇī 
sṛkkiṇī lelihānā ca krūraphūtkārakāriṇī  RKV 
vyāttāsyā ghurghurārāvā jagatsaṃkṣobhakāriṇī 
kheladbhūtānugā krūrā niḥśvāsocchvāsakāriṇī  RKV 
jātāṭṭaahāsā durnāsā vahnikuṇḍasamekṣaṇā 
prodyatkilakilārāvā dadāha sakalaṃ jagat  RKV 
dahyamānāḥ surāstatra patanti dharaṇītale 
patanti yakṣagandharvāḥ sakinnaramahoragāḥ  RKV 
patanti bhūtasaṅghāśca hāhāhaihaivirāviṇaḥ 
bumbāpātaiḥ sanirghātair uditārtasvarairapi  RKV 
vyāptam āsīt tadā viśvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram

jātaiścaṭacaṭāśabdaiḥ patadbhirgirisānubhiḥ 
tatra raudrotsave jātā rudrānandavivardhinī  RKV 
vihiṃsamānā bhūtāni carvamāṇācarānapi 
tattadgandham upādāya śivārāvavirāviṇī  RKV 
galacchoṇitadhārābhimukhā digdhakalevarā 
caṇḍaśīlābhavaccaṇḍī jagatsaṃhārakarmaṇi  RKV 
ye 'pi prāptā maharlokaṃ bhṛgvādyāśca maharṣayaḥ 
te 'pi naśyanti śataśo brahmakṣattraviśādayaḥ  RKV 
devāsurā bhayatrastāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ 
viśanti ke'pi pātālaṃ līyante ca guhādiṣu  RKV

yugakṣayakare kāle devena viniyojitā  RKV 
ekāpi navadhā jātā daśadhā daśadhā tathā 
catuḥṣaṣṭisvarūpā ca śatarūpāṭṭahāsinī  RKV 
jajñe sahasrarūpā ca lakṣakoṭitanuḥ śivā 
nānārūpāyudhākārā nānāvādanacāriṇī  RKV 
evaṃrūpā 'bhavaddevī śivasyānujñayā nṛpa 
dikṣu sarvāsu gagane vikaṭāyudhaśīlinaḥ  RKV 
rundhanto naśyamānāṃstāngaṇā māheśvarāḥ sthitāḥ 
vicaranti tayā sārddhaṃ śūlapaṭṭiśapāṇayaḥ  RKV 
tato mātṛgaṇāḥ kecidvināyakagaṇaiḥ saha 
vyavardhanta mahāraudrā jagatsaṃhārakāriṇaḥ  RKV 
tatastasyā vyavardhanta daṃṣṭrāḥ kundendusannibhāḥ 
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi ayutānyarbudāni ca  RKV 
daṃṣṭrāvaliḥ kararuhāḥ krūrāstīkṣṇāśca karkaśāḥ 
viyaddiśo likhantyeva saptadvīpāṃ vasuṃdharām  RKV 
tasyā daṃṣṭrābhisampātaiścūrṇitā vanaparvatāḥ 
śilāsaṃcayasaṃghātā viśīryate sahasraśaḥ  RKV 
himavānhemakūṭaśca niṣadho gandhamādanaḥ 
mālyavāṃścaiva nīlaśca śvetaścaiva mahāgiriḥ  RKV 
merumadhyamilāpīṭhaṃ saptadvīpaṃ ca sārṇavam 
lokālokena sahitaṃ prākampata nṛpottama  RKV 
daṃṣṭrāśanivispṛṣṭāśca viśīryante mahādrumāḥ 
utpātaiśca diśo vyāptā ghorarūpaiḥ samantataḥ  RKV 
tārā grahagaṇāḥ sarve ye ca vaimānikā gaṇāḥ 
śivāsahasrair ākīrṇā mahāmātṛgaṇaistathā  RKV 
sā cacāra jagat kṛtsnaṃ yugānte samupasthite 
bhramadbhiśca bruvadbhiśca krośadbhiśca samantataḥ  RKV 
pramathadbhir jvaladbhiśca raudrairvyāptā diśo daśa

prabhinnagopuradvāraṃ keśaśuṣkāsthisaṃkulam

citādhūmākulaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
hāhākārākulaṃ sarvamahahasvananisvanam  RKV 
jagad etad abhūt sarvamaśaraṇyaṃ nirāśrayam  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca

trailokyasaṃtrāsakarī vidyutsaṃsphoṭahāsinī

tataḥ svasthānamagamadyatra devo maheśvaraḥ 
narmadātīram āśrityāvasanmātṛgaṇaiḥ saha  RKV

taiḥ kaṭairāvṛto yasmāt parvato 'yaṃ nṛpottama

prahvaḥ praṇatabhāvena staumi taṃ nīlalohitam 
tatas tālakasampātair gaṇair mātṛgaṇaiḥ saha  RKV 
saṃpranṛtyati saṃhṛṣṭo mṛtyunā saha śaṅkaraḥ 
khaṭvāṅgairulmukaiścaiva paṭṭiśaiḥ parighais tathā  RKV 
māṃsamedovasāhastā hṛṣṭā nṛtyanti saṃghaśaḥ

mahāśiśnodarabhujā nṛtyanti ca hasanti ca

amaraṃ kaṇṭakaṃ cakruḥ prāpte kālaviparyaye

mṛtyuṃ paśyāmi nṛtyantaṃ taḍitpiṅgalamūrddhajam 
tasya pārśve sthitāṃ devīṃ vimalāmbarabhūṣitām  RKV 
kuṇḍalodghuṣṭagaṇḍāṃ tāṃ nāgayajñopavītinīm 
vicitrairupahāraiśca pūjayantīṃ maheśvaram  RKV 
apaśyaṃ narmadāṃ tatra mātaraṃ viśvavanditām

rudravaktrātsamudbhūtaḥ saṃvarto nāma viśrutaḥ 
vāyuḥ saṃśoṣayāmāsa vitatan saptasāgarān  RKV 
uddhūlitāṅgaḥ kapilākṣamūrddhajo jaṭākalāpair avabaddhamūrddhajaḥ 
mahāravo dīptaviśālaśūladhṛksa pātu yuṣmāṃśca dine dine haraḥ  RKV 
śūlī dhanuṣmānkavacī kirīṭī śmaśānabhasmokṣitasarvagātraḥ 
kapālamālākulakaṇṭhanālo mahāhisūtrairavabaddhamauliḥ  RKV 
sa gonasaughaiḥ pariveṣṭitāṅgo viṣāgnicandrāmarasindhumauliḥ 
pinākakhaṇṭūvāṅgakarālapāṇiḥ sa kṛttivāsā ḍamarupraṇādaḥ  RKV 
sa saptalokāntaraniḥsṛtātmā mahabhujāveṣṭitasarvagātraḥ 
netreṇa sūryodayasannibhena pravālakāṅkūranibhodareṇa  RKV 
sandhyābhraraktotpalapadmarāgasindūravidyutprakarāruṇena 
tatena liṅgena ca locanena cikrīḍamānaḥ sa yugāntakāle  RKV 
hiraṇmayenaiva samutsṛjan sa daṇḍena yadvad bhagavān sameruḥ 
pādāgravikṣepaviśīrṇaśailaḥ kurvañjagat so 'pi jagāma tatra  RKV 
saṃhartukāmastridivaṃ tvaśeṣaṃ pramuñcamāno vikṛtāṭṭahāsam 
jahāra sarvaṃ tridivaṃ mahātmā saṃkṣobhayanvai jagadīśa ekaḥ  RKV 
taṃ devamīśānamajaṃ vareṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā jagatsaṃharaṇaṃ maheśam 
sā kālarātriḥ saha mātṛbhiśca gaṇāśca sarve śivamarcayanti  RKV 
nandī ca bhṛṅgī ca gaṇādayaśca taṃ sarvabhūtaṃ praṇamanti devam 
jāgadvaraṃ sarvajanasya kāraṇaṃ haraṃ smarārātim aharniśaṃ te  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye sṛṣṭisaṃharaṇasaṃrambhavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcadaśo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
samātṛbhirbhūtagaṇaśca ghorairvṛtaḥ samantātsa nanarta śūlī 
gajendracarmāvaraṇe vasānaḥ saṃhartukāmaśca jagatsamastam  RKV 
maheśvaraḥ sarvasureśvarāṇāṃ mantrair anekekhabaddhamālī 
medovasāraktavicarcitāṅgastrailokyadāhe praṇanarta śambhuḥ  RKV 
sa kālarātryā sahito mahātmā kāle trilokīṃ sakalāṃ jahāra 
saṃvartakākhyaḥ sahabhānubhāvaḥ śambhurmahātmā jagato variṣṭhaḥ  RKV 
sa visphuliṅgotkaradhūmamiśraṃ maholkavajrāśanivātatulyam 
tato 'ṭṭahāsaṃ pramumoca ghoraṃ vivṛtya vaktraṃ vaḍavāmukhābham  RKV 
sahasravajrāśanisaṃnibhena tenāṭṭahāsena harodgatena 
āpūritāstatra diśo daśaiva saṃkṣobhitāḥ sarvamahārṇavāśca  RKV 
sa brahmalokaṃ prajagāma śabdo brahmāṇḍabhāṇḍaṃ pracacāla sarvam 
kimetadityākulacetanāste vitrastarūpā ṛṣayo babhūvuḥ  RKV 
praṇamya sarve sahasaiva bhītā brahmāṇamūcuḥ parameśvareśam 
bhītāśca sarve ṛṣayastataste surāsuraiścaiva mahoragaiśca  RKV 
vidyutprabhābhāsurabhīṣaṇāṅgaḥ ka eṣa cikrīḍati bhūtalasthaḥ 
kālānalaṃ gātramidaṃ dadhāno yasyāṭṭahāsena jagadvimūḍham  RKV 
vitrastarūpaṃ prababhau kṣaṇena saṃhartumicchetkimayaṃ trilokīm 
sārdhaṃ tvayā saptabhirarṇakaiśca janastapaḥ satyamabhiprayāti  RKV 
saṃhartukāmo hi ka eṣa deva etatsamastaṃ kathayāprameya 
na dṛṣṭametad viṣamaṃ kadāpi jānāsi tattvaṃ paramo mato naḥ  RKV 
niśamya tadvākyamathābabhāṣe brahmā samāśvāsya surādisaṅghān  RKV 
śrībrahmovāca
sa eṣa kālastridivaṃ tvaśeṣaṃ saṃhartukāmo jagadakṣayātmā 
pūrṇe ca śete parivatsarāṇāṃ bhaviṣyatīśānavibhurna citram  RKV 
saṃvatsaro 'yaṃ parivatsaraśca udvatsaro vatsara eṣa devaḥ 
dṛṣṭo 'pyadṛṣṭaḥ prahutaḥ prakāśī sthūlaśca sūkṣmaḥ paramāṇureṣaḥ  RKV 
nātaḥ paraṃ kiṃcidihāsti loke parāparo 'yaṃ prabhurātmavādī 
tuṣyeta me kālasamānarūpa ityevamuktvā bhagavānsureśaḥ  RKV 
sanatkumārapramukhaiḥ sametaḥ saṃtoṣayāmāsa tato yatātmā  RKV 
brahmovāca
namo 'stu sarvāya suśāntamūrtāye hyaghorarūpāya namonamaste 
sarvātmane sarva namonamaste mahātmane bhūtapate namaste  RKV 
oṅkāra huṅkārapariṣkṛtāya svadhāvaṣaṭkāra namonamaste 
guṇatrayeśāya maheśvarāya te trayīmayāya triguṇātmane namaḥ  RKV 
tvaṃ śaṅkaratvaṃ hi maheśvaro 'si pradhānamagryaṃ tvamasi praviṣṭaḥ 
tvaṃ viṣṇurīśaḥ prapitāmahaśca tvaṃ saptajihvastvamanantajihvaḥ  RKV 
sraṣṭāsi sṛṣṭiśca vibho tvameva viśvasya vedyaṃ ca paraṃ nidhānam 
āhurdvijā vedavido vareṇyaṃ parātparastvaṃ parataḥ paro 'si  RKV 
sūkṣmātisūkṣmaṃ pravadanti yacca vāco nivartanti mano yataśca  RKV 
śrīmahādeva uvāca
tvayā stuto'haṃ vividhaiśca mantraiḥ puṣṇāmi śāntiṃ tava padmayone 
īkṣasva māṃ lokamimaṃ jvalantaṃ vaktrairanekaiḥ prasabhaṃ harantam  RKV 
evamuktvā sa deveśo devyā saha jagatpatiḥ 
pitāmahaṃ samāśvāsya tatraivāntaradhīyata  RKV 
idaṃ mahatpuṇyatamaṃ variṣṭhaṃ stotraṃ niśamyeha gatiṃ labhante 
pāpairanekaiḥ pariveṣṭitā ye prayānti rudraṃ vimalairvimānaiḥ  RKV 
bhayaṃ ca teṣāṃ na bhavetkadācitpaṭhanti ye tāta idaṃ dvijāgryāḥ 
saṅgrāmacaurāgnivane tathābdhau teṣāṃ śivastrāti na saṃśayo 'tra  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye brahmakṛtaśivastutivarṇanaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśo

varjayitvā mahāpuṇyāṃ narmadāṃ nṛpasattama  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śrīnarmadāmāhātmye dvādaśādityarūpeṇa jagatsaṃharaṇavarṇanaṃ

 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
