siddhiṃ kīrtiṃ ratiṃ brāhmīṃ kālarātrimayonijām 
tām evāhaṃ tadātyantamīśvarāntikamāsthitām  RKV 
adrākṣaṃ candravadanāṃ dhṛtiṃ sarveśvarīmumām  RKV 
śāntaṃ prasuptaṃ navahemavarṇamumāsahāyaṃ bhagavantamīśam 
tamovṛtaṃ puṇyatamaṃ vīraṣṭhaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya namaskaromi  RKV 
tataḥ prasuptaḥ sahasā vibuddho rātrikṣaye devavaraḥ svabhāvāt 
vikṣobhayan bāhubhir arṇavāmbho jagatpraṇaṣṭaṃ salile vimṛśya  RKV 
kiṃ kāryamityeva vicintayitvā vārāharūpo 'bhavadadbhutāṅgaḥ 
mahāghanāmbhodharatulyavarcāḥ pralambamālāmbaraniṣkamālī  RKV 
saśaṅkhacakrāsidharaḥ kirīṭī savedavedāṅgamayo mahātmā 
trailokyanirmāṇakaraḥ purāṇo devatrayīrūpadharaśca kārye  RKV 
sa eva rudraḥ sa jagajjahāra sṛṣṭyarthamīśaḥ prapitāmaho 'bhūt 
saṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ jagataḥ sa eva hariḥ sucakrāsigadābjapāṇiḥ  RKV 
teṣāṃ vibhāgo na hi kartumarho mahātmanām ekaśarīrabhājām 
mīmāṃsāhetvarthaviśeṣatarkair yasteṣu kuryāt pravibhedam ajñaḥ  RKV 
sa yāti ghoraṃ narakaṃ krameṇa vibhāgakṛddveṣamatirdurātmā 
yā yasya bhaktiḥ sa tayaiva nūnaṃ dehaṃ tyajan svaṃ hyamṛtatvameti  RKV 
saṃmohayan mūrtibhir atra lokaṃ sraṣṭā ca goptā kṣayakṛtsa devaḥ 
tasmān na mohātmakamāviśeta dveṣaṃ na kuryāt pravibhinnamūrtiḥ  RKV 
vārāhamīśānavaro 'pyato 'sau rūpaṃ samāsthāya jagadvidhātā 
naṣṭe triloke 'rṇavatoyamagne vimārgitoyaughamaye 'ntarātmā  RKV 
bhittvārṇavaṃ toyamathāntarasthaṃ viveśa pātālatalaṃ kṣaṇena 
jale nimagnāṃ dharaṇīṃ samastāṃ samaspṛśatpaṅkajapatranetrām  RKV 
viśīrṇaśailopalaśṛṅgakūṭāṃ vasuṃdharāṃ tāṃ pralaye pralīnām 
daṃṣṭraikayā viṣṇuratulyasāhasaḥ samuddadhāra svayameva devaḥ  RKV 
sā tasya daṃṣṭrāgravilambitāṅgī kailāsaśṛṅgāgragateva jyotsnā 
vibhrājate sāpyasamānamūrtiḥ śaśāṅkaśṛṅge ca taḍidvilagnā  RKV 
tāmujjahārārṇavatoyamagnāṃ karī nimagnāmiva hastinīṃ haṭhāt 
nāvaṃ viśīrṇāmiva toyamadhyād udīrṇasattvo 'nupamaprabhāvaḥ  RKV 
sa tāṃ samuttārya mahājalaughāt samudramāryo vyabhajatsamastam 
mahārṇaveṣveva mahārṇavāmbho nikṣepayāmāsa punarnadīṣu  RKV 
śīrṇāṃśca śailānsa cakāra bhūyo dvīpānsamastāṃśca tathārṇavāṃśca 
śailopalairye vicitāḥ samantācchiloccayāṃstānsa cakāra kalpe  RKV 
anekarūpaṃ pravibhajya dehaṃ cakāra devendragaṇānsamastān 
mukhācca vahnirmanasaśca candraścakṣośca sūryaḥ sahasā babhūva  RKV 
jajñe 'tha tasyeśvarayogamūrteḥ pradhyāyamānasya surendrasaṅghaḥ 
vedāśca yajñāśca tathaiva varṇās tathā hi sarvauṣadhayo rasāśca  RKV 
jagatsamastaṃ manasā babhūva yatsthāvaraṃ kiṃcidihāṇḍajaṃ vā 
jarāyujaṃ svedajam udbhijjaṃ vā yat kiṃcid ā kīṭapipīlakādyam  RKV 
tato vijajñe manasā kṣaṇena anekarūpāḥ sahasā maheśā 
cakāra yanmūrtibhir avyayātmā aṣṭābhir āviśya punaḥ sa tatra  RKV 
līlāṃ cakārātha samṛddhatejā ato 'tra me paśyata eva viprāḥ 
teṣāṃ mayā darśanameva sarvaṃ yāvanmuhūrtātsamakāri bhūpa  RKV 
kṛtvā tvaśeṣaṃ kila līlayaiva sa devadevo jagatāṃ vidhātā 
sarvatradṛksarvaga eva devo jagāma cādarśanamādikartā  RKV 
yattanmuhūrtādiha nāmarūpaṃ tāvat prapaśyāmi jagattathaiva 
dvīpaiḥ samudrair abhisaṃvṛtaṃ hi nakṣatratārādivimānakīrṇam  RKV 
viyatpayodagrahacakracitraṃ nānāvidhaiḥ prāṇigaṇair vṛtaṃ ca 
tāṃ vai na paśyāmi mahānubhāvāṃ gorūpiṇīṃ sarvasureśvarīṃ ca  RKV 
kva sāṃprataṃ seti vicintya rājanvibhrāntacittastvabhavaṃ tadaiva 
diśo vibhāgānavalokayān ṛte punastāṃ kathamīśvarāṅgīm  RKV 
paśyāmi tāmatra punaśca śubhrāṃ mahābhranīlāṃ śuciśubhratoyām 
vṛkṣairanekairupaśobhitāṅgīṃ gajaisturaṅgairvihagairvṛtāṃ ca  RKV 
yathā purātīramupetya devyāḥ samāsthitaścāpyamarakaṇṭake tu 
tathaiva paśyāmi sukhopaviṣṭa ātmānam avyagramavāptasaukhyam  RKV 
tathaiva puṇyā malatoyavāhāṃ dṛṣṭvā punaḥ kalpaparikṣaye 'pi 
ambām ivāryām anukampamānām akṣīṇatoyāṃ virujāṃ viśokaḥ  RKV 
evaṃ mahatpuṇyatamaṃ ca kalpaṃ paṭhanti śṛṇvanti ca ye dvijendrāḥ 
mahāvarāhasya maheśvarasya dine dine te vimalā bhavanti  RKV 
aśubhaśatasahasraṃ te vidhūya prapannāstridivamamarajuṣṭaṃ siddhagandharvayuktam 
vimalaśaśinibhābhiḥ sarva evāpsarobhiḥ saha vividhavilāsaiḥ svargasaukhyaṃ labhante  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śrīnarmadāmāhātmye vārāhakalpavṛttāntavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutā me vividhā dharmāḥ saṃhārāstvatprasādataḥ 
kṛtā devena sarveṇa ye ca dṛṣṭāstvayānagha  RKV 
sāmprataṃ śrotumicchāmi prabhāvaṃ śārṅgadhanvanaḥ 
tvayānubhūtaṃ viprendra tanme tvaṃ vaktumarhasi  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi prajāsaṃhāralakṣaṇam 
yaccihnaṃ dṛśyate tatra yathā kalpo vidhīyate  RKV 
ulkāpātāḥ sanirghātā bhūmikampastathaiva ca 
patate pāṃśuvarṣaṃ ca nirghoṣaścaiva dāruṇaḥ  RKV 
yakṣakinnaragandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ 
sarve te pralayaṃ yānti yugānte samupasthite  RKV 
parvatāḥ sāgarā nadyaḥ sarāṃsi vividhāni ca 
vṛkṣāḥ śeṣaṃ samāyānti vallījātaṃ tṛṇāni ca  RKV 
evaṃ hi vyākulībhūte sarvauṣadhijalojjhite 
kāṣṭhabhūte tu saṃjāte trailokye sacarācare  RKV 
yāvatpaśyāmi madhyāhne snānakāla upasthite 
trailokyaṃ jvalanākāraṃ durnirīkṣaṃ durāsadam  RKV 
dvau sūryau pūrvatastāta paścimottarayostathā 
tathaiva dakṣiṇe dvau ca sūryau dṛṣṭau pratāpinau  RKV 
dvau sūryau nāgalokasthau madhye dvau gaganasya ca 
ityete dvādaśādityāstapante sarvato diśam  RKV 
pṛthivīmadahansarvāṃ saśailavanakānanām 
nādagdhaṃ dṛśyate kiṃcidṛte revāṃ ca māṃ tathā  RKV 
pṛthivyāṃ dahyamānāyāṃ havirgandhaśca jāyate 
tato me śuṣyate gātraṃ tṛṣāpyevaṃ durāsadā  RKV 
na hi vindāmi pānīyaṃ śoṣitaṃ ca divākaraiḥ 
yāvatkamaṇḍaluṃ vīkṣe śuṣkaṃ tatrāpi tajjalam  RKV 
tato 'haṃ śokasaṃtapto viśeṣātkṣuttṛṣārditaḥ 
utpapāta kṣiterūrdhvaṃ paśyamāno divaṃ prati  RKV 
tāvatpaśyāmi gagane gṛhaṃ śṛṅgārabhūṣitam 
tatastajjñātukāmo 'haṃ prasthito rājasattama  RKV 
prākāreṇa vicitreṇa kapāṭārgalabhūṣitam 
vicitraśikharopetaṃ dvāradeśamupāgataḥ  RKV 
ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ samucchraye 
tadardhaṃ tu pṛthaktvena kāñcanaṃ ratnabhūṣitam  RKV 
tatra madhye parāṃ śayyāṃ paśyāmi nṛpasattama 
śayyopari śayānaṃ tu puruṣaṃ divyamūrdhajam  RKV 
vikuñcitāgrakeśāntaṃ samastaṃ yojanāyatam 
mukuṭena vicitreṇa dīptikāntena śobhitam  RKV 
śyāmaṃ kamalapatrābhaṃ suprabhaṃ ca sunāsikam 
siṃhāsyamāyatabhujaṃ gallaśmaśruvarāṅkitam  RKV 
trivalībhaṅgasubhagaṃ karṇakuṇḍalabhūṣitam 
viśālābhaṃ supīnāṅgaṃ pārśvasvāvartabhūṣitam  RKV 
śobhitaṃ kaṭibhāgena vibhaktaṃ jānujaṅghayoḥ 
padmāṅkitatalaṃ devam ātāmrasunakhāṅgulim  RKV 
meghanādasugambhīraṃ sarvāvayavasundaram 
śayyāmadhyagataṃ devamapaśyaṃ puruṣottamam  RKV 
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ śayānaṃ dakṣiṇena tu 
akṣasūtrodyatakaraṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham  RKV 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhaktimāndevaṃ stotukāmo vyavasthitaḥ 
jayeśa jaya vāgīśa jaya divyāṅgabhūṣaṇa  RKV 
jaya devapate śrīmansākṣādbrahma sanātana 
tava lokāḥ śarīrasthāstvaṃ gatiḥ parameśvara  RKV 
tvadādhārā hi deveśa sarve lokā vyavasthitāḥ 
tvaṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvasattvānāṃ tvaṃ kartā dharaṇīdharaḥ  RKV 
tvaṃ hautram agnihotrāṇāṃ sūtramantrastvameva ca 
gokarṇaṃ bhadrakarṇaṃ ca tvaṃ ca māheśvaraṃ padam  RKV 
tvaṃ kīrtiḥ sarvakīrtīnāṃ dainyapāpapraṇāśinī 
tvaṃ naimiṣaṃ kurukṣetraṃ tvaṃ ca viṣṇupadaṃ param  RKV 
tvayā tu līlayā deva padākrāntā ca medinī 
tvayā baddho balirdeva tvayendrasya padaṃ kṛtam  RKV 
tvaṃ kalirdvāparaṃ deva tretā kṛtayugaṃ tathā 
pralambadamanaśca tvaṃ sraṣṭā tvaṃ ca vināśakṛt  RKV 
tvayā vai dhāryate lokāstvaṃ kālaḥ sarvasaṃkṣayaḥ 
tvayā hi deva sṛṣṭāstāḥ sarvā vai devayonayaḥ  RKV 
tvaṃ panthāḥ sarvalokānāṃ tvaṃ ca mokṣaḥ parā gatiḥ 
brahmā tvadudbhavo devo rajorūpaḥ sanātanaḥ 
rudraḥ krodhodbhavo 'pyevaṃ tvaṃ ca sattve vyavasthitaḥ  RKV 
etaccarācaraṃ deva krīḍanārthaṃ tvayā kṛtam 
evaṃ saṃtaptadehena stuto devo mayā prabhuḥ  RKV 
bhaktyā paramayā rājansarvabhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ 
stuvanvai tatra paśyāmi vāripūrṇāṃstato ghaṭān  RKV 
tato mayā vismṛtā yā tṛṣā sā vardhitā punaḥ 
upāsarpaṃ tatastasya pārśvaṃ vai puruṣasya hi  RKV 
pānīyaṃ pātukāmena cintitaṃ ca mayā punaḥ 
nāpaśyata hi māṃ caiṣa supto 'pi na ca budhyate  RKV 
yastu pāpena saṃmūḍhaḥ sukhaṃ suptaṃ prabodhayet 
jāyate tasya pāpasya brahmahatyāphalaṃ mahat  RKV 
evaṃ saṃcintyamāne tu dvitīyo hyāgataḥ pumān 
nekṣate jalpate kiṃcidvāmaskandhe mṛgājinī  RKV 
jaṭī kamaṇḍaludharo daṇḍī mekhalayā vṛtaḥ 
bhasmonmṛditasarvāṅgo mahātejāstrilocanaḥ  RKV 
yāvat taṃ stotukāmo 'ham apaśyaṃ svacchacakṣuṣā 
tāvat sarvāṅgasambhūtyāmahatyā rūpasampadā  RKV 
apaśyaṃ saṃvṛtāṃ nārīṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām 
dṛṣṭvā tāṃ patito bhūmau jayasveti bruvaṃstataḥ  RKV 
jaya rudrāṅgasambhūte jayavāhini sanātani 
jaya kaumāri māhendri vaiṣṇavī vāruṇī tathā  RKV 
jaya kauberi sāvitri jaya dhātri varānane 
tṛṣṇayā taptade hasya rakṣāṃ kuru carācare  RKV 
śrīdevyuvāca
prasannā vipraśārdūla tava vākyaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ 
vartate mānase yatte mayā jñātaṃ dvijottama  RKV 
śṛṇu vipra mamāpyasti vratametatsudāruṇam 
strīlaghutvānmayārabdhaṃ duṣkaraṃ mandamedhayā  RKV 
yadi bhāvī ca me putro dharmiṣṭho lokaviśrutaḥ 
viprasya tu stanaṃ dattvā paścāddāsyāmi bālake  RKV 
sa me putraḥ samutpanno yathokto me mahāmune 
stanaṃ piba tvaṃ viprendra yadi jīvitumicchasi  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
akāryametadviprāṇāṃ yastvimaṃ pibate stanam 
punaścaivopanayanaṃ vratasiddhiṃ na gacchati  RKV 
brāhmaṇatvaṃ tribhirlokairdurlabhaṃ padmalocane 
saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛto vipro yaiśca jāyeta tacchṛṇu  RKV 
prathamaṃ caiva nārīṣu saṃskārair bījavāpatam 
bījaprakṣepaṇādeva bījakṣepaḥ sa ucyate  RKV 
tadante ca mahābhāge garbhādhānaṃ dvitīyakam 
puṃsavanaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu sīmantaṃ ca caturthakam  RKV 
pañcamaṃ jātakarma syānnāma vai ṣaṣṭhamucyate 
niṣkrāmaḥ saptamaścaiva hyannaprāśanamaṣṭamam  RKV 
navamaṃ vai cūḍakarma daśamaṃ mauñjibandhanam 
aiṣikaṃ dārvikaṃ caiva saumikaṃ bhaumikaṃ tathā  RKV 
patnīsaṃyojanaṃ cānyaddaivakarma tataḥ param 
mānuṣyaṃ pitṛkarma syāddaśamāṣṭāsu śobhane  RKV 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ tatheṣṭaṃ ca pārvaṇaṃ ca tataḥ param  RKV 
śrāddhaṃ śrāvaṇyāmāgrayaṇaṃ ca caitrāśvayujyāṃ daśapaurṇamāsyām 
nirūḍhapaśusavanasautrāmaṇyagniṣṭomātyagniṣṭomāḥ  RKV 
ṣoḍaṣīvājapeyātirātrāptoryāmodaśavājapeyāḥ 
sarvabhūteṣu kṣāntiranasūyā śaucamaṅgalam akārpaṇyam aspṛheti  RKV 
ebhir aṣṭacatvāriṃśadbhiḥ saṃskāraiḥ saṃkṛto brāhmaṇo bhavati  RKV 
evaṃ jñātvā mahābhāge na tu māṃ pātumarhasi 
śiśupeyaṃ stanaṃ bhadre kathaṃ vai madvidhaḥ pibet  RKV 
mamaitadvacanaṃ śrutvā nārī vacanamabravīt  RKV 
yadi tvaṃ na pibeḥ stanyaṃ payo bālo mariṣyati 
śrūyate triṣu lokeṣu vedeṣu ca smṛtiṣvapi 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo bhrūṇahatyā na muñcati  RKV 
bhavitrī tava hatyā ca mahābhāgavataḥ punaḥ 
janmāni ca śatānyaṣṭau kliśyate bhrūṇahatyayā  RKV 
mṛtaḥ śunatvaṃ cāpnoti varṣāṇāṃ tu śatatrayam 
tatastasya kṣaye jāte kākayoniṃ vrajetpunaḥ  RKV 
tatrāpi ca śatānyaṣṭau kliśyate pāpakarmaṇi 
varāho daśa janmāni tadante jāyate kṛmiḥ  RKV 
tataścārohiṇīṃ prāpya gogajāśvanṛjanmabhāk 
śrūyate śrutiśāstreṣu vedeṣu ca paraṃtapa  RKV 
sarvapāpādhikaṃ pāpaṃ bālahatyā dvijottama 
bālahatyāyuto vipraḥ pacyate narake dhruvam  RKV 
varṣāṇi ca śatānyaṣṭau prāpnoti yamayātanām 
tasmādalpataro doṣaḥ pibato me stanaṃ tava  RKV 
tathaivāpibataḥ pāpaṃ jāyate bahuvarṣikam 
kṣudhātṛṣāvirāmaste puṇyaṃ ca pibataḥ stanam  RKV 
ato na cetaḥ saṃdigdhaṃ kartavyamiha karhicit 
ehi vipra yathākāmaṃ bālārthe piba me stanam  RKV 
tato 'haṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā stanaṃ pātuṃ samudyataḥ 
na ca tṛptiṃ vijānāmi pibataḥ stanamuttamam  RKV 
triṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi bhārataivaṃ śatāni ca 
tataḥ prabuddhotsaṅge 'haṃ māyānidrāvimohitaḥ  RKV 
nidrāvigatamoho 'haṃ yāvatpaśyāmi pāṇḍava 
tāvatsuptaṃ na paśyāmi na ca taṃ bālakaṃ vibho  RKV 
caturastāṃśca vai kumbhān paśyāmi tatra bhārata 
na ca paśyāmi tāṃ devīṃ gatā vai kutracicca te  RKV 
evaṃ vimṛśyamānasya cintayānasya tiṣṭhataḥ 
īṣaddhasitayā vācā devī vacanamabravīt  RKV 
śrīdevyuvāca
kṛṣṇaḥ sa puruṣaḥ supto dvitīyo 'pyāgato haraḥ 
ye catvāraśca te kumbhāḥ samudrāste dvijottama  RKV 
yaśca bālastvayā dṛṣṭo brāhmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
ahaṃ ca pṛthivī jñeyā saptadvīpā sarvatā  RKV 
yā gatā tvāṃ parityajya bhūtale supratiṣṭhitā 
imāṃ ca prekṣase vipra narmadāṃ saritāṃ varām  RKV 
sarvasattvopakārāya bṛhate puṇyalakṣaṇā 
revānadī tu vikhyātā na mṛtā tena narmadā  RKV 
evaṃ jñātvā śamaṃ gaccha svastho bhava mahāmune 
ityuktvā māṃ tadā devī tatraivāntaradhīyata  RKV 
evaṃ hi śete bhagavānsattvasthaḥ pralaye sadā 
sattvarūpo mahādevo yadādhāre jagatsthitam  RKV 
evaṃ mayānubhūtaṃ tu dṛṣṭamāścaryamuttamam 
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ kathitaṃ te narottama  RKV 
viṣṇoścaritamityuktaṃ yattvayā paripṛcchitam 
bhūya eva mahābāho kimanyacchrotumicchasi  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe vārāhakalpavṛttāntavarṇanaṃ nāma viṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutaṃ me vividhāścaryaṃ tvatprasādāddvijottama 
bhūyaśca śrotumicchāmi tanme kathaya suvrata  RKV 
kathameṣā nadī puṇyā sarvanadīṣu cottamā 
narmadā nāma vikhyātā bhūyo me kathayānagha  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā sarvapāpapraṇāśinī 
tārayetsarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca  RKV 
narmadāyāstu māhātmyaṃ yatpūrveṇa mayā śrutam 
tatte 'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanā nṛpa  RKV 
gaṅgā kanakhale puṇyā kurukṣetre sarasvatī 
grāme vā yadi vāraṇye puṇyā sarvatra narmadā  RKV 
tribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ saptāhena tu yāmunam 
sadyaḥ punāti gāṅgeyaṃ darśanādeva nārmadam  RKV 
kaliṅgadeśāt paścārdhe parvate 'marakaṇṭake 
puṇyā ca triṣu lokeṣu ramaṇīyā pade pade  RKV 
tatra devāśca gandharvā ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ 
tapastaptvā mahārāja siddhiṃ paramikāṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
tatra snātvā naro rājanniyamastho jitendriyaḥ 
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ kulānāṃ tārayecchatam  RKV 
siddhikṣetraṃ paraṃ tāta parvato hyamaraṃkaṭaḥ 
sarvadevāśrito yasmādṛṣibhiḥ parisevitaḥ  RKV 
siddhavidyādharā bhūtagandharvāḥ sthānamuttamam 
dṛśyādṛśyāśca rājendra sevante siddhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ  RKV 
ahaṃ ca paramaṃ sthānaṃ tataḥ prabhṛti saṃśritaḥ 
atra praṇavarūpo vai sthāne tiṣṭhatyumāpatiḥ  RKV 
śrīkaṇṭhaḥ sagaṇaḥ sarvabhūtasaṅghairniṣevitaḥ 
asmādgirivarādbhūpa vakṣye tīrthasya vistaram  RKV 
yāni santīha tīrthāni puṇyāni nṛpasattama 
yāni yānīha tīrthāni narmadāyāstaṭadvaye  RKV 
na teṣāṃ vistaraṃ vaktuṃ śakto brahmāpi bhūpate 
yojanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ śrūyate sariduttamā  RKV 
vistareṇa tu rājendra ardhayojanamāyatā 
ṣaṣṭitīrthasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭyastathaiva ca  RKV 
parvatād udadhiṃ yāvad ubhe kūle na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
saptaṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi saptaṣaṣṭiśatāni ca 
saptaṣaṣṭistathā koṭyo vāyus tīrthāni cābravīt  RKV 
paraṃ kṛtayuge tāni yānti pratyakṣatāṃ nṛpa 
paśyanti mānavāḥ sarve satataṃ dharmabuddhayaḥ  RKV 
yathāyathā kalirghoro vartate dāruṇo nṛpa 
tathātathālpatāṃ yānti hīnasattvā yato narāḥ  RKV 
jāleśvarāditīrthāni parvate 'sminnarādhipa 
pitṛtṛptipradānyāhuḥ svargamokṣapradāni ca  RKV 
śreṣṭhaṃ dāruvanaṃ tatra carukāsaṃgamaḥ śubhaḥ 
uttare narmadāyāstu carukeśvaram uttamam  RKV 
dārukeśvaratīrthaṃ ca vyatīpāteśvaraṃ tathā 
pātāleśvaratīrthaṃ ca koṭiyajñaṃ tathaiva ca  RKV 
iti caivottare kūle revāyā nṛpasattama 
amareśvarapārśve ca liṅgānyaṣṭottaraṃ śatam  RKV 
varuṇeśvaramukhyāni sarvapāpaharāṇi ca  RKV 
māndhātṛpurapārśve ca siddheśvarayameśvarau 
oṅkārātpūrvabhāge ca kedāraṃ tīrthamuttamam  RKV 
tatsamīpe mahārāja svargadvāramaghāpaham 
nāmnā brahmeśvaraṃ puṇyaṃ saptasārasvataṃ puraḥ  RKV 
rudrāṣṭakaṃ ca sāvitraṃ somatīrthaṃ tathaiva ca 
etāni dakṣiṇe tīre revāyā bharatarṣabha  RKV 
asmiṃstu parvate tāta rudrāṇāṃ koṭayaḥ sthitāḥ 
snānaistuṣṭirbhavetteṣāṃ gandhamālyānulepanaiḥ  RKV 
prītāste 'pi bhavantyatra rudrā rājan na saṃśayaḥ 
japena pāpasaṃśuddhirdhyānenānantyam aśnute  RKV 
dānena bhogānāpnoti ityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt 
parvatāt paścime deśe svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ 
sthitaḥ praṇavarūpo 'sau jagadādiḥ sanātanaḥ  RKV 
tatra snātvā śucirbhūtvā brahmacārī jitendriyaḥ 
pitṛkāryaṃ prakurvīta vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā  RKV 
tilodakena tatraiva tarpayetpitṛdevatāḥ 
ā saptamaṃ kulaṃ tasya svarge modati pāṇḍava  RKV 
ātmanā saha bhogāṃśca vividhān labhate sukhī 
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi krīḍate surapūjitaḥ  RKV 
modate suciraṃ kālaṃ pitṛpūjāphaladhitaḥ 
tataḥ svargātparibhraṣṭo jāyate vimale kule  RKV 
dhanavāndānaśīlaśca nīrogo lokapūjitaḥ 
punaḥ smarati tattīrthaṃ gamanaṃ kurute punaḥ  RKV 
dvitīye janmani bhaveddhradasyānucarotkaṭaḥ 
tathaiva brahmacaryeṇa sopavāso jitendriyaḥ  RKV 
sarvahiṃsānivṛttastu labhate phalamuttamam 
evaṃ dharmasamācāro yastu prāṇānparityajet  RKV 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yadvai tannibodha narādhipa 
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇi svarge modati pāṇḍava  RKV 
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇe divyaśabdānunādite 
divyagandhānuliptāṅgo divyālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ  RKV 
krīḍate daivataiḥ sārddhaṃ siddhagandharvasaṃstutaḥ 
tataḥ svargātparibhraṣṭo rājā bhavati vīryavān  RKV 
hastyaśvarathayānaiśca dharmajñaḥ śāstratatparaḥ 
gṛhe stambhaśatākīrṇe sauvarṇe rajatānvite  RKV

mattamātaṅganiḥśvāsairvājiheṣitanāditaiḥ  RKV

rājarājeśvaraḥ śrīmānsarvastrījanavallabhaḥ  RKV 
tasmingṛhe vasitvā tu krīḍābhogasamanvitaḥ 
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ  RKV 
evaṃ teṣāṃ bhavetsarvaṃ ye mṛtā hyamareśvare 
agnipraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryād bhaktyā hyamarakaṇṭake  RKV 
sa mṛtaḥ svargamāpnoti yāsyate paramāṃ gatim 
snānaṃ dānaṃ japo homaḥ śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham  RKV 
purāṇe śrūyate rājansarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet 
tasyāstīre tu ye vṛkṣāḥ patitāḥ kālaparyaye  RKV 
narmadātoyasaṃspṛṣṭāste yānti paramāṃ gatim 
anivṛttikā gatistasya pavanasyāmbare yathā  RKV 
patanaṃ kurute yastu tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa 
kanyāstrīṇi sahasrāṇi pātāle bhogabhāginaḥ  RKV 
tiṣṭhanti bhavane tasya preṣaṇe prārthayanti ca 
divyabhogaiḥ susampannaḥ krīḍate kālam  RKV 
pṛthivyāṃ hy āsamudrāyāṃ tādṛśo naiva jāyate 
yādṛśo 'yaṃ naraśreṣṭha parvato 'marakaṇṭakaḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ parvatasyānu paścime 
hrado jāleśvaro nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ  RKV 
tatra piṇḍapradānena sandhyopāsanakena tu 
pitaro dvādaśābdāni tarpitāstu bhavanti vai  RKV 
dakṣiṇe narmadātīre kapilā tu mahānadī 
saralārjunasaṃchannā khadirairupaśobhitā  RKV 
mādhavīsallakībhiśca vallībhiś cāpyalaṃkṛtā 
śvāpadairgarjamānaiśca gomāyuvānarādibhiḥ  RKV 
pakṣijātiviśeṣaiśca nityaṃ pramuditā nṛpa 
sāgraṃ koṭiśataṃ tatra ṛṣīṇāmiti śuśruma  RKV 
tapastaptvā gataṃ mokṣaṃ yeṣāṃ janma na cāgamaḥ 
yena tatra tapastaptaṃ kapilena mahātmanā  RKV 
tatra taccābhavattīrthaṃ puṇyaṃ siddhaniṣevitam 
yena sā kāpilaistāta sevitā ṛṣibhiḥ purā  RKV 
tena sā kapilā nāma gītā pāpakṣayaṃkarī 
tatra koṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ tīrthānām amareśvare  RKV 
ahorātroṣito bhūtvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ 
dānaṃ ca vidhivad dattvā yathāśaktyā dvijottame  RKV 
īśvarānugrahātsarvaṃ tatra koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet 
yasmādanakṣaraṃ rūpaṃ praṇavasyeha bhārata  RKV 
śivasvarūpasya tataḥ kṛtamātrākṣaraṃ bhavet 
tiryañcaḥ paśavaścaiva vṛkṣā gulmalatādayaḥ  RKV 
te 'pi tatra kṣayaṃ yātāḥ svargaṃ yānti na saṃśayaḥ 
viśalyā tatra yā proktā tatraiva tu mahānadī  RKV 
snātvā dattvā yathānyāyaṃ tatrāpi sukṛtī bhavet 
tatra devagaṇāḥ sarve sakinnaramahoragāḥ  RKV 
yakṣarākṣasagandharvā ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ 
sarve samāgatāstāṃ vai paśyanti hyamareśvare  RKV 
taiśca sarvaiḥ samāgamya vanditau tau śubhau kaṭau 
purā yuge mahāghore sarvalokabhayaṃkare  RKV 
narmadāyāḥ sutastatra saśalyo viśalīkṛtaḥ 
sarvadevaiśca ṛṣibhirviśalyā tena sā smṛtā  RKV

purā dākṣāyaṇī nāma sahitā śūlapāṇinā 
krīḍitvā narmadātoye parayā ca mudā nṛpa  RKV 
jalāduttīrya sahasā vastramanyatsamāharat 
devyāstu snānavastraṃ tatpīḍitaṃ līlayā nṛpa  RKV 
sahitānucarībhistu indrāyudhanibhaṃ bhṛśam

tathā gandharasairyuktaṃ nānāpuṣpaistu vāsitam  RKV

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sā viśalyā hyabhūdyathā 
āścaryabhūtā lokasya sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī  RKV

agniruvāca

īśvara uvāca
etāstu dhiṣṇināmnyo vai bhaviṣyanti saridvarāḥ 
patnyastava viśālākṣyo vede khyātā na saṃśayaḥ  RKV

etāḥ ṣoḍaśā nadyo vai bhāryārthaṃ saṃvyavasthitāḥ

tatkathaṃ tu bhavetpuṇyam ṛṣisiddhaniṣevitam  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
jāleśvarāt paraṃ tīrthaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati 
tasyotpattiṃ kathayataḥ śṛṇu tvaṃ pāṇḍunandana  RKV 
purā ṛṣigaṇāḥ sarve sendrāścaiva marudgaṇāḥ 
tāpitā asuraiḥ sarvaiḥ kṣayaṃ nītā hyanekaśaḥ  RKV 
bāṇāsuraprabhṛtibhirjambhaśumbhapurogamaiḥ 
vadhyamānā hyanekaiśca brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
vimānaiḥ parvatākārair hayaiścaiva gajopamaiḥ 
syandanairnagarākāraiḥ siṃhaśārdūlayojitaiḥ  RKV 
kacchapairmakaraiścānye jagmuranye padātayaḥ 
prāpya te paramaṃ sthānamaśakyaṃ yadadhārmikaiḥ  RKV 
dṛṣṭvā padmodbhavaṃ devaṃ sarvalokasya śaṅkaram 
te sarve tatra gatvā tu stutiṃ cakruḥ samāhitāḥ  RKV 
devā ūcuḥ 
jayāmeya jayābheda jaya sambhūtikāraka 
padmayone suraśreṣṭha tvāṃ vayaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
tacchrutvā tu vaco devo devānāṃ bhāvitātmanām 
meghagambhīrayā vācā pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥ  RKV 
kiṃ vo hyāgamanaṃ devāḥ sarveṣāṃ ca vivarṇatā 
kenāvamānitāḥ sarve śīghraṃ kathayatāmarāḥ  RKV 
devā ūcuḥ 
bāṇo nāma mahāvīryo dānavo baladarpitaḥ 
tenāsmākaṃ hṛtaṃ sarvaṃ dhanaratnairviyojitāḥ  RKV 
devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
cintayāmāsa deveśastasya nāśāya yā kriyā  RKV 
avadhyo dānavaḥ pāpaḥ sarveṣāṃ vai divaukasām 
muktvā tu śaṅkaraṃ devaṃ na mayā na ca viṣṇunā  RKV 
tatraiva sarve gacchāmo yatra devo maheśvaraḥ 
sa gatiścaiva sarveṣāṃ vidyate 'nyo na kaścana  RKV 
evamuktvā suraiḥ sarvairbrahmā vedavidāṃvaraḥ 
brāhmaṇaiḥ saha vidvadbhirato yatra maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
stutibhiśca supuṣṭābhistuṣṭāva parameśvaram  RKV 
devā ūcuḥ 
jaya tvaṃ devadeveśa jayomārdhaśarīradhṛk 
vṛṣāsana mahābāho śaśāṅkakṛtabhūṣaṇa  RKV 
namaḥ śūlāgrahastāya namaḥ khaṭvāṅgadhāriṇe 
jaya bhūtapate deva dakṣayajñavināśana  RKV 
pañcākṣara namo deva pañcabhūtātmavigraha 
pañcavaktramayeśāna vedaistvaṃ tu pragīyase  RKV 
sṛṣṭipālanasaṃhārāṃstvaṃ sadā kuruṣe namaḥ 
aṣṭamūrte smarahara smara satyaṃ yathā stutaḥ  RKV 
pañcātmikā tanurdeva brāhmaṇaiste pragīyate 
sadyo vāme tathāghore īśo tatpuruṣe tathā  RKV 
hemajāle suvistīrṇe haṃsavatkūjase hara 
evaṃ stuto munigaṇairbrahmādyaiśca surāsuraiḥ  RKV 
prahṛṣṭaḥ sumanā bhūtvā surasaṅghānuvāca ha  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
svāgataṃ devaviprāṇāṃ suprabhātādya śarvarī 
kiṃ kurmo vadata kṣipraṃ ko 'nyaḥ sevyaḥ surāsuraiḥ  RKV 
kiṃ duḥkhaṃ ko nu santāpaḥ kuto vo bhayamāgatam 
kathayadhvaṃ mahābhāgāḥ kāraṇaṃ yanmanogatam  RKV 
evamuktāstu rudreṇa pratyavocansurarṣabhāḥ 
svānsvāndehāndarśayanto lajjamānā adhomukhāḥ  RKV 
asti ghoro mahāvīryo dānavo baladarpitaḥ 
bāṇo nāmeti vikhyāto yasya tattripuraṃ mahat  RKV 
tena vai sutapastaptaṃ daśavarṣaśatāni hi 
tasya tuṣṭo 'bhavadbrahmā niyamena damena ca  RKV 
purāṇi tānyabhedyāni dadau kāmagamāni vai 
āyasaṃ rājataṃ caiva sauvarṇaṃ ca tathāparam  RKV 
tripuraṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭaṃ bhramattatkāmagāmi ca 
tasyaiva tu balotkṛṣṭāstripure dānavāḥ sthitāḥ  RKV 
trailokyaṃ sakalaṃ deva pīḍayanti mahāsurāḥ 
daṇḍapāśāsiśastrāṇi avikāre vikurvate 
tripuraṃ dānavairjuṣṭaṃ bhramattaccakrasaṃnibham  RKV 
kvaciddṛśyamadṛśyaṃ vā mṛgatṛṣṇaiva lakṣyate  RKV 
yasminpatati taddivyaṃ dṛptasya tripuraṃ mahat 
na tatra brāhmaṇā devā gāvo naiva tu jantavaḥ  RKV 
na tatra dṛśyate kiṃcitpatedyatra puratrayam 
nadyo grāmāśca deśāśca bahavo bhasmasātkṛtāḥ  RKV 
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ caiva maṇimauktikameva ca 
strīratnaṃ śobhanaṃ yacca tatsarvaṃ karṣate balāt  RKV 
na śastreṇa na cāstreṇa na divā niśi vā hara 
śakyate devasaṅghaiśca nihantuṃ sa kathaṃcana  RKV 
taddahasva mahādeva tvaṃ hi naḥ paramā gatiḥ 
evaṃ prasādaṃ deveśa sarveṣāṃ kartumarhasi  RKV 
yena devāśca gandharvā ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ 
parāṃ dhṛtiṃ samāyānti tatprabho kartumarhasi  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
etatsarvaṃ kariṣyāmi mā viṣādaṃ gamiṣyatha 
acireṇaiva kālena kuryāṃ yuṣmatsukhāvaham  RKV 
āśvāsayitvā tāndevānsarvānindrapurogamān 
cintayāmāsa deveśastripurasya vadhaṃ prati  RKV 
kathaṃ kena prakāreṇa hantavyaṃ tripuraṃ mayā 
tamekaṃ nāradaṃ muktvā nānyopāyo vidhīyate  RKV 
evaṃ saṃstabhya cātmānaṃ tato dhyātaḥ sa nāradaḥ 
tatkṣaṇādeva samprāpto vāyubhūto mahātapāḥ  RKV 
kamaṇḍaludharo devastridaṇḍī jñānakovidaḥ 
yogapaṭṭākṣasūtreṇa chatreṇaiva virājitaḥ  RKV 
jaṭājūṭābaddhaśirā jvalanārkasamaprabhaḥ 
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya daṇḍavatpatito bhuvi  RKV 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā nārado bhagavānmuniḥ 
stotreṇa mahatā śarvaḥ stuto bhaktyā mahāmanāḥ  RKV 
nārada uvāca
jaya śambho virūpākṣa jaya deva trilocana 
jaya śaṅkara īśāna rudreśvara namo 'stu te  RKV 
tvaṃ patistvaṃ jagatkartā tvameva layakṛdvibho 
tvameva jagatāṃ nātho duṣṭātakaniṣūdanaḥ  RKV 
tvaṃ naḥ pāhi sureśāna trayīmūrte sanātana 
bhavamūrte bhavāre tvaṃ bhajatāmabhayo bhava  RKV 
bhavabhāvavināśārthaṃ bhava tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ bhaje 
kimarthaṃ cintito deva ājñā me dīyatāṃ prabho  RKV 
kasya saṃkṣobhaye cittaṃ ko vādya patatu kṣitau 
kamadya kalahenāhaṃ yojaye jayatāṃvara  RKV 
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā devadevo maheśvaraḥ 
utphullanayano bhūtvā idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RKV 
svāgataṃ te muniśreṣṭha sadaiva kalahapriya 
vīṇāvādanatattvajña brahmaputra sanātana  RKV 
gaccha nārada śīghraṃ tvaṃ yatra tattripuraṃ mahat 
bāṇasya dānavendrasya sarvalokabhayāvaham  RKV 
bhartāro devatātulyāḥ striyastatrāpsaraḥsamāḥ 
tāsāṃ vai tejasā caiva bhramate tripuraṃ mahat  RKV 
na śakyate kathaṃ bhettuṃ sarvopāyairdvijottama 
gatvā tvaṃ mohaya kṣipraṃ pṛthagdharmairanekadhā  RKV 
nārada uvāca
tava vākyena deveśa bhedayāmi purottamam 
abhedyaṃ bahudhopāyairyattu devaiḥ savāsavaiḥ  RKV 
evamuktvā gato bhūpa śatayojanamāyatam 
bāṇasya tatpuraśreṣṭham ṛddhivṛddhisamāyutam  RKV 
kṛtakautukasambādhaṃ nānādhātuvicitritam 
anekaharmyasaṃchannam anekāyatanojjvalam  RKV 
dvāratoraṇasaṃyuktaṃ kapāṭārgalabhūṣitam 
bahuyantrasamopetaṃ prākāraparikhojjvalam  RKV 
vāpīkṛpataḍāgaiśca devatāyatanairyutam 
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇaṃ padminīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitam  RKV 
anekavanaśobhāḍhyaṃ nānāvihagamaṇḍitam 
evaṃ guṇagaṇākīrṇaṃ bāṇasya puramuttamam  RKV 
tasya madhye mahākāyaṃ saptakakṣaṃ suśobhitam 
bāṇasya bhavanaṃ divyaṃ sarvaṃ kāñcanabhūṣitam  RKV 
mauktikādāmaśobhāḍhyaṃ vajravaiḍūryabhūṣitam 
rukmapaṭṭatalākīrṇaṃ ratnabhūmyā suśobhitam  RKV 
mattamātaṅganiḥśvāsaiḥ syandanaiḥ saṃkulīkṛtam 
hayaheṣitaśabdaiśca nārīṇāṃ nūpurasvanaiḥ  RKV 
khaḍgatomarahastaiśca vajrāṅkuśaśarāyudhaiḥ 
rakṣitaṃ ghorarūpaiśca dānavairbaladarpitaiḥ  RKV 
evaṃ guṇagaṇākīrṇaṃ bāṇasya bhavanottamam 
kailāsaśikharaprakhyaṃ mahendrabhavanopamam  RKV 
nārado gagane śīghramagamatpurasaṃmukhaḥ 
dvāradeśaṃ samāsādya kṣattāraṃ vākyamabravīt  RKV 
bhobhoḥ kṣattarmahābuddhe rājakāryaviśārada 
śīghraṃ bāṇāya cācakṣva nārado dvāri tiṣṭhati  RKV 
sa vandayitvā caraṇau nāradasya tvarānvitaḥ 
sabhāmadhyagataṃ bāṇaṃ vijñaptum upacakrame  RKV 
vepamānāṅgayaṣṭistu kareṇāpihitānanaḥ 
śṛṇvatāṃ sarvayodhānāmidaṃ vacanamabravīt  RKV 
vandito devagandharvairyakṣakinnaradānavaiḥ 
kalipriyo durārādhyo nārado dvāri tiṣṭhati  RKV 
dvārapālasya tadvākyaṃ śrutvā bāṇastvarānvitaḥ 
dvāḥsthamāha mahādaityaḥ savismayamidaṃ tadā  RKV 
bāṇa uvāca
brahmaputraṃ satejaskaṃ duḥsahaṃ duratikramam 
praveśaya mahābhāgaṃ kimarthaṃ vārito bahiḥ  RKV 
śrutvā prabhorvacastasya prāveśayadudīritam 
gatvā vegena mahatā nāradaṃ gṛhamāgatam  RKV 
dṛṣṭvā devarṣim āyāntaṃ nāradaṃ surapūjitam 
sāhasotthāya saṃhṛṣṭo vavande caraṇau muneḥ  RKV 
dadau cāsanamarghyaṃ ca pādyaṃ pūjāṃ yathāvidhi 
nyavedayacca tadrājyamātmānaṃ bāndhavaiḥ saha  RKV 
papraccha kuśalaṃ cāpi muniṃ bāṇāsuraḥ svayam  RKV 
nārada uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābāho danorvaṃśavivarddhana 
ko 'nyastribhuvane ślāghyas tvāṃ muktvā danupuṃgava  RKV 
pūjito'haṃ danuśreṣṭha dhanaratnaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ 
rājyena cātmanā vāpi hyevaṃ kaḥ pūjayetparaḥ  RKV 
na me kāryaṃ hi bhogena bhuṅkṣva rājyamanāmayam 
tvaddarśanotsukaḥ prāpto dṛṣṭvā devaṃ maheśvaram  RKV 
bhramate tripuraṃ loke strīsatītvānmayā śrutam 
tāndraṣṭukāmaḥ samprāptastvaddārāndānaveśvara  RKV 
manyase yadi me śīghraṃ darśayasva ca māciram 
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā kañcukiṃ samudīkṣya vai  RKV 
antaḥpuracaraṃ vṛddhaṃ daṇḍapāṇiṃ guṇānvitam 
uvāca rājā hṛṣṭātmā śabdenāpūrayandiśaḥ  RKV 
nāradāya mahādevīṃ darśayasveha kañcukin 
antaḥpuracaraiḥ sarvaiḥ sametām aviśaṅkitaḥ  RKV 
nāthasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya gṛhītvā nāradaṃ kare 
praviśyākathayaddevyai nārado 'yaṃ samāgataḥ  RKV 
dṛṣṭvā devī muniśreṣṭhaṃ kṛtvā pādābhivandanam 
āsanaṃ kāñcanaṃ śubhram arghyapādyādikaṃ dadau  RKV 
tasyai sa bhagavāṃstuṣṭo hyāśīrvādamadātparam 
nānyā devi triloke 'pi tvatsamā dṛśyate 'ṅganā  RKV 
pativratā śubhācārā satyaśaucasamanvitā 
yasyāḥ prabhāvāttripuraṃ bhramate cakravatsadā  RKV 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ devī nāradasya sudānvitam 
paryapṛcchadṛṣiṃ bhaktyā dharmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃvarā  RKV 
rājñyuvāca
bhagavanmānuṣe loke devāstuṣyanti kairvrataiḥ 
kāni dānāni dīyante yeṣāṃ ca syānmahatphalam  RKV 
upavāsāśca ye kecitstrīdharme kathitā budhaiḥ 
yaiḥ kṛtaiḥ svargamāyānti sukṛtinyaḥ striyo yathā  RKV 
yat tat sarvaṃ mahābhāga kathayasva yathātatham 
śrotumicchāmyahaṃ sarvaṃ kathayasvāviśaṅkitaḥ  RKV 
nārada uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābhāge praśno 'yaṃ veditastvayā 
yaṃ śrutvā sarvanārīṇāṃ dharmavṛddhistu jāyate  RKV 
upavāsaiśca dānaiśca patiputrau vaśānugau 
bāndhavaiḥ pūjyate nityaṃ yaiḥ kṛtaiḥ kathayāmi te  RKV 
durbhagā subhagā yaistu subhagā durbhagā bhavet 
putriṇī putrarahitā hyaputrā putriṇī tathā  RKV 
bhartāraṃ labhate kanyā tathānyā bhartṛvarjitā 
kṛtākṛtaiśca jāyante tannibodhasva sundari  RKV 
tiladhenuṃ suvarṇaṃ ca rūpyaṃ gā vāsasī tathā 
pānīyaṃ bhūmidānaṃ ca gandhadhūpānulepanam  RKV 
pādukopānahau chatraṃ puṇyāni vyañjanāni ca 
pādābhyaṅgaṃ śiro'bhyaṅgaṃ snānaṃ śayyāsanāni ca  RKV 
etāni ye prayacchanti nopasarpanti te yamam 
madhu māṣaṃ payaḥ sarpirlavaṇaṃ guḍamauṣadham  RKV 
pānīyaṃ bhūmidānaṃ ca śālīnikṣurasāṃstathā 
āraktavāsasī ślakṣṇe dampatyorlalitādine  RKV 
saubhāgyaṃ jāyate caiva iha loke paratra ca 
brāhmaṇe vṛttasampanne surūpe ca guṇānvite  RKV 
tithau yasyāmidaṃ deyaṃ tatte rājñi vadāmyaham 
pratipatsu ca yā nārī pūrvāhṇe ca śucivratā  RKV 
indhanaṃ brāhmaṇe dadyātprīyatāṃ me hutāśanaḥ 
tasyā janmāni ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgapratyaṅgasandhiṣu  RKV 
na rajo naiva santāpo jāyate rājavallabhe 
dvitīyāyāṃ tu yā nārī navanītamudānvitā  RKV 
dadāti dvijamukhyāya sukumāratanurbhavet 
lavaṇaṃ vipravaryāya tṛtīyāyāṃ prayacchati  RKV 
gaurī me prīyatāṃ devī tasyāḥ puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu 
kaumārikā patiṃ prāpya tena sārddhamumā yathā  RKV 
krīḍatyavidhavā cāpi labhate sā mahadyaśaḥ 
naktaṃ kṛtvā caturthyāṃ vai dadyādviprāya modakān  RKV 
prīyatāṃ mama deveśo gaṇanātho vināyakaḥ 
tasyāstena phalenāśu sarvakarmasu bhāmini  RKV 
vighnaṃ na jāyate kvāpi evamāha pitāmahaḥ 
pañcamīṃ tu tataḥ prāpya brāhmaṇe tiladā tu yā  RKV 
sā bhavedrūpasampannā yathā caiva tilottamā 
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ tu yā madhūkasya phaladā tu bhavetsadā  RKV 
uddiśya cāgnijaṃ devaṃ brāhmaṇe vedapārage 
tasyāḥ putro yathā skando devasaṅgheṣu cottamaḥ  RKV 
utpadyate mahārājaḥ sarvalokeṣu pūjitaḥ 
saptamyāṃ yā dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ suvarṇena prapūjayet  RKV 
uddiśya jagato nāthaṃ devadevaṃ divākaram 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yadvai kathitaṃ dvijasattamaiḥ  RKV 
tatte rājñi pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ sati 
dadrūcitrakakuṣṭhāni maṇḍalāni vicarcikā  RKV 
na bhavantīha cāṅgeṣu pūrvakarmārjitānyapi 
kṛṣṇāṃ dhenuṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ yā prayacchati bhāminī  RKV 
brāhmaṇe vṛttasampanne prīyatāṃ me maheśvaraḥ 
tasyā janmārjitaṃ pāpaṃ naśyate vibhavānvitā  RKV 
jāyate nātra sandeho yasmāddānamanuttamam 
gandhadhūpaṃ tu yā nārī bhaktyā viprāya dāpayet  RKV 
kātyāyanīṃ samuddiśya navamyāṃ śṛṇu yatphalam 
tasyā bhrātā pitā putraḥ patirvā raṇamuttamam  RKV 
prāpyate naiva sīdanti tena dānena rakṣitāḥ 
ikṣudaṇḍarasaṃ devi daśamyāṃ yā prayacchati  RKV 
lokapālānsamuddiśya brāhmaṇe vyaṅgavarjite 
tena dānena sā nityaṃ sarvalokasya vallabhā  RKV 
jāyate nātra sandeha ityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt 
ekādaśyāmupoṣyātha dvādaśyāmudakapradā  RKV 
nārāyaṇaṃ samuddiśya brāhmaṇe viṣṇutatpare 
sā sadā sparśasambhāṣairdrāvayedbhāvayejjanam  RKV 
yasmāddānaṃ maharloke hyanantam udake bhavet 
pādābhyaṅgaṃ śiro'bhyaṅgaṃ kāmamuddiśya vai dvije  RKV 
dadāti ca trayodaśyāṃ bhaktyā paramayāṅganā 
yasyāṃ yasyāṃ mṛtā jāyed bhūyo yonyāṃ tu janmani  RKV 
tasyāṃ tasyāṃ tu sā bharturna viyujyeta karhicit 
tathāpyevaṃ caturdaśyāṃ dadyāt pātramupānahau  RKV 
brahmaṇe dharmamuddiśya tasyā lokā hyanāmayāḥ 
evaṃ ca pakṣapakṣānte śrāddhe tarped dvijottamān  RKV 
avyucchinnā sadā rājñi santatir jāyate bhuvi 
evaṃ te tithimāhātmyaṃ dānayogena bhāṣitam  RKV 
tathā vanaspatīnāṃ tu ārādhanavidhiṃ śṛṇu 
jambūṃ nimbataruṃ caiva tindukaṃ madhukaṃ tathā  RKV 
āmraṃ cāmalakaṃ caiva śālmaliṃ vaṭapippalau 
śamībilvāmalīvṛkṣaṃ kadalīṃ pāṭalīṃ tathā  RKV 
anyānpuṇyatamānvṛkṣānupetya svargamāpnuyāt  RKV 
nārada uvāca
caitre māse tu yā nārī kuryādvratamanuttamam 
tasya vratasya cānyāni kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  RKV 
śrutena yena subhage durbhagatvaṃ na paśyati 
yathā himaṃ raviṃ prāpya vilayaṃ yāti bhūtale  RKV 
tathā duḥkhaṃ ca daurbhāgyaṃ vratādasmādvilīyate 
madhukākhyāṃ tu lalitāmārādhayati yena vai  RKV 
vidhiṃ taṃ śṛṇu subhage kathyamānaṃ sukhāvaham 
caitre śuklatṛtīyāyāṃ susnātā śuddhamānasā  RKV 
pratimāṃ madhuvṛkṣasya śāṅkarīm umayā saha 
kārayitvā dvijavaraiḥ pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi  RKV 
sugandhikusumairdhūpaistathā karpūrakuṅkumaiḥ 
pūjayed vidhinā devaṃ mantrayuktena bhāminī  RKV 
pādau namaḥ śivāyeti meḍhre vai manmathāya ca 
kālodarāyet yudaraṃ nīlakaṃṭhāya kaṇṭhakam  RKV 
śiraḥ sarvātmane pūjya umāṃ paścātprapūjayet 
kṣāmodarāyaihyudaraṃ sukaṇṭhāyai ca kaṇṭhakam  RKV 
śiraḥ saubhāgyadāyinyai paścādarghyaṃ pradāpayet  RKV 
namaste devadeveśa umāvara jagatpate 
arghyeṇānena me sarvaṃ daurbhāgyaṃ nāśaya prabho 
iti arghyamantraḥ  RKV 
arghyaṃ dattvā tataḥ paścātkarakaṃ vāripūritam 
madhūkapātropabhṛtaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ tu śaktitaḥ  RKV 
karakaṃ vārisampūrṇaṃ saubhāgyena tu saṃyutam 
dattaṃ tu lalite tubhyaṃ saubhāgyādivivardhanam 
iti karakadānamantraḥ  RKV 
mantreṇānena viprāya dadyāt karakamuttamam 
lavaṇaṃ varjayec chuklāṃ yāvadanyāṃ tṛtīyikām  RKV 
kṣamāpya devīṃ deveśāṃ naktam adyātsvayaṃ haviḥ 
anena vidhinā sārdhaṃ māsi māsi hy apakramet  RKV 
phālgunasya tṛtīyāyāṃ śuklāyāṃ tu samāpyate 
vaiśākhe lavaṇaṃ deyaṃ jyeṣṭhe cājyaṃ pradīyate  RKV 
āṣāḍhe māsi niṣpāvāḥ payo deyaṃ tu śrāvaṇe 
mudgā deyā nabhasye tu śālimāśvayuje tathā  RKV 
kārttike śarkarāpātraṃ karakaṃ rasasaṃbhṛtam 
mārgaśīrṣe tu kārpāsaṃ karakaṃ ghṛtasaṃyutam  RKV 
pauṣe tu kuṅkumaṃ deyaṃ māghe pātraṃ tilair bhṛtam 
phālgune māsi samprāpte pātraṃ modakasaṃbhṛtam  RKV 
paścāttṛtīyādeyaṃ yattatpūrvasyāṃ vivarjayet 
vidhānamāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ sāmānyaṃ manasaḥ priye  RKV 
pratimāṃ madhuvṛkṣasya tāmeva pratipūjayet 
tasmai sarvaṃ tu viprāya ācāryāya pradīyate  RKV 
tataḥ saṃvatsarasyānte udyāpanavidhiṃ śṛṇu 
madhuvṛkṣaṃ tato gatvā bahusambhārasaṃvṛtaḥ  RKV 
nikhanetpratimāṃ madhye mādhūkīṃ madhukasya ca 
tatrasthaṃ pūjayet sarvam umādehārddhadhāriṇam  RKV 
pūjopahārairvipulaiḥ kuṅkumena punaḥpunaḥ 
ślakṣṇābhiḥ puṣpamālābhiḥ kausumbhaiḥ kesareṇa ca  RKV 
kausumbhe vāsasī śubhre atasīpuṣpasannibhe 
paridhāpya tāṃ pratimāṃ dampatī ravisaṃkhyayā  RKV 
upānadyugalaiśchatraiḥ kaṇṭhasūtraiḥ sakaṇṭhikaiḥ 
kaṭakairaṅgulīyaiśca śayanīyaiḥ śubhāstṛtaiḥ  RKV 
kuṅkumena viliptāṅgau bahupuṣpaiśca pūjitau 
bhojayed vividhai ratnair madhūkāvāsake sthitau  RKV 
bhuktotthitau tu viśrāmya śayyāsu ca kṣamāpayet 
gurumūlaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ gururjñeyo maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
prīte gurau tataḥ sarvaṃ jagatprītaṃ surāsuram 
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ loke yatkiṃciddayitaṃ gṛhe  RKV 
tatsarvaṃ gurave deyamātmanaḥ śreya icchatā 
idaṃ tu dhanibhir deyamanyair deyaṃ yathocyate  RKV 
dāmpatyamekaṃ vidhivatpratipūjya śubhavrataiḥ 
dvitīyaṃ gurudāmpatyaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ vivarjayet  RKV 
tataḥ kṣamāpayeddevīṃ devaṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ gurum 
yathā tvaṃ devi lalite na viyuktāsi śambhunā  RKV 
tathā me patiputrāṇām aviyogaḥ pradīyatām 
anena vidhinā kṛtvā tṛtīyāṃ madhusaṃjñikām  RKV 
indrāṇī cendrapatnītvamavāpa sutamuttamam 
saubhāgyaṃ sarvalokeṣu sarvarddhisukhamuttamam  RKV 
anena vidhinā yā tu kumārī vratamācaret 
śobhanaṃ patimāpnoti yathendrāṇyā śatakratuḥ  RKV 
durbhagā subhagatvaṃ ca subhagā putriṇī bhavet 
putriṇyakṣayamāpnoti na śokaṃ paśyati kvacit  RKV 
anekajanmajanitaṃ daurbhāgyaṃ naśyati dhruvam 
mṛtā tu tridivaṃ prāpya umayā saha modate  RKV 
kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān 
punastu sambhave loke pārthivaṃ patim āpnuyāt  RKV 
subhagā rūpasampannā pārthivaṃ janayet sutam  RKV 
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ vratānāmuttamaṃ vratam 
anyatpṛcchasva subhage vāñchitaṃ yaddhṛdi sthitam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye madhūkatṛtīyāvratavidhānamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ  
nāma ṣaḍviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā rājñī vacanam abravīt 
prasādaṃ kuru viprendra gṛhṇa dānaṃ yathepsitam  RKV 
suvarṇamaṇiratnāni vastrāṇi vividhāni ca 
tatte dārayāmi viprendra yaccānyad api durlabham  RKV 
rājñyāstu vacanaṃ śrutvā nārado vākyam abravīt 
anyeṣāṃ dīyatāṃ bhadre ye dvijāḥ kṣīṇavṛttayaḥ  RKV 
vayaṃ tu sarvasampannā bhaktigrāhyāḥ sadaiva hi 
ityuktā sā tadā rājñī vedavedāṅgapāragān  RKV 
āhūya brāhmaṇān niḥsvāndātuṃ samupacakrame 
yat kiṃcinnāradenoktaṃ dānasaubhāgyavardhanam  RKV 
tena dānena me nityaṃ prīyetāṃ hariśaṅkarau 
tato rājñī ca sā prāha nāradaṃ munipuṃgavam  RKV 
rājñyuvāca
dānaṃ dattaṃ tvayoktaṃ yadbhartṛkarmaparaṃ hi tat 
ājanmajanma me bhartā bhavedbāṇo dvijottama  RKV 
nānyo hi daivataṃ tāta muktvā bāṇaṃ dvijottama 
tena satyena me bhartā jīvecca śaradāṃ śatam  RKV 
nānyo dharmo bhavet strīṇāṃ daivataṃ hi patiryathā 
tathāpi tava vākyena dānaṃ dattaṃ yathāvidhi  RKV 
svakaṃ karma kariṣyāmo bhartāraṃ prati mānada 
brahmarṣe gaccha cedānīṃ tvamāśīrvādaḥ pradīyatām  RKV 
tatheti tāmanujñāpya nārado nṛpasattama 
sarvāsāṃ mānasaṃ hṛtvā anyataḥ kṛtamānasaḥ  RKV 
jagāmādarśanaṃ vipraḥ pūjyamānastu khecaraiḥ 
tato gatamanaskāstā bhartāraṃ prati bhārata  RKV 
vivarṇā niṣprabhā jātā nāradena vimohitāḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye tripurakṣobhaṇavarṇanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
etasminn antare rudro narmadātaṭamāsthitaḥ 
krīḍate hyumayā sārddhaṃ nāradas tatra cāgataḥ  RKV 
praṇamya devadeveśamumayā saha śaṅkaram 
vyajñāpayat tadā devaṃ yad vṛttaṃ tripure tadā  RKV 
gato 'haṃ svāminirdeśād yatra tadbāṇamandiram 
dṛṣṭā bāṇaṃ yathānyāyaṃ gato hyantaḥpuraṃ mahat  RKV 
tatra bhāryāsahasrāṇi dṛṣṭvā bāṇasya dhīmataḥ 
yathāyogyaṃ yathākāmam āgataḥ kṣobhya tatpuram  RKV 
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā sādhu sādhviti pūjayan 
cintayāmāsa deveśo bhramaṇaṃ tripurasya hi  RKV 
karamuktaṃ yathā cakraṃ viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā 
mahāvegaṃ mahāyāmaṃ rakṣitaṃ tejasā mama  RKV 
sa ca me bhaktinirato bāṇo loke ca viśrutaḥ 
bhāratī ca mayā dattā brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ  RKV 
evaṃ sa suciraṃ kālaṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ 
cintayitvā sunirvāṇaṃ kāryaṃ prati janeśvaraḥ  RKV

yamaṃ tu dakṣiṇe pārśve vāme kālaṃ sudāruṇam 
ādityacandrau cakre tu gandharvānārakādiṣu  RKV 
yantāraṃ ca surajyeṣṭhaṃ vedānkṛtvā hayottamān

kṛtvā pratodam oṃkāraṃ mukhagrāhyaṃ maheśvaraḥ 
dhātāraṃ cāgrataḥ kṛtvā vidhātāraṃ ca pṛṣṭhataḥ  RKV 
mārutātsarvato digbhya ūrdhvayantre tathaiva ca 
mahoragapiśācāṃśca siddhavidyādharāṃstathā  RKV 
gaṇāṃśca bhūtasaṅghāṃśca sarve sarvāṅgasaṃdhiṣu 
yugamadhye sthito meruryugasyādho mahāgiriḥ  RKV 
sarpā yantrasthitā ghorāḥ śamye varuṇanairṛtau 
gāyatrī caiva sāvitrī sthite te raśmibandhane  RKV 
satyaṃ rathadhvaje śaucaṃ damaṃ rakṣāṃ samantataḥ 
rathaṃ devamayaṃ kṛtvā devadevo maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
saṃnaddhaḥ kavacī khaḍgī baddhagodhāṅgulitravān 
baddhā parikaraṃ gāḍhaṃ jaṭājūṭaṃ niyamya ca  RKV 
sajjaṃ kṛtvā dhanurdivyaṃ yojayitvā rathottamam 
rathamadhye sthito devaḥ śuśubhe ca yudhiṣṭhira  RKV 
dhanuṣaḥ śabdanādenākampayacca jagattrayam 
sthānaṃ kṛtvā tu vaiśākhaṃ nibhṛtaṃ saṃsthito haraḥ  RKV 
nirīkṣya suciraṃ kālaṃ kopasaṃraktalocanaḥ 
dhyātvā taṃ paramaṃ mantram ātmānaṃ ca nirudhya saḥ  RKV 
mumoca sahasā bāṇaṃ purasya vadhakāṅkṣayā 
yadā trīṇi sametāni antarikṣasthitāni tu  RKV 
tataḥ kālanimeṣārdhaṃ dṛṣṭvaikyaṃ tripurasya ca 
triparvaṇā triśalyena tatastānyavasādayat  RKV 
tato lokā bhayatrastās tripure bharatottama 
sarvāsuravināśāya kālarūpā bhayāvahāḥ  RKV 
aṭṭahāsān pramuñcanti kaṣṭarūpā narās tadā 
nimeṣonmeṣaṇaṃ caiva kurvanti lipikarmasu  RKV 
niṣpandanayanā martyāścitreṣvālikhitā iva 
devāyatanagā devā raṭanti prahasanti ca 
svapne paśyanti cātmānaṃ raktāmbaravibhūṣitam  RKV 
raktamālyottamāṅgāśca patantaḥ kārdame hrade 
paśyanti nāma cātmānaṃ satailābhyaṅgamastakam  RKV 
paśyanti yānamārūḍhaṃ rāsabhaiśca nṛpottama 
saṃvartako mahāvāyuryugāntapratimo mahān  RKV 
gṛhān unmūlayāmāsa vṛkṣajātīnanekaśaḥ 
bhūmikampāḥ sanirghātā ulkāpātāḥ sahasraśaḥ  RKV 
rudhiraṃ varṣate devo miśritaṃ karkarairbahu 
agnikuṇḍeṣu viprāṇāṃ hutaḥ samyagghutāśanaḥ  RKV 
jvalate dhūmasaṃyukto visphuliṅgakaṇaiḥ saha 
kuṃjarā vimadā jātāsturagāḥ sattvavarjitāḥ  RKV 
avāditāni vādyante vāditrāṇi sahasraśaḥ 
dhvajā hyakampitāḥ petuśchatrāṇi vividhāni ca  RKV 
jvalati pādapāstatra parṇāni ca sabhaṃ tataḥ 
sarvaṃ tadvyākulībhūtaṃ hāhākārasamanvitam  RKV 
udyānāni vicitrāṇi prababhañja prabhañjanaḥ 
tena saṃpreritāḥ sarve jvalanti viśikhāḥ śikhāḥ  RKV 
vṛkṣagulmalatāvallyo gṛhāṇi ca samantataḥ 
digvibhāgaiśca sarvaiśca pravṛtto havyavāhanaḥ  RKV 
sarvaṃ kiṃśukaparṇābhaṃ prajvalaccaiva dṛśyate 
gṛhādgṛhaṃ tadā gantuṃ naiva dhūmena śakyate  RKV 
harakopāgninirdagdhāḥ krandante tripure janāḥ 
pradīptaṃ sarvato dikṣu dahyate tripuraṃ param  RKV 
patanti śikharāgrāṇi viśīrṇāni sahasraśaḥ 
pāvako dhūmasaṃpṛkto dahyamānaḥ samantataḥ  RKV 
nṛtyanvai vyāptadigdeśaḥ kāntāreṣvabhidhāvati 
devāgāreṣu sarveṣu gṛheṣvaṭṭālakeṣu ca  RKV 
pravṛtto hutabhuktatra pure kālapracoditaḥ 
dadāha lokānsarvatra harakopaprakopitaḥ  RKV 
dahate traipuraṃ lokaṃ bālavṛddhasamanvitam 
sapuraṃ sagṛhadvāraṃ savāhanavanaṃ nṛpa  RKV 
kecidbhojanasaktāśca pānāsaktāstathāpare 
aparā nṛtyagīteṣu saṃsaktā vārayoṣitaḥ  RKV 
anyonyaṃ ca pariṣvajya hutāśanaśikhārditāḥ 
dahyamānā nṛpaśreṣṭha sarve gacchantyacetanāḥ  RKV 
athānye dānavāstatra dahyante 'gnivimohitāḥ 
na śaktāścānyato gantuṃ dhūmenākulitānanāḥ 
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇā nalinyo hemapaṅkajāḥ  RKV 
dahyante vividhās tatra vāpyaḥ kūpāśca bhārata 
dṛśyante 'naladagdhāni purodyānāni dīrghikāḥ 
amlānaiḥ paṅkajaiśchannā vistīrṇāvasuyojanāḥ  RKV 
girikūṭanibhāstatra prāsādā ratnaśobhitāḥ 
dṛśyante 'nalasaṃdagdhā viśīrṇā dharaṇītale  RKV 
narastrībālavṛddheṣu dahyamāneṣu sarvataḥ 
nirdayaṃ jvalate vahnirhāhākāro mahānabhūt 
kācicca sukhasaṃsuptāpramattānyā nṛpottama  RKV 
krīḍitvā ca suvistīrṇaśayanasthā varāṅganā 
kācitsuptā viśālākṣī hārāvalivibhūṣitā 
dhūmenākulitā dīnā nyapataddhavyavāhane  RKV 
kācittasminpure dīpte putrasnehānulālasā 
putram āliṅgate gāḍhaṃ dahyate tripure 'gninā  RKV 
kācitkanakavarṇābhā indranīlavibhūṣitā 
bhartāraṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā patitā tasya copari  RKV 
kācidādityavarṇābhā prasuptā tu priyopari 
agnijvālāhatā gāḍhaṃ kaṃṭhamāliṅgate nṛpa  RKV 
medhavarṇā parā nārī calatkanakamekhalā 
śvetavastrottarīyā tu papāta dharaṇītale  RKV 
kācitkundenduvarṇābhā nīlaratnavibhūṣitā

kācitprabhūtaduḥkhārtā vilalāpa varāṅganā

vepate patitā bhūmau kheditā vaḍavā yathā 
itaścetaśca kācicca dahyamānā varāṅganā  RKV

kūṣmāṇḍasya ca dhūmrasya kuhakasya bakasya ca 
virūpanayanasyāpi virūpākṣasya caiva hi  RKV 
śumbho ḍimbhaśca raudraśca prahlādaścāsurottamaḥ 
daṇḍapāṇir vipāṇiśca siṃhavaktras tathānagha  RKV

evamanye 'pi ye keciddānavā baladarpitāḥ

kiṃ tvayā na śrutaṃ loke avadhyāḥ sarvathā striyaḥ 
kiṃ tu tubhyaṃ guṇo hyasti dahane pavaneritaḥ  RKV 
na kāruṇyaṃ tvayā kiṃcid dākṣiṇyaṃ ca striyaṃ prati 
dayāṃ mlecchā hi kurvanti vacanaṃ vīkṣya yoṣitām  RKV

na mātā na pitā caiva na bandhur nāparo janaḥ  RKV 
muktvā caiva maheśānaṃ paramārtiharaṃ param

ahaṃ punaḥ samastaiśca dahyāmi saha sādhubhiḥ 
evamuktvā śivaṃ liṅgaṃ kṛtvā tanmastakopari  RKV 
nirjagāma gṛhācchīghraṃ pāvakenāvaguṇṭhitaḥ

prāṇādiṣṭatamaṃ deva tasmād rakṣitum arhasi

bāṇa uvāca
śiva śaṅkara sarvaharāya namo bhavabhītabhayārtiharāya namaḥ 
kusumāyudhadehavināśaṃkara pramadāpriyakāmaka deva namaḥ  RKV

jaya nirmalabhasmaviliptagātra jaya mantramūla jagadekapātra  RKV 
jaya viṣadharakapilajaṭākalāpa jaya bhairavavighṛtapinākacāpa 
jaya viṣamanayanaparimuktasaṅga jaya śaṅkara dhṛtagāṅgataraṅga  RKV 
jaya bhīmarūpa khaṭvāṅgahasta śaśiśekhara jaya jagatāṃ praśasta 
jaya sukhareśa suralokasāra jaya sarvasakalanirdagdhasāra  RKV 
jaya kīrtanīya jagatāṃ pavitra jaya vṛṣāṅka bahuvidhacaritra 
jaya viracitanarakaṅkālamāla aghāsuradehakaṅkālakāla  RKV 
jaya nīlakaṃṭha varavṛṣabhagamana jaya sakalalokaduritānuśamana 
jaya siddhasurāsuravinatacaraṇa jaya rudra raudrabhavajaladhitaraṇa  RKV 
jaya giriśa sureśvaramānanīya jaya sūkṣmarūpa saṃcitanīya 
jaya dagdhatripura viśvasattva jaya sakalaśāstraparamārthatattva  RKV 
jaya duravabodha saṃsāratāra kalikaluṣamahārṇavaghoratāra 
jaya surāsuradevagaṇeśa namo hayavānarasiṃhagajendramukha  RKV 
atihrasvasthūlasudīrghatama upalabdhir na śakyate te hyamaraiḥ 
praṇato 'smi nirañjana te caraṇau jaya sāmba sulocanakāntihara  RKV 
aprāpya tvāṃ kim atyantam ucchrayī na vināśayet 
atipramāthi ca tadā tapo mahatsudāruṇam  RKV 
na putrabāndhavā dārā na samastaḥ suhṛjjanaḥ 
saṅkaṭe 'bhyupagacchanti vrajantamekagāminam  RKV 
yadeva karma kaivalyaṃ kṛtaṃ tena śubhāśubham 
tadeva sārthavat tasya bhavatyagre tu gacchataḥ  RKV 
nirdhanasyaiva carato na bhayaṃ vidyate kvacit 
dhanībhayairna mucyeta dhanaṃ tasmāttyajāmyaham  RKV 
lubdhāḥ pāpāni kurvanti śuddhāṃśā naiva mānavāḥ 
śrutvā dharmasya sarvasvaṃ śrutvā caivāvadhārya tat  RKV 
tvaṃ viṣṇustvaṃ jagannātho brahmarūpaḥ sanātanaḥ 
indrastvaṃ devadeveśa suranātha namo 'stu te  RKV 
tvaṃ kṣitirvaruṇaścaiva pavanastvaṃ hutāśanaḥ 
tvaṃ dīkṣā yajamānaśca ākāśaṃ soma eva ca  RKV 
tvaṃ sūryastvaṃ tu vitteśo yamastvaṃ gurureva ca 
tvayā vyāptaṃ jagatsarvaṃ trailokyaṃ bhāsvatā yathā  RKV 
etadbāṇakṛtaṃ stotraṃ śrutvā devo maheśvaraḥ 
krodhaṃ muktvā prasannātmā tadā vacanam abravīt  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
na bhetavyaṃ na bhetavyamadyaprabhṛti dānava 
sauvarṇe bhavane tiṣṭha mama pārśve 'thavā punaḥ  RKV 
putrapautraprapautraiśca bāndhavaiḥ saha bhāryayā 
adyaprabhṛti vatsa tvamavadhyaḥ sarvaśatruṣu  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
bhūyastasya varo datto devadevena bhārata 
svarge martye ca pātāle pūjitaḥ sasurāsuraiḥ  RKV 
akṣayaścāvyayaścaiva vasa tvaṃ vai yathāsukham 
tato nivārayāmāsa rudraḥ saptaśikhaṃ tadā  RKV 
tṛtīyaṃ rakṣitaṃ tasya puraṃ devena śambhunā 
jvālāmālākulaṃ cānyatpatitaṃ dharaṇītale  RKV 
ardhena prasthitādūrdhvaṃ tasya jvālā divaṃ gatāḥ 
hāhākāro mahāṃstatra ṛṣisaṅghairudīritaḥ  RKV 
daivataiśca mahābhāgaiḥ siddhavidyādharādibhiḥ 
ekaṃ tu patitaṃ tatra śrīśaile khaṇḍamuttaram  RKV 
dvitīyaṃ patitaṃ rājañchaile hyamarakaṇṭake 
prajvalatpatitaṃ tatra tena jvāleśvaraṃ smṛtam  RKV 
dagdhe tu tripure rājanpatite khaṇḍa uttame 
rudro devaḥ sthitastatra jvālāmālānivārakaḥ  RKV 
hāhākāraparāṇāṃ tu ṛṣīṇāṃ rakṣaṇāya ca 
svayaṃ mūrtirmaheśān umāvṛṣabhasaṃyutaḥ  RKV 
manasāpi smared yastu bhaktyā hyamarakaṇṭakam 
cāndrāyaṇādhikaṃ puṇyaṃ sa labhennātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
atipuṇyo giriśreṣṭho yasmād bharatasattama 
asmānnityaṃ bhaved rājansarvapāpakṣayaṃkaraḥ  RKV

nānāgulmalatākīrṇo nānāvallībhir āvṛtaḥ  RKV 
siṃhavyāghrasamākīrṇo mṛgayūthairalaṃkṛtaḥ

brahmendraviṣṇupramukhairhyamaraiśca sahasraśaḥ 
sevyate devadeveśaḥ śaṅkarastatra parvate  RKV 
patanaṃ kurute yo 'sminparvate 'marakaṇṭake 
krīḍate kramaśo rājanbhuvanāni caturdaśa  RKV 
aindraṃ vāhnaṃ ca kauberaṃ vāyavyaṃ yāmyameva ca 
nairṛtyaṃ vāruṇaṃ caiva saumyaṃ sauraṃ tathaiva ca  RKV 
brāhmaṃ ca padamakliṣṭaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tadanantaram 
umārudraṃ mahābhāga aiśvaraṃ tadanantaram  RKV 
paraṃ sadāśivaṃ śāntaṃ sūkṣmaṃ jyotiratīndriyam 
tasminyāti layaṃ dhīro vidhinā nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
ko 'pyatra vidhiruddiṣṭaḥ patane ṛṣisattama 
etanme sarvamācakṣva saṃśayo 'sti mahāmune  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇuṣva kathayiṣyāmi taṃ vidhiṃ pāṇḍunandana 
yatkṛtvā prathamaṃ karma nipatettadanantaram  RKV

tasya parvatarājasya yaḥ karoti pradakṣiṇam 
pradakṣiṇīkṛtā tena pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
vācikaṃ mānasaṃ caiva kāyikaṃ trividhaṃ ca yat 
naśyate pātakaṃ sarvamityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt  RKV 
amareśvarapārśve ca tīrthaṃ śakreśvaraṃ nṛpa 
tapas taptvā purā tatra śakreṇa sthāpitaṃ kila  RKV 
kuśāvartaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ brahmaṇā ca kṛtaṃ śubham 
brahmakuṇḍamiti khyātaṃ haṃsatīrthaṃ tathā param  RKV 
ambarīṣasya tīrthaṃ ca mahākāleśvaraṃ tathā 
kāveryāḥ pūrvabhāge ca tīrthaṃ vai mātṛkeśvaram  RKV 
etāni dakṣiṇe tīre revāyā bharatarṣabha 
saṃsevanasnānadānaiḥ pāpasaṅghaharāṇi ca  RKV 
bhṛgutuṅge mahārāja prasiddho bhairavaḥ śivaḥ 
tasya yāmyavibhāge ca tīrthaṃ vai capaleśvaram  RKV 
etau sthitau duḥkhaharau revāyā uttare taṭe 
tāvabhyarcya tathā natvā samyag yātrāphalaṃ bhavet 
adṛṣṭapūjitau tau hi narāṇāṃ vighnakārakau  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe tripuravidhvaṃsane jvāleśvaratīrthāmareśvatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ  
nāmāṣṭāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kāverīti ca vikhyātā triṣu lokeṣu sattama 
māhātmyaṃ śrotum icchāmi tasyā mārkaṇḍa tattvataḥ  RKV 
kīdṛśaṃ darśanaṃ tasyāḥ phalaṃ sparśe 'thavā vibho 
snāne jāpye 'thavā dāna upavāse tathā mune  RKV 
kathayasva mahābhāga kāverīsaṅgame phalam

yathā dharmaprasaṅge tu mune dharmo 'pi jāyate  RKV 
svargaśca narakaścaiva ityevaṃ vaidikī śrutiḥ  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābhāga yatpṛṣṭo 'haṃ tvayādhunā 
śṛṇuṣvaikamanā bhūtvā kāverīphalam uttamam  RKV 
asti yakṣo mahāsattvaḥ kuberonāma viśrutaḥ 
so 'pi tīrthaprabhāvena rājanyakṣādhipo 'bhavat  RKV 
tacchṛṇuṣva vidhānena bhaktyā paramayā nṛpa 
siddhiṃ prāpto mahābhāga kāverīsaṅgamena tu  RKV

tatra snātvā śucirbhūtvā kuberaḥ satyavikramaḥ  RKV

īśvara uvāca
yattvayā prārthitaṃ sarvaṃ phalaṃ dharmasya tattathā 
ityevamuktvā taṃ tatra jagāmādarśanaṃ haraḥ  RKV 
so 'pi snātvā vidhānena saṃtarpya pitṛdevatāḥ 
āmantrayitvā tattīrthaṃ kṛtārthaśca gṛhaṃ yayau  RKV 
pūjitastatra yakṣaistu so 'bhiṣikto vidhānataḥ

anāśakaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yadvai tacchṛṇuṣva narottama  RKV 
gandharvāpsaraḥsaṃkīrṇe vimāne sūryasannibhe

ādhiśokavinirmukto jīvecca śaradāṃ śatam  RKV

labdhaṃ yair narmadātoyaṃ ye ca kuryuḥ pradakṣiṇam 
ye pibanti jalaṃ tatra te puṇyā nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
na teṣāṃ santaticchedo daśa janmāni pañca ca 
teṣāṃ pāpaṃ vilīyeta himaṃ sūryodaye yathā  RKV

gaṅgā ṣaṣṭisahasraistu kṣetrapālaiḥ prapūjyate

amareśvare tu saritāṃ ye yogāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
te tvaśītisahasraistu kṣetrapālaistu rakṣitāḥ  RKV

eṣā te kathitā tāta kāverī saritāṃ varā

  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye kāverīsaṅgamamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśo

citronāma mahātejā indrasya dayitaḥ purā 
tasya putro nṛpaśreṣṭha pattreśvara iti śrutaḥ  RKV 
rūpavān subhagaścaiva sarvaśatrubhayaṃkaraḥ 
indrasya dayito 'tyarthaṃ jaya ityeva cāparaḥ  RKV 
sa kadācit sabhāmadhye sarvadevasamāgame 
menakānṛtyagītena mohitaḥ suciraṃ kila  RKV

tāvatsurapatirdevaḥ śaśāpāthājitendriyam  RKV

evam uktaḥ surendreṇa citrasenasuto yuvā 
vepamānaḥ suraśreṣṭhaḥ kṛtāñjaliruvāca ha  RKV 
pattreśvara uvāca
mayā pāpena mūḍhena ajitendriyacetasā 
prāptaṃ vai yatphalaṃ tasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi  RKV 
śakra uvāca
narmadātaṭamāśritya dvādaśābdaṃ jitendriyaḥ

loko'yaṃ pāpināṃ naiva iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ  RKV

gandharvatanayo dhīmānpraṇamyāgāttu bhūtalam  RKV

snātvā japtvā vidhānena arcayitvā ca śaṅkaram  RKV

īśvara uvāca
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te varado 'haṃ tavānagha 
yamicchasi dadāmyadya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
pattreśvara uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si deveśa yadi deyo varo mama 
atra tvaṃ satataṃ tīrthe mama nāmnā bhava prabho  RKV 
etacchrutvā mahādevo harṣagadgadayā girā 
tathetyuktvā yayau hṛṣṭa umayā saha śaṅkaraḥ  RKV

snātvā jāpyavidhānena tarpayitvā pitḥn punaḥ  RKV 
sthāpayāmāsa deveśaṃ tasmiṃs tīrthe vidhānataḥ 
pattreśvaraṃ tu vikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu bhārata  RKV 
indralokaṃ gataḥ śāpānmuktaḥ so 'pi nareśvara 
hṛṣṭaḥ pramudito ramyaṃ jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ  RKV 
eṣa te kathitaḥ praśnaḥ pṛṣṭo yo vai yudhiṣṭhira

  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe patreśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca

etattvāścaryamatulaṃ sarvalokeṣvanuttamam

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahāprājña pṛṣṭaḥ praśnastvayānava

rūpayauvanasampannaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ pṛthivīpatim

aṅgapratyaṅgasampannā yasmāllokeṣu viśrutā

rājovāca
nāhaṃ dravyavihīnasya asavarṇasya karhicit

na kiṃcid uktvā rājānaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata  RKV

mantrayitvātha kāle tu tuṣṭo makhamukhe sthitaḥ  RKV 
yajataśca makhe bhaktyā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha bhārata

viprā durmanaso bhūtvā gatā rājño hi mandiram 
vahnināśaṃ vimanaso rājānam idam abruvan  RKV 
brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ 
duryodhana mahārāja śrūyatāṃ mahadadbhutam

agnikāryapravṛttānāṃ sarveṣāṃ vidhivannṛpa 
kenāpi hetunā vahnirdṛśyate na jvalatyuta  RKV 
tacchrutvā vipriyaṃ ghoraṃ rājā vipramukhāccyutam

kim etad āścaryaparamiti bhobho dvijottamāḥ 
kathyatāṃ kāraṇaṃ sarvaṃ śāstradṛṣṭyā vibhāvya ca  RKV 
mama vā duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcidutāho bhavatāmiha 
yena naṣṭo 'gniśālāyāṃ hutabhuk kena hetunā  RKV

kriyāhīnaṃ kṛtaṃ vātha kena vahnir na dṛśyate  RKV 
annahīno dahed rāṣṭraṃ mantrahīnastu ṛtvijaḥ 
dātāraṃ dakṣiṇāhīno nāsti yajñasamo ripuḥ  RKV 
brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ 
na mantrahīnā hi vayaṃ na ca rājanvrataistathā 
dravyeṇa ca na hīnastvamanyat pāpaṃ vicintyatām  RKV 
rājovāca
tathāpi yūyaṃ sahitā upāyaṃ cintayantviti 
yena śreyo bhaven nityam iha loke paratra ca  RKV 
evamuktāstataḥ sarve brāhmaṇāḥ kṛtaniścayāḥ

evaṃ jñātvā mahārāja svasutāṃ dātumarhasi  RKV 
rājovāca
bhavatāṃ tasya vā kāryaṃ devasya vacanaṃ hṛdi

maya uvāca
