śāpāhato vepamāna indrasya caraṇau śubhau 
prapīḍya mūrdhnā deveśaṃ vijñāpayati bhārata  RKV 
tamuvācābhiśaptaṃ cāpyanāthaṃ ca sureśvaraḥ 
karmaṇā kena śāpasya ghorasyānto bhaviṣyati  RKV 
narmadātaṭamāśritya toṣayanvai maheśvaram 
tiṣṭha yāvad yugasyāntaṃ punarjanma hyavāpsyasi  RKV 
punarbhūtvā tu pūtastvaṃ dāruko nāma viśrutaḥ 
saṃsevya paramaṃ devaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam  RKV 
mānuṣaṃ bhāvamāpannastataḥ siddhimavāpsyasi 
evamuktastu devena sahasrākṣeṇa dhīmatā  RKV 
praṇamya śirasā bhūmim āgato 'sau hyacetanaḥ 
narmadātaṭamāśritya karṣayannijavigraham  RKV 
vratopavāsasaṃkhinno japahomarataḥ sadā 
mahādevaṃ mahātmānaṃ varadaṃ śūlapāṇinam  RKV 
bhaktyā tu parayā rājanyāvadābhūtasamplavam 
aṃśāvataraṇād viṣṇoḥ sūto bhūtvā mahāmatiḥ  RKV 
toṣayan vai jagannāthaṃ tato yāto hi sadgatim  RKV 
eṣa tatsambhavastāta dārutīrthasya suvrata 
kathito 'yaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ yathā me śaṅkaro 'bravīt  RKV 
tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śrutvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ 
bhrātḥn vilokayāmāsa hṛṣṭaromā muhurmuhuḥ  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tasmiṃstīrthe naraḥ snātvā vidhipūrvaṃ nareśvara 
upāsya saṃdhyāṃ deveśamarcayedyaśca śaṅkaram  RKV 
vedābhyāsaṃ tu tatraiva yaḥ karoti samāhitaḥ 
so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ rājaṃllabhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
tasmiṃstīrthe tu yo bhaktyā bhojayed brāhmaṇāñchuciḥ 
sa tu viprasahasrasya labhate phalamuttamam  RKV 
snānaṃ dānaṃ japo homaḥ svādhyāyo devatārcanam 
yatkṛtaṃ śuddhabhāvena tatsarvaṃ saphalaṃ bhavet  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe dārukatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheta rājendra devatīrthamanuttamam 
yena devāstrayastriṃśat snātvā siddhiṃ parāṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kathaṃ tāta surāḥ sarve dānavairbalavattaraiḥ 
nirjitāstatra tīrthe ca snātvā siddhiṃ parāṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
purā daityagaṇairugrairyuddhe 'tibalavattaraiḥ 
indro devagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ svarājyāccyāvito nṛpa  RKV 
hastyaśvarathayānaughairmardayitvā varūthinīm 
vidhvastā bhejire mārgaṃ prahārair jarjarīkṛtāḥ  RKV 
jambhaśumbhaiśca kūṣmāṇḍakuhakādibhiḥ 
vepamānārditāḥ sarve brahmāṇamupatasthire  RKV 
praṇamya śirasā devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam 
tadā vijñāpayāmāsurdevā vahnipurogamāḥ  RKV 
paśya paśya mahābhāga dānavaiḥ śakalīkṛtāḥ 
viyojitāḥ putradāraistvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
paritrāyasva deveśa sarvalokapitāmaha 
nānyā gatiḥ sureśāna tvāṃ muktvā parameśvara  RKV 
brahmovāca
dānavānāṃ vighātārthaṃ narmadātaṭam āsthitāḥ 
tapaḥ kurudhvaṃ svasthāḥ stha tapo hi paramaṃ balam  RKV 
nānyopāyo na vai mantro vidyate na ca me kriyā 
vinā revājalaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram  RKV 
dāridryavyādhimaraṇabandhanavyasanāni ca 
etāni caiva pāpasya phalānīti matirmama  RKV 
evaṃ jñātvā tataścaiva tapaḥ kuruta duṣkaram 
tathā caiva surāḥ sarve devā hyagnipurogamāḥ  RKV 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tathyaṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
narmadām āgatāḥ sarve devā hyagnipurogamāḥ  RKV 
cerurvai tatra vipulaṃ tapaḥ siddhimavāpnuvan 
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ devatīrtham anuttamam  RKV 
gīyate triṣu lokeṣu sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram 
tatra gatvā ca yo martyo vidhinā saṃyatendriyaḥ  RKV 
snānaṃ samācaredbhaktyā sa labhenmauktikaṃ phalam 
yastu bhojayate viprāṃstasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa  RKV 
sa labhenmukhyaviprāṇāṃ phalaṃ sāhasrikaṃ nṛpa 
tatra devaśilā ramyā mahāpuṇyavivardhinī  RKV 
saṃnyāsena mṛtā ye tu teṣāṃ syād akṣayā gatiḥ 
agnipraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃs tīrthe narādhipa  RKV 
rudraloke vaset tāvad yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam 
evaṃ snānaṃ japo homaḥ svādhyāyo devatārcanam  RKV 
sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ vā 'pi tatra tīrthe 'kṣayaṃ bhavet 
eṣa te vidhiruddiṣṭa utpattiścaiva bhārata  RKV 
devatīrthasya nikhilā yathā vai śaṅkarācchrutā 
paṭhanti ye pāpaharaṃ sarvaduḥkhavimocanam  RKV 
devatīrthasya caritaṃ devalokaṃ vrajanti te  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe devatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheta rājendra guhāvāsīti cottamam 
yatra siddho mahādevo guhāvāsī samārbudam  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kena kāryeṇa bho tāta mahādevo jagadguruḥ 
guhāyām anayatkālaṃ sudīrghaṃ dvijasattama  RKV 
etadvistarataḥ sarvaṃ kathayasva mamānagha 
śrotumicchāmyahaṃ sarvaparaṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu praśno mahārāja pṛṣṭo yo vai tvayottamaḥ 
purāṇe vistaro hyasya na śakyo hi mayādhunā  RKV 
kathituṃ vṛddhabhāvatvādatīto bahukālikaḥ 
saṃkṣepāt tena te tāta kathayāmi nibodha me  RKV 
purā kṛtayuge rājannāsīd dāruvanaṃ mahat 
nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāvallyupaśobhitam  RKV 
siṃhavyāghravarāhaiśca gajaiḥ khaḍgairniṣevitam 
bahupakṣiyutaṃ divyaṃ yathā caitrarathaṃ vanam  RKV 
tatra kecin mahāprājñā vasanti saṃśitavratāḥ 
vasanti parayā bhaktyā caturāśramabhāvitāḥ  RKV 
brahmacārī gṛhasthaśca vānaprastho yatis tathā 
svadharmaniratāḥ sarve vāñchantaḥ paramaṃ padam  RKV 
tāvadvasantasamaye kasmiṃścit kāraṇāntare 
vimānastho mahādevo gacchanvai hyumayā saha  RKV 
dadarśa toya āvāsamṛksāmayajurnāditam 
alakṣyāgatanirgamyaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram  RKV 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā muditā devī harṣagaṅgadayā girā 
papraccha devadeveśaṃ śaśāṅkakṛtabhūṣaṇam  RKV 
devyuvāca
kasyāyamāśramo deva vedadhvaninināditaḥ 
yaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣutpipāsādyaiḥ śramaiśca parihīyate  RKV 
maheśvara uvāca
kiṃ tvayā na śrutaṃ devi mahādāruvanaṃ mahat 
bahuviprajano yatra gṛhadharmeṇa vartate  RKV 
atra yaḥ strījanaḥ kaścid bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ 
nānyo devo na vai dharmo jñāyate śailanandini  RKV 
etacchrutvā paraṃ vākyaṃ devadevena bhāṣitam 
kautūhalasamāviṣṭā śaṅkaraṃ punarabravīt  RKV 
yattvayoktaṃ mahādeva patidharmaratāḥ striyaḥ 
tāsāṃ tvaṃ madano bhūtvā cāritraṃ kṣobhaya prabho  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
yattvayoktaṃ ca vacanaṃ na hi me rocate priye 
brāhmaṇā hi mahadbhūtaṃ na caiṣāṃ vipriyaṃ caret  RKV 
manyupraharaṇā viprāścakrapraharaṇo hariḥ 
cakrātkrūrataro manyus tasmād vipraṃ na kopayet  RKV 
na te devā na te lokā na te nagā na cāsurāḥ 
dṛśyante triṣu lokeṣu ye tairdṛṣṭair na nāśitāḥ  RKV 
teṣāṃ mokṣas tathā svargo bhūmirmartye phalāni ca 
yeṣāṃ tuṣṭā mahābhāgā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣitidevatāḥ  RKV 
evaṃ jñātvā mahābhāge asadgrāhaṃ parityaja 
tatra loke viruddhaṃ vai kupyante yena vai dvijāḥ  RKV 
devyuvāca
nāhaṃ te dayitā deva nāhaṃ te vaśavartinī 
akṛtvādhaśva vai tāsāṃ mānaṃ surasupūjitam  RKV 
lokaloke mahādeva aśakyaṃ nāsti te prabho 
kriyatāṃ mama caivaikam etat kāryaṃ surottama  RKV 
evamukto mahādevo devyā vākyahite rataḥ 
kṛtvā kāpālikaṃ rūpaṃ yayau dāruvanaṃ prati  RKV 
mahāhitajaṭājūṭaṃ niyamya śaśibhūṣaṇam 
kaṇṭhatrāṇaṃ paraṃ kṛtvā dhārayan karṇakuṇḍale  RKV 
vyāghracarmaparīdhāno mekhalāhārabhūṣitaḥ 
nūpuradhvaninighoṣaiḥ kampayan vai vasuṃdharām  RKV 
mahānūrddhvajaṭāmālī kṛttibhasmānulepanaḥ 
kṛtvā haste kapālaṃ tu brahmaṇaśca mahātmanaḥ  RKV 
mahāḍamarughoṣeṇa kampayan vai vasuṃdharām 
prabhātasamaye prāpto mahādāruvanaṃ prati  RKV 
tāvat puṇyajanaḥ sarvapuṣpapatraphalārthikaḥ 
nirgato bahubhiḥ sārddhaṃ pavamānaḥ samantataḥ  RKV 
tad dṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryaṃ rūpaṃ devasya bhārata 
yuvatīnāṃ manas tāsāṃ kāmena kaluṣīkṛtam  RKV 
śobhanaṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvā api varāṅganāḥ 
kledabhāvaṃ tato jagmurmudā dāruvanastriyaḥ  RKV 
vikārā bahavastāsāṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahādbhutam 
saṃjātā viprapatnīnāṃ tadā tāsu narottama  RKV 
paridhānaṃ na jānanti kāścid dṛṣṭvā varāṅganāḥ 
uttarīyaṃ tathā cānyā mahāmohasamanvitāḥ  RKV 
keśabhāraparibhraṣṭā kācidevāsanotthitā 
dātukāmā tadā bhaikṣyaṃ ceṣṭituṃ naiva cāśakat  RKV 
kācid dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ rūpayauvanagarvitā 
utsaṅge saṃsthitaṃ bālaṃ vismṛtā pāyitum stanam  RKV 
kāmabāṇahatā cānyā bāhubhyāṃ pīḍya sustanau 
niḥśvasantī tadā coṣṇaṃ na kiṃcit pratijalpati  RKV 
evaṃ saṃkṣobhya taṃ sarvaṃ strījanaṃ parameśvaraḥ 
jagāma tatra vai tāsāṃ kṣobhaṃ kṛtvā mahādbhutam  RKV 
tāvat te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve bhramitvā kānanaṃ mahat 
āgatāḥ svagṛhe dārān dadṛśuś ca hataujasaḥ  RKV 
yāsāṃ pūrvatarā bhaktiḥ pātivratye patīnprati 
calitāstā viditvāśu nirjagmurdvijasattamāḥ  RKV 
saṃvidaṃ paramāṃ kṛtvā jñātvā devaṃ maheśvaram 
kṣobhayitvā manastāsāṃ tataścādarśanaṃ gatam  RKV 
krodhāviṣṭo dvijaḥ kaścid daṇḍamudyamya dhāvati 
kalmāṣayaṣṭimanye ca tathānye darbhamuṣṭikām  RKV 
itaścetaśca te sarve bhramitvā kānanaṃ nṛpa 
ekībhūtvā mahātmāno vyājahruśca ruṣā giram  RKV 
yad idaṃ ca hutaṃ kiṃcid guravas toṣitā yadi 
tena satyena devasya liṅgaṃ patatu cottamam  RKV 
āśramād āśramaṃ sarve na tyajāmo vidhikramāt 
tena satyena devasya liṅgaṃ patatu bhūtale  RKV 
evaṃ satyaprabhāvena triruktena dvijanmanām 
śivasya paśyato liṅgaṃ patitaṃ dharaṇītale  RKV 
hāhākāro mahānāsīllokāloke 'pi bhārata 
devasya patite liṅge jagataśca mahākṣaye  RKV 
patamānasya liṅgasya śabdo 'bhūcca sudāruṇaḥ 
ulkāpātā diśāṃ hāhā bhūmikampāśca dāruṇāḥ  RKV 
patanti parvatāgrāṇi śoṣaṃ yānti ca sāgarāḥ 
devasya patite liṅge devā vimanaso 'bhavan  RKV 
sametya sahitāḥ sarve brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam 
kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve stuvanti vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ  RKV 
tatas tuṣṭo jagannāthaś caturvadanapaṅkajaḥ 
ārtānprāha surānsarvānmā viṣādaṃ gamiṣyatha  RKV 
brahmaśāpābhibhūto 'sau devadevastrilocanaḥ 
tuṣṭaistaistapasā yuktaiḥ punarmokṣaṃ gamiṣyati  RKV 
etacchrutvā yayurdevā yathāgatamarindama 
bhāvayitvā tataḥ sarve munayaścaiva bhārata  RKV 
viśvāmitravasiṣṭhādyā jābāliratha kaśyapaḥ 
sametya sahitāḥ sarve tamūcus tripurāntakam  RKV 
brahmatejo hi balavaddvijānāṃ hi sureśvara 
kṣāntiyuktastapastaptvā bhaviṣyasi gataklamaḥ  RKV 
yataḥ kṣobhādṛṣīṇāṃ ca tadevaṃ liṅgamuttamam 
patitaṃ te mahādeva na tatpūjyaṃ bhaviṣyati  RKV 
na tacchreyo 'gnihotreṇa nāgniṣṭomena labhyate 
prāpnuvanti ca yacchreyo mānavā liṅgapūjane  RKV 
devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām 
vacanena tu viprāṇām etat pūjyaṃ bhaviṣyati  RKV 
brahmaviṣṇvindracandrāṇām etat pūjyaṃ bhaviṣyati 
yatphalaṃ tava liṅgasya iha loke paratra ca  RKV 
evamukto jagannāthaḥ praṇipatya dvijottamān 
mudā paramayā yuktaḥ kṛtāñjalir abhāṣata  RKV 
brāhmaṇā jaṅgamaṃ tīrthaṃ nirjalaṃ sārvakāmikam 
yeṣāṃ vākyodakenaiva śudhyanti malino janāḥ  RKV 
na tatkṣetraṃ na tattīrthamūṣaraṃ puṣkarāṇi ca 
brāhmaṇe manyumutpādya yatra gatvā sa śudhyati  RKV 
na tacchāstraṃ yanna viprapraṇītaṃ na tad dānaṃ yanna viprapradeyam 
na tatsaukhyaṃ yannavipraprasādānna tadduḥkhaṃ yanna vipraprakopāt  RKV 
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni gaṅgādyāḥ saritas tathā 
ekasya vipravākyasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  RKV 
abhinandya dvijānsarvānanujñāto maharṣibhiḥ 
tato 'gamat tadā devo narmadātaṭamuttamam  RKV 
paramaṃ vratamāsthāya guhāvāsī samārbudam 
tapaścacāra bhagavāñjapasnānarataḥ sadā  RKV 
samāpte niyame tāta sthāpayitvā maheśvaram 
vandyamānaḥ suraiḥ sārddhaṃ kailāsamagamat prabhuḥ  RKV 
narmadāyās taṭe tena sthāpitaḥ parameśvaraḥ 
tenaiva kāraṇenāsau narmadeśvara ucyate  RKV 
yo 'rcayennarmadeśānaṃ yatir vai saṃjitendriyaḥ 
snātvā caiva mahādevam aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
dadāti yaḥ pitṛbhyastu tilapuṣpakuśodakam 
triḥsaptapūrvajāstasya svarge modanti pāṇḍava  RKV 
yastu bhojayate viprāṃs tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa 
pāyasaṃ ghṛtamiśraṃ tu sa labhet koṭijaṃ phalam  RKV 
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vāpi brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira 
dadāti toyamadhyasthaḥ so 'gniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
aṣṭamyāṃvā caturdaśyāṃ nirāhāro vaset tu yaḥ 
narmadeśvaramāsādya prāpnuyājjanmanaḥ phalam  RKV 
agnipraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa 
tasya vyādhibhayaṃ na syāt saptajanmasu bhārata  RKV 
anāśakaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa 
anivartikā gatis tasya rudraloke bhaviṣyati  RKV 
eṣa te vidhir uddiṣṭas tasyotpattir narottama 
purāṇe vihitā tāta saṃjñā tasya tu vistarāt  RKV 
etaṃ kīrtayate yastu narmadeśvarasambhavam 
bhaktyā śṛṇoti ca naraḥ so 'pi snānaphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye narmadeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ  
nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchecca rājendra kapilātīrthamuttamam 
snānamātrānnaro bhaktyā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
āścaryabhūtaṃ lokeṣu kathitaṃ dvijasattama 
narmadeśvaramāhātmyaṃ kāpilaṃ kathayasva me  RKV 
yasmin kāle 'tha sambandhe utpannaṃ tīrtham uttamam 
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ tīrthaṃ jātaṃ kathaṃ prabho  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu vakṣye'dya te rājankapilātīrthamuttamam 
yena te vismayaḥ sarvaḥ śrutvā gacchati bhārata  RKV 
purā kṛtayugasyādau brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
utpādayitvā sakalaṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham  RKV 
japahomaparo bhaktyā kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā ca tiṣṭhati 
jvalamānāt tu kapilā tāvat kuṇḍātsamutthitā  RKV 
agnijvālojjvalaiḥ śṛṅgaistrinetrā supayasvinī 
agnipūrṇā hyagnimukhā agnighrāṇāgnilocanā  RKV 
agnikhurā hyagnipṛṣṭhā agnisarvāṅgasaṃsthitiḥ 
sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇā ghaṇṭālalitaniḥsvanā  RKV 
dṛṣṭvā tu tāṃ mahābhāgāṃ kapilāṃ kuṇḍamadhyagām 
brahmā lokagurustāta praṇamyedam uvāca ha  RKV 
namaste kapile puṇye sarvalokanamaskṛte 
maṅgalye maṅgale devi triṣu lokeṣvanupame  RKV 
tvaṃ lakṣmīstvaṃ smṛtirmedhā tvaṃ dhṛtistvaṃ varānane 
umādevīti vikhyātā tvaṃ satī nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
vaiṣṇavī tvaṃ mahādevī brahmāṇī tvaṃ varānane 
kumārī tvaṃ mahābhāge bhaktiḥ śraddhā tathaiva ca  RKV 
kālarātristu bhūtānāṃ kumārī parameśvarī 
tvaṃ lavastvaṃ truṭiścaiva muhūrtaṃ lakṣameva ca  RKV 
saṃvatsarastvaṃ māsastvaṃ kālastvaṃ ca kṣaṇastathā 
nāsti kiṃcit tvayā hīnaṃ trailokye sacarācare  RKV 
evaṃ stutā tu mānena kapilā parameṣṭhinā 
tamuvāca mahābhāgaṃ prahṛṣya padmasambhavam  RKV 
prasannā tava vākyena devadeva jagadguro 
kiṃ karomi priyaṃ te 'dya brūhi sarvaṃ pitāmaha  RKV 
brahmovāca
jagaddhitāya janitā mayā tvaṃ parameśvari 
svargānmartyaṃ tato yāhi lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  RKV 
sarvadevamayī tvaṃ tu sarvalokamayī tathā 
vidhinā ye pradāsyanti teṣāṃ vāsastriviṣṭape  RKV 
evamuktvā tato devī brahmāṇaṃ parameśvarī 
vandyamānā suraiḥ siddhair ājagāma dharātalam  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
yadāyāteha sā tāta brāhmaṇo vacanācchubhā 
tadā devāśca lokāśca kathamaṅgeṣu saṃsthitāḥ  RKV 
kathaṃ vā saṃsthitāgatya kapilā sā dvijottama 
tīrthe vā hyūṣare kṣetra etanme kathaya dvija  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sā tadā brahmaṇā coktā dhātrā lokasya bhārata 
brahmalokādgatā puṇyāṃ narmadāṃ lokapāvanīm  RKV 
tapaḥ kṛtvā suvipulaṃ narmadātaṭam āśritā 
cacāra pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ saśailavanakānanām  RKV 
tadāprabhṛti rājendra kapilātīrtham uttamam 
sarvapāpaharaṃ khyātamṛṣisaṅghair niṣevitam  RKV 
tattīrthe vidhivat snātvā kapilāyāḥ prayacchati 
pṛthvī tena bhaveddattā saśailavanakānanā  RKV 
tāṃ tu paśyati yo bhaktyā dīyamānāṃ dvijottame 
tasya varṣaśataṃ pāpaṃ naśyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahaścaiva janaḥ satyaṃ tapastathā 
te tatpṛṣṭhaṃ samāśritya sthitā lokā nṛpottama  RKV 
mukhe hyagniḥ sthito devo danteṣu ca bhujaṅgamāḥ 
dhātā vidhātā hyoṣṭhau ca jihvāyāṃ tu sarasvatī  RKV 
sahasrakiraṇau devau candrādityau sulocanau 
nāsikāmadhyagaścaiva māruto nṛpasattama  RKV 
lalāṭe tu mahādevo hyaśvinau karṇasaṃsthitau 
naranārāyaṇau śṛṅge śṛṅgamadhye pitāmahaḥ  RKV 
kambalo 'dhigatas tāta pāśadhṛg varuṇas tathā 
yamaśca bhagavāndeva āśritya codaraṃ śritaḥ  RKV 
khureṣu pannagāścaivaṃ pucchāgre sūryaraśmayaḥ 
evambhūtāṃ hi kapilāṃ sarvadevamayīṃ nṛpa  RKV 
ye dhārayanti ca gṛhe dhanyāste nātra saṃśayaḥ 
prātar utthāya yastasyāḥ kurute tu pradakṣiṇām  RKV 
pradakṣiṇā kṛtā tena saśailavanakānanā 
kapilāpañcagavyena yaḥ snāpayati śaṅkaram  RKV 
upavāsaparo yastu tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa 
snātvā hyuktavidhānena tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ  RKV 
tasya te vaṃśajāḥ sarve daśa pūrve daśāpare 
tṛptā rohanti vai svarge dhyāyanto 'sya manorathān  RKV 
eṣa te vidhiruddiṣṭaḥ sambhavo nṛpasattama 
tīrthasya ca phalaṃ puṇyaṃ kimanyat paripṛcchasi  RKV 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ sarvaduḥkhaghnamuttamam 
yacchrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śrīnarmadāmāhātmye kapilātīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra karañjeśvaram uttamam 
yatra siddho mahābhāgo daityo lokeṣu viśrutaḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
yo 'sau siddho mahābhāga tatra tīrthe mahātapāḥ 
kasya putraḥ kathaṃ siddhaḥ kasminkāle vada dvija  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
purā kṛtayuge rājanmānaso brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ 
vedavedāṅgatattvajño marīcirnāma nāmataḥ  RKV 
tasyāpi tapaso rāśeḥ kālena mahatānagha 
putro 'tha mānaso jātaḥ sākṣād brahmeva cāparaḥ  RKV 
kṣamā damo dayā dānaṃ satyaṃ śaucam athārjavam 
marīceśca guṇā hyete santi tasya ca bhārata  RKV 
evaṃ guṇagaṇākīrṇaṃ kaśyapaṃ dvijasattamam 
jñātvā prajāpatir dakṣo bhāryārthe svasutāṃ dadau  RKV 
aditirditirdanuścaiva tathāpyevaṃ daśāparāḥ 
yāsāṃ putrāśca saṃjātāḥ pautrāśca bharatarṣabha  RKV 
aditirjanayāmāsa putrān indrapurogamān 
jātāstasya mahābāho kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ  RKV 
yaistu lokatrayaṃ vyāptaṃ sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ mahat 
tathānyasya mahābhāgo danoḥ putro vyajāyata  RKV 
sarvalakṣaṇasampannaḥ karañjo nāma nāmataḥ 
bāla eva mahābhāga cacāra sa mahattapaḥ  RKV 
narmadātaṭamāśritya cātighoram anuttamam 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ ca kṛcchracāndrāyaṇaṃ nṛpa  RKV 
śākamūlaphalāhāraḥ snānahomaparāyaṇaḥ 
tatastuṣṭo mahādeva umayā sahitaḥ kila  RKV 
vareṇa chandayāmāsa tripurāntakaraḥ prabhuḥ 
bhoḥ karañja mahāsattva parituṣṭo 'smi te 'nagha  RKV 
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva te dadmi hyamaratvamṛte mama  RKV 
karañja uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo mahādeva yadi deyo varo mama 
tarhi putrāśca pautrāśca santu me dharmavatsalāḥ  RKV 
tathetyuktvā mahādeva umayā sahitas tadā 
vṛṣārūḍho gaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata  RKV 
gate cādarśanaṃ deve so 'pi daityo mudānvitaḥ 
svanāmnātra mahādevaṃ sthāpayitvā yayau gṛham  RKV 
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ sarvatīrtheṣvanuttamam 
snānamātrānarastatra mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ 
so 'gniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam  RKV 
anāśakaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa 
anivartyā gatistasya rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  RKV 
athavāgnijale prāṇānyastyajed dharmanandana 
ayutadvitayaṃ vaste varṣāṇāṃ śivamandire  RKV 
tataścaiva kṣaye jāte jāyate vimale kule 
vedavedāṅgatattvajñaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ  RKV 
rājā vā rājatulyo vā jīvecca śaradaḥ śatam 
putrapautrasamopetaḥ sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ  RKV 
evaṃ te sarvamākhyātaṃ pṛṣṭaṃ yadyattvayānagha 
tīrthasya tu phalaṃ tasya snānadāneṣu bhārata  RKV 
etatpuṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam 
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam  RKV 
yastu śrāvayate śrāddhe paṭhet pitṛparāyaṇaḥ 
akṣayaṃ jāyate puṇyamityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye karañjeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ  
nāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchecca rājendra kuṇḍaleśvaramuttamam 
yatra siddho mahāyakṣaḥ kuṇḍadhāro nṛpottama  RKV 
tapaḥ kṛtvā suvipulaṃ surāsurabhayaṃkaram 
paulastyamandire caiva cikrīḍa nṛpasattama  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kasminyuge samutpannaḥ kasya putro mahāmatiḥ 
tapastaptvā suvipulaṃ toṣito yena śaṅkaraḥ  RKV 
etadvistaratastāta kathayasva mamānagha 
śṛṇvataśca na tṛptir me kathāmṛtamanuttamam  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tretāyuge brahmasamaḥ paulastyonāma viśravāḥ 
tapaḥ kṛtvā suvipulaṃ bharadvājasutodbhavaḥ  RKV 
putraṃ pautragaṇair yuktaṃ patnyā bhaktyā sutoṣitaḥ 
dhanadaṃ janayāmāsa sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam  RKV 
jātamātraṃ tu taṃ jñātvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
cakāra nāma suprīta ṛṣidevasamanvitaḥ  RKV 
yasmād viśravaso jāto mama pautratvam āgataḥ 
tasmād vaiśravaṇo nāma tava dattaṃ mayānagha  RKV 
tathā tvaṃ sarvadevānāṃ dhanagoptā bhaviṣyasi 
caturtho lokapālānāmakṣayaścāvyayo bhuvi  RKV 
tasya bhāryā mahārāja īśvarīti ca viśrutā 
yakṣo yakṣādhipaḥ śreṣṭhastasya kuṇḍo 'bhavat sutaḥ  RKV 
sa ca rūpaṃ paraṃ prāpya mātāpitroranujñayā 
tapaś cacāra vipulaṃ narmadātaṭamāśritaḥ  RKV 
grīṣme pañcāgnisaṃtapto varṣāsu sthaṇḍileśayaḥ 
hemante jalamadhyastho vāyubhakṣaḥ śataṃ samāḥ  RKV 
evaṃ varṣaśate pūrṇe ekāṅguṣṭhe 'bhavan nṛpa 
asthibhūtaḥ paraṃ tāta ūrdhvabāhustataḥ param  RKV 
atapacca ghṛtaśvāsaḥ kuṇḍalo bharatarṣabha 
caturthe varṣaśatake tutoṣa vṛṣavāhanaḥ  RKV 
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bho vatsa yatte manasi rocate 
dadāmi te na sandehastapasā toṣito hyaham  RKV 
kuṇḍala uvāca
yakṣādhipaprasādena tasyaivānucaraḥ pure 
vicarāmi yathākāmamavadhyaḥ sarvaśatruṣu  RKV 
tathetyuktvā mahādevaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ 
jagāmākāśamāviśya kailāsaṃ dharaṇīdharam  RKV 
gate cādarśanaṃ deve so 'pi yakṣo mudānvitaḥ 
sthāpayāmāsa deveśaṃ kuṇḍaleśvaramuttamam  RKV 
alaṃkṛtvā jagannāthaṃ puṣpadhūpānulepanaiḥ 
vimānaiścāmaraiśchatrais tathā vai liṅgapūraṇaiḥ  RKV 
tarpayitvā dvijānsamyagannapānādibhūṣaṇaiḥ 
prīṇayitvā mahādevaṃ tataḥ svabhavanaṃ yayau  RKV 
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam 
uttamaṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ kuṇḍaleśvaranāmataḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścid upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ 
arcayed devamīśānaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  RKV 
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vāpi maṇiṃ mauktikameva ca 
dadyād bhojyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sa sukhī modate divi  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā ṛgyajuḥsāmago 'pi vā 
ṛcamekāṃ japitvā tu sakalaṃ phalamaśnute  RKV 
gāṃ prayacchati viprebhyastatphalaṃ śṛṇu pāṇḍava 
yāvanti tasyā romāṇi tatprasūtikuleṣu ca  RKV 
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate 
svarge vāso bhavettasya putrapautraiḥ samanvitaḥ  RKV 
tāvanti varṣāṇi mahānubhāvaḥ svarge vaset putrapautraiśca sārddham 
tatrānnado yāti maheśalokamasaṃkhyavarṣāṇi na saṃśayo 'tra  RKV 
sa vai sukhī modate svargaloke gandharvasiddhāpsaraḥsampragīte 
evaṃ tu te dharmasuta prabhāvastīrthasya sarvaḥ kathitaśca pārtha  RKV 
śrutvā stuvanmucyate sarvapāpaiḥ punastrilokīm iha tatprabhāvāt  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye kuṇḍaleśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ  
nāmaikacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra pippaleśvaramuttamam 
yatra siddho mahāyogī pippalādo mahātapāḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
pippalādasya caritaṃ śrotumicchāmyahaṃ vibho 
māhātmyaṃ tasya tīrthasya yatra siddho mahātapāḥ  RKV 
kasya putro mahābhāga kimarthaṃ kṛtavāṃstapaḥ 
etadvistarataḥ sarvaṃ kathayasva mamānagha  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
mithilāstho mahābhāgo vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ 
yājñavalkyaḥ purā tāta cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ  RKV 
tāpasī tasya bhaginī yājñavalkyasya dhīmataḥ 
sā saptame 'pi varṣe ca vaidhavyaṃ prāpa daivataḥ  RKV 
pūrvakarmavipākena hīnābhūtpitṛmātṛtaḥ 
nābhūttatpatipakṣe 'pi ko'pītyekākinī sthitā  RKV 
bhūmau bhramantī bhrātuḥ sā samīpamagamacchanaiḥ 
cacāra ca tapaḥ so 'pi paralokasukhepsayā  RKV 
cacāra sāpi tatrasthā śuśrūṣantī mahattapaḥ 
kasmiṃścit samaye sātha snātāhani rajasvalā  RKV 
antarvāso dhṛtavatī dṛṣṭvā karpaṭakaṃ rahaḥ 
yājñavalkyo 'pi tadrātrau supto yatra susaṃvṛtaḥ  RKV 
svapnaṃ dṛṣṭvātyajacchukraṃ kaupīne raktabinduvat 
virājitena tapasā siddhaṃ tadanalaprabham  RKV 
yāvatprabuddho vipro 'sau vīkṣyocchiṣṭaṃ tad aṃśukam 
cikṣepa dūrato 'spṛśyaṃ śaucaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ  RKV 
niṣiddhaṃ tu niśi snānamiti suṣvāpa sa dvijaḥ 
niśīthe sāpi tadvastraṃ bhagasyāvaraṇaṃ vyadhāt  RKV 
prātar anveṣayāmāsa munirvastramitastataḥ 
tataḥ sā brāhmaṇī prāha kiṃ anveṣayase prabho 
kena kāryaṃ tava tathā vadasva mama tattvataḥ  RKV 
yājñavalkya uvāca
apavitro mayā bhadre svapno dṛṣṭo 'dya vai niśi 
sakledaṃ tatra me vastraṃ nikṣiptaṃ tanna dṛśyate  RKV 
tacchrutvā brāhmaṇī vākyaṃ bhītabhītāvadan nṛpa 
tadvastraṃ tu mayā vipra snātvā hyantaḥ kṛtaṃ mahat  RKV 
tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā hāhetyuktvā mahāmuniḥ 
nipapāta tadā bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥ  RKV 
kimetaditi setyuktvā hyākāśamiva nirmalā 
āśvāsayantī taṃ vipraṃ provāca vacanaṃ tadā  RKV 
vadasva kāraṇaṃ tāta guhyād guhyataraṃ yadi 
pratīkāro 'sya yenaiva vimṛśya kriyate tvarā  RKV 
tataḥ sa suciraṃ dhyātvā labdhavāgvai tataḥ kṣaṇam 
provāca sādhvasamanā yattacchṛṇu nareśvara  RKV 
nātra doṣo 'sti te kaścinmama caiva śubhavrate 
tavodare tu garbho yastatra daivaṃ parāyaṇam  RKV 
tasya tattvena rakṣā ca tvayā kāryā sadaiva hi 
vināśī naiva kartavyo yāvatkālasya paryayaḥ  RKV 
tatheti vrīḍitā sādhvī dūyamānena cetasā 
apālayacca taṃ garbhaṃ yāvatputro hyajāyata  RKV 
jātamātraṃ ca taṃ garbhaṃ gṛhītvā brāhmaṇī ca sā 
aśvatthacchāyām āśritya tam utsṛjya vaco 'bravīt  RKV 
yāni sattvāni lokeṣu sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca 
tāni sarvāṇi rakṣantu tyaktaṃ vai bālakaṃ mayā  RKV 
evamuktvā gatā sā tu brāhmaṇī nṛpasattama 
tathāgataḥ sa tu śiśus tatra sthitvā muhūrtakam  RKV 
pāṇipādau vinikṣipya nikuñcya nayane śubhe 
āsyaṃ tu vikṛtaṃ kṛtvā ruroda vikṛtaiḥ svaraiḥ  RKV 
tena śabdena vitrastāḥ sthāvarā jaṅgamāśca ye 
ākampitā mahotpātaiḥ saśailavanakānanā  RKV 
tato jñātvā mahadbhūtaṃ kṣudhāviṣṭaṃ dvijarṣabham 
na jahāti nagaśchāyāṃ pānārthāya tataḥ param 
apibacca sutaṃ tasmādabhṛtaṃ caiva bhārata  RKV 
evaṃ sa vardhitas tatra kumāro nijacetasi 
cintayāmāsa viśrabdhaḥ kiṃ mama grahagocaram  RKV 
tataḥ krūrasabhācāraḥ krūraṃ dṛṣṭvā nirīkṣitaḥ 
papāta sahasā bhūmau śanaiścārī śanaiścaraḥ  RKV 
uvāca ca bhayatrastaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭastadā 
kiṃ mayāpakṛtaṃ vipra pippalāda mahāmune  RKV 
caranvai gaganād yena pātito dharaṇītale 
sauriṇā hyevamuktastu pippalādo mahāmuniḥ  RKV 
krodharūpo 'bravīdvākyaṃ tacchṛṇuṣva narādhipa 
pitṛmātṛvihīnasya mama bālasya durmate 
pīḍāṃ karoṣi kasmāt tvaṃ saure brūhi hyaśeṣataḥ  RKV 
śanaiścara uvāca
krūrasvabhāvaḥ sahajo mama dṛṣṭistathedṛśī 
muñcasva māṃ tathā kartā yadbravīṣi na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
pippalāda uvāca
adyaprabhṛti bālānāṃ varṣād ā ṣoḍaśādgraha 
pīḍā tvayā na kartavyā eṣa te samayaḥ kṛtaḥ  RKV 
evamastviti coktvā sa jagāma punarāgataḥ 
devamārgaṃ śanaiścārī praṇamya ṛṣisattamam  RKV 
gate cādarśanaṃ tatra so 'pi bālo mahāgrahaḥ 
vicintayanvai pitaraṃ krodhena kaluṣīkṛtaḥ  RKV 
āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ dhyātvā janayāmāsa pāvakam 
kṛtyāmantrairjuhāvāgnau kṛtyā vai saṃbhavatviti  RKV 
tāvajjhaṭiti sā kanyā jvālāmālāvibhūṣitā 
hutabhuksadṛśākārā kiṃ karomīti cābravīt  RKV 
śoṣayāmi samudrān kiṃ cūrṇayāmi ca parvatān 
avaniṃ veṣṭayāmīti pātaye kiṃ nabhastalam  RKV 
kasya mūrdhni patiṣyāmi ghātayāmi ca kaṃ dvija 
śīghramādiśyatāṃ kāryaṃ mā me kālātyayo bhavet  RKV 
tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā pippalādo mahātapāḥ 
krodhasaṃraktanayana idaṃ vacanam abravīt  RKV 
mahatā krodhavegena mayā tvaṃ cintitā śubhe 
pitā me yājñavalkyaśca tasya tvaṃ pata māciram  RKV 
evamuktvāgamacchīghraṃ sphoṭayantī nabhastalam 
mithilāstho mahāprājñastapastepe mahāmanāḥ  RKV 
yāvatpaśyati digbhāgaṃ jvalanārkasamaprabham 
yājñavalkyo mahātejā mahadbhūtamupasthitam  RKV 
tad dṛṣṭvā sahasāyāntaṃ bhītabhīto mahāmuniḥ 
anuyukto 'tha bhūtena janakaṃ nṛpatiṃ yayau  RKV 
śaraṇyaṃ mām anuprāptaṃ viddhi tvaṃ nṛpasattama 
mahadbhūtabhayādrakṣa yadi śaknoṣi pārthiva  RKV 
brahmatejobhavaṃ bhūtamanivāryaṃ durāsadam 
na ca śaknomyahaṃ trātuṃ rājā vacanam abravīt  RKV 
tataścānyaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭhaṃ śaraṇārthī mahātapāḥ 
jagāma tena mukto 'sau cendrasya sadanaṃ bhayāt  RKV 
devarāja namaste 'stu mahābhūtabhayānnṛpa 
kampamāno 'bravīd vipro rakṣasveti punaḥpunaḥ  RKV 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā devarājo 'bravīd idam 
na śaknomi paritrātuṃ brahmakopādahaṃ mune  RKV 
tataḥ sa brahmabhavanaṃ brāhmaṇo brahmavittamaḥ 
jagāma viṣṇulokaṃ ca tenāpītyukta eva saḥ  RKV 
tataḥ sa munirudvigno nirāśo jīvite nṛpa 
anugamyamāno bhūtena agacchacchaṅkarālayam  RKV 
tasya yogabalopeto mahādevasya pāṇḍava 
nakhamāṃsāntare gupto yathā devo na paśyati  RKV 
tadante cāgamadbhūtaṃ jvalanārkasamaprabham 
muñca muñceti puruṣaṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram  RKV 
evamukto mahādevas tena bhūtena bhārata 
yogīndraṃ darśayāmāsa nakhamāṃsāntare tadā  RKV 
saṃsthāpya bhūtaṃ bhūteśaḥ paramāpadgataṃ munim 
uvāca mā bhaistvaṃ vipra nirgacchasva mahāmune  RKV 
tataḥ susūkṣmadehasthaṃ bhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvābravīdidam 
kimasya tvaṃ mahābhūta kariṣyasi vadasva me  RKV 
kṛtyovāca
krodhāviṣṭena deveśa pippalādena cintitā 
asya dehaṃ haniṣyāmi hiṃsārthaṃ viddhi māṃ prabho  RKV 
etacchrutvā mahādevo bhūtasya vadanāccyutam 
kaṭisthaṃ yājñavalkyaṃ ca mantrayāmāsa mantravit  RKV 
yogīśvareti viprasya kṛtvā nāma yudhiṣṭhira 
visarjayitvā deveśastatraivāntaradhīyata  RKV 
preṣayitvā tu taṃ bhūtaṃ pippalādo 'pi durmanāḥ 
pitṛmātṛsamudvigno narmadātaṭamāśritaḥ  RKV 
ekāṅguṣṭho nirāhāro varṣād ā ṣoḍaśān nṛpa 
toṣayāmāsa deveśamumayā saha śaṅkaram  RKV 
tatastattapasā tuṣṭaḥ śaṅkaro vākyamabravīt  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
parituṣṭo 'smi te vipra tapasānena suvrata 
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva te dadmi manasā cepsitaṃ śubham  RKV 
pippalāda uvāca
yadi me bhagavāṃs tuṣṭo yadi deyo varo mama 
atra saṃnihito deva tīrthe bhava maheśvara  RKV 
evamuktastathetyuktvā pippalādaṃ mahāmunim 
jagāmādarśanaṃ devo bhūtasaṅghasamanvitaḥ  RKV 
pippalādo gate deve snātvā tatra mahāmbhasi 
sthāpayitvā mahādevaṃ jagāmottaraparvatam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe naro bhaktyā snātvā mantrayutaṃ nṛpa 
tarpayitvā pitḥn devān pūjayecca maheśvaram  RKV 
aśvamedhasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam 
mṛto rudrapuraṃ yāti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
atha yo bhojayed viprān pitḥn uddiśya bhārata 
tasya te dvādaśābdāni modante divi tarpitāḥ  RKV 
saṃnyāsena tu yaḥ kaścit tatra tīrthe tanuṃ tyajet 
anivartikā gatistasya rudralokāt kadācana  RKV 
etatsarvaṃ samākhyātaṃ yatpṛṣṭhe hi tvayānagha 
māhātmyaṃ pippalādasya tīrthasyotpattireva ca  RKV 
etatpuṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam 
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye pippalādatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma  
dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra vimaleśvaram uttamam 
tatra devaśilā ramyā svayaṃ devair vinirmitā  RKV 
tatra snātvā tu yo bhaktyā brāhmaṇānpūjayen nṛpa 
svalpenāpi hi dānena tasya cānto na vidyate  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kāni dānāni viprendra śastāni dharaṇītale 
yāni dattvā naro bhaktyā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ maṇimauktikameva ca 
bhūmidānaṃ ca godānaṃ mocayat paśubhānnaram  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścitkurute prāṇasaṃkṣayam 
rudraloke vaset tāvad yāvad ā bhūtasamplavam  RKV 
tataḥ puṣkariṇīṃ gacchet sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarīm 
tatra snātvārcayeddevaṃ tejorāśiṃ divākaram  RKV 
ṛcamekāṃ japet sāmnaḥ sāmavedaphalaṃ labhet 
yajurvedasya japanād ṛgvedasya tathaiva ca  RKV 
akṣaraṃ vā japen mantraṃ dhyāyamāno divākaram 
ādityahṛdayaṃ japtvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā vidhinā japeddvijān 
tasya koṭiguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
anāśakenāgnigatyā jale vā dehapātanāt 
tasmiṃstīrthe mṛto yastu sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  RKV 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā nṛpasattama 
vihitaṃ karma kurvāṇaḥ sa gacchet paramāṃ gatim  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
vyādhiṃ sattvakṣayaṃ mohaṃ jñātvā varṇā dvijottama 
pāpebhyo vipramucyante kena tatsādhanaṃ vada  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tilodakī tilasnāyī kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ 
brāhmaṇo 'naśanaiḥ prāṇāṃs tyajallabhati sadgatim  RKV 
saṅgrāme sadgatiṃ tāta kṣatriyo nidhane labhet 
tadabhāvānmahāprājña sevamāno labhed iti  RKV 
vyādhigrahagṛhīto vā vṛddho vā vikalendriyaḥ 
ātmānaṃ dāhayitvāgnau vidhinā sadgatiṃ labhet  RKV 
vaiśyo 'pi hi tyajanprāṇānevaṃ vai śubhabhāg bhavet 
jale vā śuddhabhāvena tyaktvā prāṇāñchivo bhavet  RKV 
śūdro 'pi dvijaśuśrūṣustoṣayitvā maheśvaram 
vimucya nānyathā pāpaḥ patate narake dhruvam  RKV 
athavā praṇavāśakto dvijebhyo gurave tathā 
pañcāgnau śoṣayeddehamāpṛcchya dvijasattamān  RKV 
śāntadāntajitakrodhāñchāstrayuktān vicakṣaṇān 
teṣāṃ caivopadeśena karīṣāgniṃ prasādhayet  RKV 
evaṃ varṇā yathātvena mūḍhāhaṅkāramohitāḥ 
patanti narake ghore yathāndho girigahvare  RKV 
ye śāstravidhimutsṛjya vartante kāmacārataḥ 
kṛmiyoniṃ prapadyante teṣāṃ piṇḍo na ca kriyā  RKV 
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ tyaktvā yathecchācārasevinaḥ 
aṣṭāviṃśatirvai koṭyo narakāṇāṃ yudhiṣṭhira  RKV 
pratyekaṃ vā patantyete magnā narakasāgare 
durlabhaṃ mānuṣaṃ janma bahudharmārjitaṃ nṛpa  RKV 
tallabdhvā madamātsaryaṃ yo vai tyajati mānavaḥ 
saṃniyamya sadātmānaṃ jñānacakṣur naro hi saḥ  RKV 
ajñānatimirāndhasya jñānāṃjanaśalākayā  RKV 
yasya nonmīlitaṃ cakṣurjñeyo jātyandha eva saḥ 
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭaṃ nṛpasattama  RKV 
tathāniṣṭatarāṇāṃ hi rudrasya vacanaṃ yathā 
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā rudradehād viniḥsṛtā  RKV 
tārayet sarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca 
sarvadevādhidevena īśvareṇa mahātmanā  RKV 
lokānāṃ ca hitārthāya mahāpuṇyāvatāritā 
mānasaṃ vācikaṃ pāpaṃ snānānnaśyati karmajam  RKV 
rudradehādviniṣkrāntā tena puṇyatamā hi sā 
prātarutthāya yo nityaṃ bhūmimākramya bhaktitaḥ  RKV 
etanmantraṃ japettāta snānasya labhate phalam 
namaḥ puṇyajale devi namaḥ sāgaragāmini  RKV 
namo'stu pāpanirmoce namo devi varānane  RKV 
namo 'stu te ṛṣivarasaṅghasevite namo 'stu te trinayanadehaniḥsṛte 
namo 'stu te sukṛtavatāṃ sadā vare namo 'stu te satatapavitrapāvani  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe vimaleśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ tacchṛṇuṣva narādhipa 
revāyā dakṣiṇe kūle nirmitaṃ śūlapāṇinā  RKV 
mokṣārthaṃ mānavendrāṇāṃ nirmitaṃ nṛpasattama 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutā me vividhā dharmāstīrthāni vividhāni ca 
dānadharmāḥ samastāśca tvatprasādāddvijottama  RKV 
anyacca śrotumicchāmi saṃsāraśchidyate yathā 
punarāgamanaṃ nāsti mokṣaprāptirbhaved yathā  RKV 
etadākhyāhi me sarvaṃ prasādād dvijasattama  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇuṣvaikamanā bhūtvā tīrthāt tīrthāntaraṃ mahat 
śrute yasya prabhāve tu mucyate cābdikādaghāt  RKV 
vācikairmānasairvāpi śārīraiśca viśeṣataḥ 
kīrtanāt tasya tīrthasya mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
pañcakrośapramāṇaṃ tu tacca tīrthaṃ mahīpate 
bhuktimuktipradaṃ divyaṃ prāṇināṃ pāpakarmiṇām  RKV 
revāyā dakṣiṇe kūle parvato bhṛgusaṃjñitaḥ 
tasya mūrdhni ca tattīrthaṃ sthāpitaṃ caiva śambhunā  RKV 
śūlabhedeti vikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu bhūpate 
tatra sthitāśca ye vṛkṣāstīrthāccaiva caturdiśam  RKV 
patitā nilayaṃ yānti rudrasya nātra saṃśayaḥ 
mṛtāstatraiva ye kecij jantavo bhuvi pakṣiṇaḥ  RKV 
te yānti paramaṃ lokaṃ tatra tīrthe na saṃśayaḥ 
pātālān niḥsṛtā gaṅgā bhogavatītisaṃjñitā  RKV 
niṣkrāntā śūlabhedāc ca sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī 
yā sā gīrvāṇanāmnyanyā vahet puṇyā mahānadī  RKV 
patitā kuṇḍamadhye tu yatra bhinnaṃ triśūlinā 
śambhunā ca purā tāta utpādya ca sarasvatī  RKV 
sā tatra patitā rājan prācīnāghavimocinī 
bhāsvatyā tritayaṃ yatra śilā gīrvāṇasaṃjñitā  RKV 
tatra tīrthe ca tattīrthaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati 
kedāraṃ ca prayāgaṃ ca kurukṣetraṃ gayā tathā  RKV 
anyāni ca sutīrthāni kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm 
pañca sthānāni tīrthāni pṛthagbhūtāni yāni ca  RKV 
vakṣyāmi ca samāsena ekaikaṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak 
gayā nābhyāṃ yathā puṇyā cakratīrthaṃ ca tatsamam  RKV 
dharmāraṇye yathā kūpaṃ śūlabhedaṃ ca tatsamam 
brahmayūpaṃ yathā puṇyaṃ devanadyāstathaiva ca  RKV 
yathā gayāśiraḥ puṇyaṃ surāṇāṃ ca yathā śilā 
yathā ca puṣkaraṃ sthānaṃ mārkaṇḍahrada eva ca  RKV 
dattvā piṇḍodakaṃ tatra piṇḍāṇāṃ ca tathākṣayam 
yas tatra kurute śrāddhaṃ toyaṃ pibati nityaśaḥ 
mucyate sarvapāpaistu uragaḥ kañcukairiva 
anindyānpūjayed viprān dambhakrodhavivarjitān  RKV 
trayodaśadinaṃ dānaṃ trayodaśaguṇaṃ bhavet 
abhyarcitaṃ suraṃ dṛṣṭvā gaṇanāthaṃ gajānanam  RKV 
sarve vighnā vinaśyanti dṛṣṭvā kambalakṣetrapam  RKV 
pūjayetparayā bhaktyā śūlapāṇiṃ maheśvaram  RKV 
devasya pūrvabhāge tu umā pūjyā prayatnataḥ 
mārkaṇḍeśaṃ tato bhaktyā pūjayed guhavāsinam  RKV 
mucyante pātakaiḥ sarvair ajñānajñānasaṃcitaiḥ 
guhāmadhye praviṣṭastu japet sūktaṃ tu tryakṣaram  RKV 
nīlaparvatajaṃ puṇyaṃ ṣaṣṭhāṃśena labheta saḥ 
trinarās tatra tiṣṭhanti sādityamarutaiḥ saha  RKV 
sarvadevamayaṃ sthānaṃ koṭiliṅgamanuttamam 
yathā nadīnadāḥ sarve sāgare yānti saṃkṣayam  RKV 
tathā pāpāni naśyanti śūlabhedasya darśanāt 
pratyakṣo dṛśyate 'dyāpi pratyayo hyavanīpate  RKV 
visphuliṅgā liṅgamadhye spandante snānayogataḥ 
dvitīyaḥ pratyayas tatra tailabindur na sarpati  RKV 
evaṃ hi pratyayas tatra śūlabhedaprabhāvajaḥ 
yaḥ smarecchūlabhedaṃ tu trikālaṃ nityameva ca  RKV 
sa pūtaśca bhavetsākṣāt sabāhyābhyantaro nṛpa 
na kasyacin mayā khyātaṃ pṛṣṭo 'haṃ tridaśairapi  RKV 
guhyādguhyataraṃ tīrthaṃ sadā gopyaṃ kṛtaṃ mayā 
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvadoṣaghnamuttamam  RKV 
sarvatīrthamayaṃ tīrthaṃ śūlabhedaṃ janeśvara 
śrute yasya prabhāve tu mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
śūlabhedaṃ mayā tāta saṃkṣepāt kathitaṃ tava 
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śūlabhedapraśaṃsāvarṇanaṃ nāma catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
eṣa eva purā praśnaḥ paripṛṣṭo maheśvaram 
rājñā cottānapādena ṛṣidevasamāgame  RKV 
uttānapāda uvāca
idaṃ tīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvadevamayaṃ param 
guhyādguhyataraṃ sthānaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ na śrutaṃ hara  RKV 
śūlabhedaṃ kathaṃ jātaṃ kenaivotpāditaṃ purā 
māhātmyaṃ tasya tīrthasya vistarācchaṃsa me prabho  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
āsītpurā mahāvīryo dānavo baladarpitaḥ 
martye na tādṛśaḥ kaścid vikrameṇa balena vā  RKV 
sūnur brahmasutasyāyam andhako nāma durmadaḥ 
nijasthāne vasan pāpaḥ kurvan rājyam akaṇṭakam  RKV 
hṛṣṭapuṣṭo vasan martye sa surairnābhibhūyate 
bhavanaṃ tasya pāpasya vahnerupavanaṃ yathā  RKV 
etasminn andhakaḥ kāle cintayāmāsa bhārata 
toṣayāmi mahādevaṃ yena sānugraho bhavet  RKV 
prārthayāmi varaṃ divyaṃ yo me manasi vartate 
paraṃ sa niścayaṃ kṛtvā so 'ndhako nirgato gṛhāt  RKV 
revātaṭaṃ samāsādya dānavastapasi sthitaḥ 
ugraṃ tapaścacārāsau dāruṇaṃ lomaharṣaṇam  RKV 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ sa nirāhāro 'bhavat tataḥ 
dvitīyaṃ tu sahasraṃ sa nyavasadvāribhojanaḥ  RKV 
tṛtīyaṃ tu sahasraṃ sa dhūmapānarato 'bhavat 
caturthaṃ varṣasāhasraṃ yogābhyāsena saṃsthitaḥ  RKV 
kopīha nedṛśa cakre tapaḥ paramadāruṇam 
asthicarmāvaśeṣo 'sau yāvattiṣṭhati bhārata  RKV 
tasya mūrdhni tato rājan dhūmavārttir viniḥsṛtā 
devalokamatītyāsau kailāsaṃ vyāpya saṃsthitā  RKV 
tāvaddevasamīpasthā umā vacanam abravīt 
ko 'styayaṃ mānuṣe loke tapasogreṇa saṃsthitaḥ  RKV 
caturvarṣasahasrāṇi vyatīyuḥ parameśvara 
na kenāpīdṛśaṃ taptaṃ tapo dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ tathā  RKV 
avajñāṃ kuruṣe deva kimatra niyamānvite 
sarvasya datse śīghraṃ tvamalpena tapasā vibho  RKV 
nākṣakrīḍāṃ kariṣye 'dya tvayā saha maheśvara 
yāvannotthāpyate hyeṣa dānavo bhaktavatsala  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahādevi sarvalakṣaṇalakṣite 
ahaṃ taṃ na vijānāmi kliśyantaṃ dānaveśvaram  RKV 
yogābhyāse sthito bhadre dhyāyaṃstatparamaṃ padam 
tatrāgaccha mayā sārddhaṃ yatra tapyatyasau tapaḥ  RKV 
umayā sahito devo gatastatra maheśvaraḥ 
asthicarmāvaśeṣastu dṛṣṭo devena śambhunā  RKV 
pratyuvāca prasanno 'sau devadevo maheśvaraḥ 
bhobhoḥ kaṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ bhīmaṃ dāruṇaṃ lomaharṣaṇam  RKV 
īdṛśaṃ ca tapo ghoraṃ kasmādvatsa tvayā kṛtam 
varaṃ dāsyāmyahaṃ vatsa yaste manasi vartate  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si me deva varado yadi śaṅkara 
surān sarvān vijeṣyāmi tvatprasādān maheśvara  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
svapne 'pi tridaśāḥ sarve na yoddhavyāḥ kadācana 
asaṃbhāvyaṃ na vaktavyaṃ manaso yanna rocate  RKV 
anyaṃ kimapi yācasva yaste manasi vartate 
svarge vā yadi vā martye pātāleṣu ca saṃsthitān  RKV 
martyeṣu vividhān bhogān bhokṣyasi tvaṃ yathepsitān 
kuru niṣkaṇṭakaṃ rājyaṃ svarge devapatiryathā  RKV 
devasya vacanaṃ śrutvā so 'ndhako vimanāḥ sthitaḥ 
vṛthā kleśaśca me jāto na kiṃcit sādhitaṃ mayā  RKV 
niśvāsaṃ paramaṃ muktvā nipapāta dharātale 
mūlacchinno yathā vṛkṣo nirucchvāsas tadābhavat  RKV 
mūrcchāpannaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā devī vacanam abravīt 
yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayatyeṣa tamasmai dehi śaṅkara  RKV 
bhaktānupekṣamāṇasya tavākīrtir bhaviṣyati  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
yadi dāsye varaṃ devi icchābhūtaṃ kadācana 
tato na maṃsyate viṣṇuṃ na brahmāṇaṃ na māmapi  RKV 
uccatvamāpto deveśi anyānapi surāsurān  RKV 
devyuvāca
kamapyupāyamāśritya utthāpaya maheśvara 
viṣṇuvarjaṃ surānsarvāñjayasveti varaṃ vada  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
upāyaḥ śobhano devi yo me manasi vartate 
tamevāsmai pradāsyāmi yastvayā kathito varaḥ  RKV 
tato 'mṛtena saṃsiktaḥ svastho 'bhūt tatkṣaṇād ayam 
tathā punarnavo jātaḥ sarvāvayavaśobhitaḥ  RKV 
śṛṇuṣvaikamanā bhūtvā gṛhāṇa varamuttamam 
viṣṇuvarjaṃ pradāsyāmi yattavābhimataṃ priyam  RKV 
sarvaṃ ca saphalaṃ tubhyaṃ mā dharmaste 'nyathā bhavet 
dadāmīti varaṃ tubhyaṃ manyase yadi cāsura  RKV 
viṣṇuvarjaṃ surān sarvāñjeṣyasi tvaṃ ca māṃ vinā  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
bhavatvevam iti prāha balamāsthāya kevalam 
viṣṇuvarjaṃ vijeṣye 'haṃ svabalena maheśvara  RKV 
kṛtārtho 'haṃ hi saṃjāta ityuktvā praṇatiṃ gataḥ 
gaccha devomayāsārddhaṃ kailāsaśikharaṃ varam  RKV 
vṛṣapuṃgavam āruhya devo 'sāvumayā saha 
varaṃ dattvā sa tasyaivaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe andhakavarapradānavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sa dānavo varaṃ labdhvā jagāma svapuraṃ prati 
dadarśa svapuraṃ rājañchobhitaṃ citracatvaraiḥ  RKV 
udyānaiścaiva vividhaiḥ kadalīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitaiḥ 
panasairbakulaiścaivāmrātairāmraiśca campakaiḥ  RKV 
aśokairnālikeraiśca mātuliṅgaiḥ sadāḍimaiḥ 
nānāvṛkṣaiśca śobhāḍhyaṃ taḍāgairupaśobhitam  RKV 
devatāyatanair divyair dhvajamālāsuśobhitaiḥ 
vedādhyayananirghoṣair maṅgalādyair vināditam  RKV 
prāviśadbhavane divye kāñcane rukmamālini 
apaśyatsa sutān bhāryām amātyān dāsabhṛtyakān  RKV 
tato jayapradān sarvān itaścetaśca dhāvataḥ 
hṛcchobhāṃ ca prakurvāṇān vai jayantībhiruccakaiḥ  RKV 
kecit toraṇam ābadhya kecit puṣpāṇyavākiran 
mātuliṅgakarāścānye dhāvanti hyandhakaṃ prati  RKV 
pure janāśca dṛśyante bhājanairannapūritaiḥ 
pūrṇahastāḥ pradṛśyante tatraiva bahavo janāḥ  RKV 
sākṣatair bhājanais tatra śatasāhasrayoṣitaḥ 
mantrān paṭhanti viprāśca maṅgalānyapi yoṣitaḥ  RKV 
amātyāścaiva bhṛtyāśca gajāṃścāḍhaukayanti ca 
vardhāpayanti te sarve ye kecit puravāsinaḥ  RKV 
hṛṣṭastuṣṭo 'vasattatra sacivaiḥ saha so 'ndhakaḥ 
dadarśa sa jagatsarvaṃ turaṅgāṃśca padātikān  RKV 
tathaiva vividhān kośāṃs tatra kāñcanapūritān 
mahiṣīrgā vṛṣāṃścaivāpaśyacchatrāṇyanekadhā  RKV 
sa evamandhakas tatra kiyantaṃ kālamāvasat 
hṛṣṭastuṣṭo vasan martye sa surair nābhyabhūyata  RKV 
varaṃ labdhaṃ tu taṃ jñātvā śaṅkitāḥ svargavāsinaḥ 
ekībhūtāśca te sarve vāsavaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
śakra uvāca
kathamāgamanaṃ vo 'tra sarveṣām api nākinām 
kasmādvo bhayamutpannamāgatāḥ śaraṇaṃ katham  RKV 
tataste hyamarāḥ sarve śakram etad vaco 'bruvan  RKV 
devā ūcuḥ 
suranāthāndhako nāma daityaḥ śambhuvarorjitaḥ 
ajeyaḥ sarvadevānāṃ kiṃ nu kāryamataḥ param  RKV 
tattvaṃ cintaya deveśa ka upāyo vidhīyatām 
itthaṃ vadanti te devāḥ śakrāgre mantraṇodyatāḥ  RKV 
mantrayanti ca yāvad vai tāvaccāramukheritam 
jñātvā tatra sa devaughaṃ dānavo nirgato gṛhāt  RKV 
ekākī syandanārūḍha āyurdhaibahubhir vṛtaḥ 
durgamaṃ merupṛṣṭhaṃ sa līlayaiva gato nṛpa  RKV 
svarṇaprākārasaṃyuktaṃ śobhitaṃ vividhāśramaiḥ 
durgamaṃ śatruvargasya tadā pārthivasattama  RKV 
praviveśāsurastatra līlayā svagṛhe yathā 
vṛtrahā bhayamāpannaḥ svakīyaṃ cāsanaṃ dadau  RKV 
upaviṣṭo 'ndhakastatra śakrasyaivāsane śubhe 
āsthānaṃ kalayāmāsa sarvatastridaśāvṛtam  RKV 
śakra uvāca
kiṃ tavāgamanaṃ cātra kiṃ kāryaṃ kathayasva me 
yadasmadīyaṃ vittaṃ hi tatte dāsyāmi dānava  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
nāhaṃ vai kāmaye kośaṃ na gajāṃśca sureśvara 
svakīyaṃ darśayasvādya svargaśṛṅgārabhūṣitam  RKV 
airāvataṃ mahānāgaṃ taṃ caivoccaiḥśravohayam 
urvaśyādīni ratnāni mama darśaya gopate  RKV 
pārijātakapuṣpāṇi vṛkṣajātīnanekaśaḥ 
vāditrāṇi ca sarvāṇi darśayasva śacīpate  RKV 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śakraś cintitavān idam 
yo 'muṃ nihanti pāpmānaṃ na taṃ paśyāmi karhicit  RKV 
nāsti rakṣāpradaḥ kaścitsvargalokasya duḥkhinaḥ 
bhayatrasto dadāvanyadvāditrādyapsarogaṇaiḥ  RKV 
raṅgabhūmāvupāviśya kārayāmāsa tāṇḍavam 
upaviṣṭāḥ surāḥ sarve yamamārutakinnarāḥ  RKV 
urvaśyādyā apsaraso gītavāditrayogataḥ 
nanṛtuḥ puratastasya sarvā ekaikaśo nṛpa  RKV 
na vyaśrāmyata taccittaṃ dṛṣṭvā cāpsarasastadā 
śacīṃ prati manastasya sakāmamabhavannṛpa  RKV 
gṛhītvā śakrabhāryāṃ sa prasthitaḥ svapuraṃ prati 
tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhamandhakasya suraiḥ saha  RKV 
tena devagaṇāḥ sarve dhvastāḥ pārthivasattama 
saṃgrāme vividhaiḥ śastraiś cakravajrādibhirghanaiḥ  RKV 
saṃtāpitāḥ surāḥ sarve kṣayaṃ nītā hyanekaśaḥ 
sarve 'pi marutastena bhagnāḥ saṃgrāmamūrdhani  RKV 
yathā siṃhogajān sarvān vicitya vicared vanam 
tadvad ekena te devā jitāḥ sarve parāṅmukhāḥ  RKV 
bālo 'dhipo yathā grāme svecchayā pīḍayejjanān 
svairamākramya gṛhṇāti kośavāsāṃsi cāsakṛt  RKV 
gataṃ na paśyaty ātmānaṃ prajāsaṃtāpanena ca 
gṛhītvā śakrabhāryāṃ sa gato vai dānavottamaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śūlabhedamāhātmye śacīharaṇavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
gīrvāṇāśca tataḥ sarve brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
gajair girivarākārair hayaiścaiva gajopamaiḥ  RKV 
syandanairnagarākāraiḥ siṃhaśārdūlayojitaiḥ 
kacchapair mahiṣaiścānyair makaraiśca tathāpare  RKV 
brahmalokamanuprāptā devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ 
dṛṣṭvā padmodbhavaṃ devaṃ sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇatāḥ surāḥ  RKV 
devā ūcuḥ 
jaya deva jagadvandya jaya saṃsṛtikāraka 
padmayone suraśreṣṭha tvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
sodvegaṃ bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā devānāṃ bhāvitātmanām 
meghagambhīrayā vācā devarājamuvāca ha  RKV 
kimatrāgamanaṃ devāḥ sarveṣāṃ vai vivarṇatā 
kenāpamānitāḥ sarve śīghraṃ me kathyatāṃ svayam  RKV 
devā ūcuḥ 
andhakākhyo mahādaityo balavān padmasambhava 
tena devagaṇāḥ sarve dhanaratnair viyojitāḥ  RKV 
hatvā devagaṇāṃs tāvad asicakraparaddviśvadhaiḥ 
gṛhītvā śakrabhāryāṃ sa dānavo 'pi gato balāt  RKV 
devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
cintayāmāsa rājendra vadhārthaṃ dānavasya ha  RKV 
avadhyo dānavaḥ pāpaḥ sarveṣāṃ vo divaukasām 
sa trātā sarvajagatāṃ nānyo vidyeta kutracit  RKV 
evamuktāḥ surāḥ sarve brahmaṇā tadanantaram 
brahmāṇaṃ te puraskṛtya gatā yatra sa keśavaḥ 
tuṣṭuvurvividhaiḥ stotrair brahmādyāś cakrapāṇinam  RKV 
devā ūcuḥ 
jaya tvaṃ devadeveśa lakṣmyā vakṣaḥsthalāśritaḥ 
asurakṣaya deveśa vayaṃ te śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
stūyamānaḥ suraiḥ sarvairbrahmādyaiśca janārdanaḥ 
samprahṛṣṭamanā bhūtvā surasaṅghamuvāca ha  RKV 
śrīvāsudeva uvāca
svāgataṃ devaviprāṇāṃ suprabhātādya śarvarī 
kiṃ kāryaṃ procyatāṃ kṣipraṃ kasya ruṣṭā divaukasaḥ  RKV 
kiṃ duḥkhaṃ kaśca saṃtāpaḥ kuto vā bhayam āgatam 
kathayantu mahābhāgāḥ kāraṇaṃ yanmanogatam  RKV 
parābhavaḥ kṛto yena so 'dya yātu yamālayam 
evamuktāstu kṛṣṇena kathayāmāsurasya tat  RKV 
darśayantaḥ svakāndehān lajjamānā hyadhomukhāḥ 
hṛtarājyā hyandhakena kṛtā nistejasaḥ prabho  RKV 
piteva putraṃ parirakṣa deva jahīndraśatruṃ saha putrapautraiḥ 
tatheti coktaḥ kamalāsanena surāsurair vanditapādapadmaḥ  RKV 
śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ cāpaṃ saṃgṛhya parameśvaraḥ 
utthito bhogaparyaṅkād devānāṃ puratastadā  RKV 
śrīvāsudeva uvāca
pātāle yadi vā martye nāke vā yadi tiṣṭhati 
taṃ haniṣyāmyahaṃ pāpaṃ yena saṃtāpitāḥ surāḥ  RKV 
svaṃ sthānaṃ yāntu gīrvāṇāḥ saṃtuṣṭā bhāvitaujasaḥ 
viṣṇostadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmādyāste savāsavāḥ  RKV 
svayānaistu hariṃ natvā hṛdi tuṣṭā divaṃ yayuḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe gīrvāṇasvargamanavarṇanaṃ nāma saptacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
uttānapāda uvāca
kasminsthāne 'vasad deva so 'ndhako daityapuṃgavaḥ 
sarvāndevāṃśca nirjitya kasminsthāne samāsthitaḥ  RKV 
śrīmaheśa uvāca
praviṣṭo dānavo yatra kathayāmi narādhipa 
pātālalokamāśritya kanyā vidhvaṃsate tu saḥ  RKV 
tatra sthitaṃ taṃ vijñāya cāpamādāya keśavaḥ 
vyasṛjadbāṇamāgneyaṃ dahyatāmiti cintayan  RKV 
dahyamāno 'gninā so 'pi vāruṇāstraṃ sa saṃdadhe 
vāruṇāstreṇa mahatā āgneyaṃ śamitaṃ tadā  RKV 
tato 'sau cintayāmāsa kena bāṇo visarjitaḥ 
kasyaiṣā pauruṣī śaktiḥ ko yāsyati yamālayam  RKV 
tato 'ndhako mṛdhe kruddho bāṇamārgeṇa nirgataḥ 
sa dṛṣṭvā bāṇamārgeṇa cāpahastaṃ janārdanam  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
na śarma lapsyase hyadya mayā dṛṣṭyābhivīkṣitaḥ 
na śaknoṣi tathā gantuṃ nāgaḥ śārdūladarśanāt  RKV 
āgacchati yathā bhakṣyaṃ mārjārasya ca mūṣikaḥ 
na śaknoṣi tathā yātuṃ saṃsthitas tvaṃ mamāgrataḥ  RKV 
ahaṃ tvāṃ preṣayiṣyāmi yamamārge sudāruṇe 
ahamanveṣayiṣyāmi kila yāsyāmi te gṛham  RKV 
upanīto 'si kālena saṅgrāme mama keśava 
ye tvayā nirjitāḥ pūrvaṃ dānavā apyanekaśaḥ  RKV 
na bhavanti pumāṃsaste striyastāś caiva keśava 
paraṃ na śastrasaṅgrāmaṃ kariṣyāmi tvayā saha  RKV 
vadato dānavendrasya na cukopa sa keśavaḥ 
ayudhyamānaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā cintayāmāsa dānavaḥ  RKV 
dvandvayuddhaṃ kariṣyāmi niścitya yuyudhe nṛpa 
sa kṛṣṇena padākṣiptaḥ patitaḥ pṛthivītale  RKV 
muhūrtātsa samāśvasya utthāyedaṃ vyacintayat 
aśakto dvandvayuddhāya tataḥ sāma prayuktavān 
pāṇibhyāṃ sampuṭaṃ kṛtvā sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇataḥ śuciḥ  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
jaya kṛṣṇāya haraye viṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ 
hṛṣīkeśa jagaddhātre acyutāya mahātmane  RKV 
namaḥ paṅkajanābhāya namaḥ paṅkajamāline 
janārdanāya śrīśāya śrīpate pītavāsase  RKV 
govindāya namo nityaṃ namo jaladhiśāyine 
namaḥ karālavaktrāya narasiṃhāya nādine  RKV 
śārṅgiṇe sitavarṇāya śaṅkhacakragadābhṛte 
namo vāmanarūpāya yajñarūpāya te namaḥ  RKV 
namo varāharūpāya krāntalokatrayāya ca 
vyāptāśeṣadigantāya keśavāya namonamaḥ  RKV 
vāsudeva namastubhyaṃ namaḥ kaiṭabhanāśine 
lakṣmyālaya suraśreṣṭha namaste suranāyaka  RKV 
viṣṇordevādhidevasya pramāṇaṃ ye 'pi kurvate 
prajāpaterjagaddhātus teṣām api namāmyaham  RKV 
samastabhūtadevasya vāsudevasya dhīmataḥ 
praṇāmaṃ ye prakurvanti teṣāmapi namāmyaham  RKV 
tasya yajñavarāhasya viṣṇoramitatejasaḥ 
praṇāmaṃ ye prakurvanti teṣāmapi namāmyaham  RKV 
guṇānāṃ hi nidhānāya namaste 'stu punaḥpunaḥ 
kāruṇyāmbunidhe deva sarvabhaktipriyāya ca  RKV 
śrībhagavān uvāca
tuṣṭaste dānavendrāhaṃ varaṃ vṛṇu yathepsitam 
dadāmi te varaṃ nūnamapi trailokyadurlabham  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si me deva varaṃ dāsyasi cepsitam 
tadā dadasva me deva yuddhaṃ paramaśobhanam 
avaddhastapūto yenāhaṃ lokāngantāsmi śobhanān  RKV 
śrībhagavānuvāca
kathaṃ dadāmi te yuddhaṃ toṣito 'haṃ tvayā punaḥ 
na tvāṃ tu prabhavetkopaḥ kathaṃ yudhyāmi te 'ndhaka  RKV 
yadi te vartate buddhiryuddhaṃ prati na saṃśayaḥ 
tato gacchasva yuddhāya devaṃ prati maheśvaram  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
na tatra sidhyate kāryaṃ devaṃ prati maheśvaram  RKV 
śrībhagavān uvāca
putra tvaṃ śikharaṃ gatvā dhūnayasva balena ca  RKV 
vidhūte tatra deveśaḥ kopaṃ kartā sudāruṇam 
kopitaḥ śaṅkaro raudraṃ yuddhaṃ dāsyati dānava  RKV 
viṣṇuvākyādasau pāpo gato yatra maheśvaraḥ 
kailāsaśikharaṃ prāpya dhunoti sma muhurmuhuḥ  RKV 
dhūnite tatra śikhare kampitaṃ bhuvanatrayam 
nipetuḥ śikharāgrāṇi kampamānānyanekaśaḥ  RKV 
catvāraḥ sāgarāḥ kṣipramekībhūtā mahīpate 
nipeturulkāpātāśca pādapā apyanekaśaḥ  RKV 
umayā sahito devo vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ 
gāḍhamāliṅgya girijā devaṃ vacanam abravīt  RKV 
kimarthaṃ kampate śailaḥ kimarthaṃ kampate dharā 
kimarthaṃ kampate nāgo martyaḥ pātālameva ca 
kiṃ vā yugakṣayo deva tanmamākhyātum arhasi  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
kasyaiṣā durmatirjātā kṣiptaḥ sarpamukhe karaḥ 
lalāṭe ca kṛtaṃ varma sa yāsyati yamālayam  RKV 
kailāsamāśrito yena supto 'haṃ yena bodhitaḥ 
taṃ vadhiṣye na sandehaḥ sammukho vā bhaved yadi  RKV 
cintayāmāsa deveśo hyandhako 'yaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
upāyaṃ cintayāmāsa yenāsau vadhyate kṣaṇāt  RKV 
āgatāśca surāḥ sarve brahmādyā vasubhiḥ saha 
rathaṃ devamayaṃ kṛtvā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam  RKV 
keciddevāḥ sthitāścakre kecit tuṇḍāgrapārśvayoḥ 
kecin nābhyāṃ sthitā devāḥ keciddhuryeṣu saṃsthitāḥ  RKV 
dhurīṣu niścalāḥ kecitkecidyūpeṣu saṃsthitāḥ 
kecitsyandanasaṃstambhāḥ kecitsyandanaveṣṭakāḥ  RKV 
āmalasārake 'nye 'pi anye 'pi kalaśe sthitāḥ 
riporbhayaṃkaraṃ divyaṃ dhvajamālādiśobhitam  RKV 
rathaṃ devamayaṃ kṛtvā tamārūḍho jagadguruḥ 
niryayau dānavo yatra kopāviṣṭo maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
tiṣṭha tiṣṭhetyuvācātha kva prayāsyasi durmate 
śarāsanaṃ kare gṛhya śarāṃścikṣepa dānave  RKV 
dānave 'dhiṣṭhite yuddhe śaraiścicheda sāyakān 
śarāsaneṇa tatraiva andhakaśchāditas tadā  RKV 
na tatra dṛśyate sūryo nākāśaṃ na ca candramāḥ 
āgneyamastraṃ vyasṛjaddānavo 'pi śivaṃ prati  RKV 
dahyamānāḥ śarāṅgāraistatrasuḥ sarvadevatāḥ 
rakṣa rakṣa mahādeva dahyamānāṃstu dānavāt  RKV 
tato devādhidevo 'sau vāruṇāstramayo 'jayat 
vāruṇāstreṇa nimiṣādāgneyaṃ nāśitaṃ tadā  RKV 
dānavena tadā muktaṃ vāyavyāstraṃ raṇājire 
vāruṇaṃ ca gataṃ tāta vāyavyāstravināśitam  RKV 
devo vyasarjayatsārpaṃ krodhāviṣṭena cetasā 
mārutaṃ nāśitaṃ bāṇaiḥ sarpais tatra na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
dānavena tato muktaṃ garuḍāstraṃ ca līlayā 
gāruḍāstraṃ ca tad dṛṣṭvā sārpaṃ naiva vyadṛśyata  RKV 
tato devādhidevena nārasiṃhaṃ visarjitam 
nārasiṃhāstrabāṇena gāruḍāstraṃ praśāmitam  RKV 
astramastreṇa śamyeta na bādhyeta parasparam 
mahad yuddham abhūt tātasurāsurabhayaṃkaram  RKV 
cakranālīkanārācaistomaraiḥ khaḍgamudgaraiḥ 
vatsadantaistathā bhallaiḥ karṇikāraiśca śobhanaiḥ  RKV 
evaṃ na śakyate hantuṃ dānavo vividhāyudhaiḥ 
tadā jvālākarālāśca khaḍganārācatomarāḥ  RKV 
vṛṣāṅkena vimuktāstu samare dānavaṃ prati 
na saṃspṛśanti śastrāṇi gātraṃ gauḍavadhūriva  RKV 
āyudhāni tatastyaktvā bāhuyuddham upasthitau 
karaṃ kareṇa saṃgṛhya praharantau svamuṣṭibhiḥ 
raṇaprayogairyudhyantau yuyudhāte śivāndhakau  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
andhakaṃ prati deveśaścintayāmāsa nigraham 
haniṣyāmi na sandeho duṣṭātmānaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
sa śivena yadā kṣiptaḥ patitaḥ pṛthivītale 
ūrdhvabāhuradhovaktro dānavo nṛpasattama  RKV 
krodhāviṣṭena deveśaḥ saṅgrāme devaśatruṇā 
kakṣayoḥ kuhare kṣiptvā bandhenākramya pīḍitaḥ  RKV 
nispandaścābhavad devo mūrcchāyukto maheśvaraḥ 
mūrcchāpannaṃ tu taṃ jñātvā cintayāmāsa dānavaḥ  RKV 
hāhā kaṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ me 'dya duṣkṛtaṃ pāpakarmaṇā 
kiṃ karomi kathaṃ karma kasminsthāne tu mocaye  RKV 
gṛhītvā devamutsaṅge gataḥ kailāsaparvatam 
śayyāyāṃ śaṅkaraṃ nyasya niryayau daityarāṭ tataḥ  RKV 
śayyāyāṃ patito devaḥ prapede vedanāṃ tataḥ 
tāvaddadarśa cātmānaṃ svakīyabhavanasthitam  RKV 
parābhavaḥ kṛto madyaṃ kathaṃ tena durātmanā 
krodhavegasamāviṣṭo niryayau dānavaṃ prati  RKV 
āyasīṃ laguḍīṃ gṛhya prabhur bhārasahasrajām 
dānavaṃ ca tato dṛṣṭvā prākṣipattasya mūrdhani  RKV 
khaḍgena tāḍayāmāsa dānavaḥ prahasanraṇe 
devenāthasmṛtaṃ cāstraṃ kauccherākhyaṃ mahāhave  RKV 
dīpyamānaṃ samutsṛjya hṛdaye tāḍitaḥ kṣaṇāt 
tataḥ sa tāḍitastena rudhirodgāramudvaman  RKV 
patito 'dhomukho bhūtvā tataḥ śūlena bheditaḥ

ādeśo dīyatāṃ deva ko yāsyati yamālayam  RKV 
īśvara uvāca

tato vāgbhiḥ pratuṣṭāva devadevaṃ maheśvaram  RKV 
andhaka uvāca
jayasva devadeveśa umārdhārdhāśarīradhṛk

vṛṣabhāsanamārūḍha śaśāṅkakṛtaśekhara

saṃhatābhyāṃ tu pāṇibhyāṃ praṇanāma maheśvaram  RKV

dhūpadīpādinaivedyaiḥ sraṅmālāgurucandanaiḥ 
arcāṃ kurvanti ye viṣṇoḥ paṭheyuḥ prāktanīṃ kathām  RKV 
ṛgyajuḥsāmamantroktaṃ sūktaṃ japati yo dvijaḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati  RKV 
prātaḥ śrāddhaṃ prakurvīta dvijān sampūjya yatnataḥ 
dānaṃ dadyād yathāśakti gohiraṇyāmbarādikam  RKV 
pitarastasya tṛpyanti yāvad ābhūtasamplavam 
śrāddhadastu vrajet tatra yatra devo janārdanaḥ  RKV 
trayodaśyāṃ tato gacchedguhāvāsini liṅgake 
dṛṣṭvā mārkaṇḍamīśānaṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
uttānapāda uvāca
guhāmadhye mahādeva liṅgaṃ paramaśobhitam 
yena pratiṣṭhitaṃ deva tanmamākhyātum arhasi  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
triṣu lokeṣu vikhyāto mārkaṇḍeyo munīśvaraḥ 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ sa tapastepe sudāruṇam  RKV 
guhāmadhyaṃ praviṣṭo 'sau yogābhyāsamupāśritaḥ 
liṅgaṃ tu sthāpitaṃ tena mārkaṇḍeśvarasaṃjñitam  RKV 
tatra snātvā ca yo bhaktyā sopavāso jitendriyaḥ 
tatra jāgaraṇaṃ kurvan dadyād dīpaṃ prayatnataḥ  RKV 
devasya snapanaṃ kuryānmṛtaiḥ pañcabhis tathā 
yathā śaktyā samālabhya pūjāṃ kuryād yathāvidhi  RKV 
svaśākhotpannamantraiśca japaṃ kuryur dvijātayaḥ 
sāvitryaṣṭasahasraṃ tu śatāṣṭakam athāpi vā  RKV 
etatkṛtvā nṛpaśreṣṭha janmanaḥ phalamāpnuyāt 
caturdaśyāṃ tu vai snātvā pūjāṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi  RKV 
pātraṃ parīkṣya dātavyam ātmanaḥ śreya icchatā 
pitarastasya tṛpyanti dvādaśābdānyasaṃśayam  RKV 
dātā sa gacchate tatra yatra bhogāḥ sanātanāḥ 
guhāmadhye praviṣṭastu loṭayeccaiva śaktitaḥ  RKV 
nīle girau hi yatpuṇyaṃ tatsamastaṃ labhanti te 
śūlabhede tu yaḥ kuryācchrāddhaṃ parvaṇi parvaṇi  RKV 
viśeṣāccaitramāsānte tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu 
kedāre caiva yatpuṇyaṃ gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame  RKV 
sitāsite tu yatpuṇyamanyatīrthe viśeṣataḥ 
arbude vidyate puṇyaṃ puṇyaṃ cāmaraparvate  RKV 
gayādisarvatīrthānāṃ phalamāpnoti mānavaḥ 
vidhimantrasamāyuktas tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ  RKV 
kulānāṃ tārayed viṃśaṃ daśa pūrvān daśāparān 
dakṣiṇasyāṃ tato mūrtau śucirbhūtvā samāhitaḥ  RKV 
nyāsaṃ kṛtvā tu pūrvoktaṃ pradadyād aṣṭapuṣpikām 
śāstroktairaṣṭabhiḥ puṣpairmānasaiḥ śṛṇu tadyathā  RKV 
vārijaṃ saumyamāgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ pārthivaṃ punaḥ 
vānaspatyaṃ bhavet ṣaṣṭhaṃ prājāpatyaṃ tu saptamam  RKV 
aṣṭamaṃ śivapuṣpaṃ syād eṣāṃ śṛṇu vinirṇayam 
vārijaṃ salilaṃ jñeyaṃ saumyaṃ madhughṛtaṃ payaḥ  RKV 
āgneyaṃ dhūpadīpādyaṃ vāyavyaṃ candanādikam 
pārthivaṃ kandamūlādyaṃ vānaspatyaṃ phalātmakam  RKV 
prājāpatyaṃ tu pāṭhādyaṃ śivapuṣpaṃ tu vāsanā 
ahiṃsā prathamaṃ puṣpaṃ puṣpamindriyanigrahaḥ  RKV 
tṛtīyaṃ tu dayā puṣpaṃ kṣamā puṣpaṃ caturthakam 
dhyānapuṣpaṃ tapaḥ puṣpaṃ jñānapuṣpaṃ tu saptamam  RKV 
satyaṃ caivāṣṭamaṃ puṣpamebhis tuṣyanti devatāḥ 
bhaktyā tapasvinaḥ pūjyā jñāninaśca narādhipa  RKV 
chatramāvaraṇaṃ dadyād upānadyugalaṃ tathā 
tena pūjitamātreṇa pūjitāḥ puruṣāstrayaḥ  RKV 
svargaloke vaset tāvad yāvad ābhūtasamplavam 
śūlapāṇestu bhaktyā vai jāpyaṃ kurvanti ye narāḥ  RKV 
pañcāmṛtaiḥ pañcagavyair yakṣakardamakuṅkumaiḥ 
samālabheta deveśaṃ śrīkhaṇḍāgurucandanaiḥ  RKV 
nānāvidhaiśca ye puṣpairarcāṃ kurvanti śūlinaḥ 
niśi jāgaraṇaṃ kuryur dīpadānaṃ prayatnataḥ  RKV 
dhūpanaivedyakaṃ dadyāt paṭhetpaurāṇikīṃ kathām 
tatra sthāne sthitā bhaktyā japaṃ kurvanti ye narāḥ  RKV 
śrīsūktaṃ pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ pāvamānaṃ vṛṣākapim 
vedoktaiścaiva mantraiśca raudrīṃ vā bahurūpiṇīm  RKV 
brāhmaṇān pūjayed bhaktyā pūjayitvā praṇamya ca 
nānāvidhair mahābhogaiḥ śivaloke mahīyate  RKV 
agnim ityādi jāpyāni ṛgvedī japate tu yaḥ 
rudrān puruṣasūktaṃ ca ślokādhyāyaṃ ca śukriyam  RKV 
iṣetvā dikamantraughaṃ jyotirbrāhmaṇameva ca 
gāyatryaṃ vai madhu caiva maṇḍalabrāhmaṇāni ca  RKV 
etāñjapyāṃstu yo bhaktyā yajurvedī japed yadi 
devavrataṃ vāmadevyaṃ puruṣarṣabhameva ca  RKV 
bṛhadrathāntaraṃ caiva yo japed bhaktitatparaḥ 
sa prayāti naraḥ sthānaṃ yatra devo maheśvaraḥ  RKV 
pādaśaucaṃ tathābhyaṅgaṃ kurute yo 'tra bhaktitaḥ 
godāne caiva yatpuṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet tatra madhunā pāyasena ca 
ekasmin bhojite vipre koṭir bhavati bhojitā  RKV 
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vastraṃ dadyād bhaktyā dvijottame 
tarpitāstena devāḥ syur manuṣyāḥ pitaras tathā  RKV 
candrasūryagrahe bhaktyā snānaṃ kurvanti ye narāḥ 
devārcanaṃ ye ca kuryur japaṃ homaṃ viśeṣataḥ 
dadyād dānaṃ yathāśakti brāhmaṇe vedapārage  RKV 
aśvaṃ rathaṃ gajaṃ yānaṃ tulāpuruṣameva ca 
śakaṭaṃ yaḥ pradadyādvā saptadhānyaprapūritam  RKV 
sayoktraṃ lāṅgalaṃ dadyādyuvānau tu dhuraṃdharau 
gobhūtilahiraṇyādi pātre dātavyam arcitam  RKV 
apātre viduṣā kiṃcinna deyaṃ bhūtimicchatā 
yato 'sau sarvabhūtāni dadhāti dharaṇī kila  RKV 
tato viprāya sā deyā sarvasasyaughamālinī 
athānyacchṛṇu rājendra godānasya tu yatphalam  RKV 
yāvadvatsasya pādau dvau mukhaṃ yonyāṃ pradṛśyate 
tāvadgauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvad garbhaṃ na muñcati  RKV 
yena kenāpyupāyena brāhmaṇe tāṃ samarpayet 
pṛthvī dattā bhavet tena saśailavanakānanā  RKV 
tārayenniyataṃ dattā kulānām ekaviṃśatim 
raupyakhurīṃ kāṃsyadohāṃ savastrāṃ ca payasvinīm  RKV 
ye prayacchanti kṛtino graste sūrye niśākare 
teṣāṃ saṃkhyāṃ na jānāmi puṇyasyābdaśātair api  RKV 
sarvasyāpi hi dānasya saṃkhyāstīha narādhipa 
candrasūryoparāge ca dānasaṃkhyā na vidyate  RKV 
yatra gaur dṛśyate rājan sarvatīrthāni tatra hi 
tatra parva vijānīyānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
punaḥ smṛtvā tu tattīrthaṃ yaḥ kuryād gamanaṃ naraḥ 
athavā mriyate yo 'tra rudrasyānucaro bhavet  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śūlabhede dānadharmapraśaṃsāvarṇanaṃ nāmaikapañcāśattamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
īśvara uvāca
anyadākhyānakaṃ vakṣye purā vṛttaṃ narādhipa 
sakuṭumbo gataḥ svargaṃ muniryatra mahātapāḥ  RKV 
uttānapāda uvāca
kathaṃ nākaṃ gato vipraḥ sakuṭumbo mahānṛṣiḥ 
kautukaṃ paramaṃ deva kathayasva mama prabho  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
citrasena iti khyātaḥ kāśīrājaḥ purābhavat 
śūro dātā sudharmātmā sarvakāmasamṛddhimān  RKV 
sā purī janasaṃkīrṇā nānāratnopaśobhitā 
vārāṇasīti vikhyātā gaṅgātīram upāśritā  RKV 
śaraccandrapratīkāśā vidvajjanavibhūṣitā 
indrayaṣṭisamākīrṇā gopagokulasaṃvṛtā  RKV 
bahudhvajasamākīrṇā vedadhvaninināditā 
vaṇigjanair bahuvidhaiḥ krayavikrayaśālinī  RKV 
yantrādānaiḥ pratolībhiruccaiścānyaiḥ suśobhitā 
devatāyatanair divyair āśramair gahanair yutā  RKV 
nānāpuṣpaphalair ramyā kadalīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitā 
panasair bakulais tālair aśokair āmrakais tathā  RKV 
rājavṛkṣakapitthaiśca dāḍimair upaśobhitā 
vedādhyayananirghoṣaiḥ pavitrīkṛtamaṅgalā  RKV 
tasyā uttaradigbhāge āśramo 'bhūtsuśobhanaḥ 
tanmandāravanaṃ nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam  RKV 
bahumandārasaṃyuktaṃ tena mandārakaṃ viduḥ 
vipro dīrghatapā nāma sarvadā tatra tiṣṭhati  RKV 
tapastapati so 'tyarthaṃ tena dīrghatapāḥ smṛtaḥ 
sa tiṣṭhati sapatnīkaḥ sasutaḥ sasnuṣas tathā  RKV 
śuśrūṣanti sadā tasya putrāḥ pañca prayatnataḥ 
tasya putraḥ kanīyāṃstu ṛkṣaśṛṅgo mahātapāḥ  RKV 
vedādhyayanasampanno brahmacārī guṇānvitaḥ 
yogābhyāsarato nityaṃ kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ  RKV 
tiṣṭhate mṛgarūpeṇa mṛgayūthacarastadā 
dinānte ca dinānte ca mātāpitroḥ samīpagaḥ  RKV 
abhivādayate nityaṃ bhaktimān muniputrakaḥ 
punargacchati tatraiva kānane girigahvare  RKV 
krīḍanbālamṛgaiḥ sārddhaṃ pratyahaṃ sa muneḥ sutaḥ 
kadāciddaivayogena ṛkṣaśṛṅgo mamāra saḥ  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe
śūlabhedamāhātmye ṛkṣaśṛṅgacaritre dīrghatapomunyākhyānavarṇanaṃ nāma dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKV adhyāya 
uttānapāda uvāca
āśrame vasatas tasya sa dīrghatapaso muneḥ 
kanīyāṃs tanayo deva kathaṃ mṛtyumupāgataḥ  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
śṛṇuṣvaikamanā bhūtvā kathāṃ divyāṃ mahīpate 
śravaṇādeva yasyāstu mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
kāśīrājo mahāvīryo mahābalaparākramaḥ 
citrasena iti khyātāṃ dharaṇyāṃ sa narādhipa  RKV 
tasya rājye sadā dharmo nādharmo vidyate kvacit 
vedadharmarato nityaṃ prajā dharmeṇa pālayan  RKV 
svadharmanirataścaiva yuddhātithyapriyaḥ sadā 
kṣatradharmaṃ samāśritya bhogānbhuṅkte sa kāmataḥ  RKV 
kośasyānto na vidyeta hastyaśvarathapattimān 
itihāsapurāṇajñaiḥ paṇḍitaiḥ saha saṃkathām  RKV 
kathayanrājate rājā kailāsa iva śaṅkaraḥ 
evaṃ sa pālayanrājyaṃ rājā mantriṇam abravīt  RKV 
mṛgayāyāṃ gamiṣyāmi tiṣṭhadhvaṃ rājyapālane 
gamyatāṃ sacivaiḥ prokte gato 'sau vasudhādhipaḥ  RKV 
aśvārūḍhāśca dhāvanto rājāno maṇḍalādhipāḥ 
chatraiśchatrāṇi ghṛṣyanto 'nujagmuḥ kānanaṃ prati  RKV 
rajastatrotthitaṃ bhaumaṃ gajavājipadāhatam 
tenaitacchāditaṃ sarvaṃ sadiṅmārtaṇḍamaṃlam  RKV 
na tatra dṛśyate sūryo na kāṣṭhā na ca candramāḥ 
pādapāśca na dṛśyante giriśṛṅgāṇi sarvataḥ  RKV 
parasparaṃ na paśyanti niśārddhe vārṣike yathā 
tatrāsau sumahadyūthaṃ mṛgāṇāṃ samalakṣyata  RKV 
adhāvatsahitaḥ sarvaiḥ sa rājā rājaputrakaiḥ 
vṛndāsphoṭo 'bhavat teṣāṃ śīghraṃ jagmurdiśo daśa  RKV 
ekamārgagato rājā citraseno mahīpatiḥ 
ekākī sa gatastatra yatra yatra ca te mṛgāḥ  RKV 
praviṣṭo 'sau tato durgaṃ kānanaṃ girigahvaram 
vallīgulmasamākīrṇaṃ sthito yatra na lakṣyate  RKV 
adṛśyāṃstu mṛgānmatvā diśo rājā vyalokayat 
kāṃ diśaṃ nu gamiṣyāmi kva me sainyasamāgamaḥ  RKV 
evaṃ kaṣṭaṃ gato rājā citraseno narādhipaḥ 
vṛkṣacchāyāṃ samāśritya viśrāmamakaronnṛpaḥ  RKV 
kṣuttṛṣārto bhramandurge kānane girigahvare 
tato 'paśyatsaro divyaṃ padminīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitam  RKV 
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇaṃ cakravākopaśobhitam 
tato dṛṣṭvā sa rājendraḥ samprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ  RKV 
kamalāni gṛhītvā tu tataḥ snānaṃ samācarat 
tarpayitvā pitṛdevānmanuṣyāṃśca yathāvidhi  RKV 
ācchādya śatapatraiśca pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram 
yayau pānīyamamalaṃ yathāvatsa samāhitaḥ  RKV 
uttīrya salilāttīre dṛṣṭvā vṛkṣaṃ samīpagam 
uttarīyamadhaḥ kṛtvopaviṣṭo dharaṇītale  RKV 
cintayannupaviṣṭo 'sau kimadya prakaromyaham 
tatrāsīno dadarśātha vanoddeśe mṛgānbahūn  RKV 
kecitpūrvamukhāstatra cāpare dakṣiṇāmukhāḥ 
vāruṇyamimukhāḥ kecit kecit kauberadiṅmukhāḥ  RKV 
kecin nidrāparāḥ kecidūrdhvakarṇāḥ sthitāḥ pare 
mṛgamadhye sthito yogī ṛkṣaśṛṅgo mahātapāḥ  RKV 
mṛgāndṛṣṭvā tato rājā āhārārtham acintayat 
hatvaiteṣu mṛgaṃ kaṃcidbhakṣayāmi yadṛcchayā  RKV 
svasthāvastho bhaviṣyāmi mṛgamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇāt 
kāśīṃ prati gamiṣyāmi mārgamanviṣya yatnataḥ  RKV 
vicintyaivaṃ tato rājā vṛkṣamūlamupāśritaḥ 
cāpaṃ gṛhya karāgreṇa sa śaraṃ saṃdadhe tataḥ  RKV 
vicikṣepa śaraṃ tatra yatra te bahavo mṛgāḥ 
teṣāṃ madhye sa vai viddha ṛkṣaśṛṅgo mahātapāḥ  RKV 
jagmustrastāstu te sarve śabdaṃ kṛtvā vanaukasaḥ 
sa ṛṣiḥ patitas tatra kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti cābravīt  RKV 
hāhā kaṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ tena yenāhaṃ ghātito 'dhunā 
kasyaiṣā durmatirjātā pāpabuddher mamopari  RKV 
mṛgamadhye sthitaścāhaṃ na kaṃcid uparodhaye 
tāṃ vācaṃ mānuṣīṃ śrutvā sa rājā vismayānvitaḥ  RKV 
śīghraṃ gatvā tato 'paśyad brāhmaṇaṃ brahmatejasā 
hāhā kaṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ me 'dya yenāsau ghātito dvijaḥ  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
akāmādghātitastvaṃ tu mṛgabhrāntyā mayānagha 
gṛhītvā bahudārūṇi svatanuṃ dāhayāmyaham  RKV 
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaṃ tu yatkiṃcinna samaṃ brahmahatyayā 
anyathā brahmahatyāyāḥ śuddhir me na bhaviṣyati  RKV 
ṛkṣaśṛṅga uvāca
na te siddhir bhavet kācinmayi pañcatvamāgate 
bahvyo hatyā bhaviṣyanti vināśe mama sāmpratam  RKV 
jananī me pitā vṛddho bhrātaraśca tapasvinaḥ 
bhrātṛjāyā mariṣyanti mayi pañcatvam āgate  RKV 
etā hatyā bhaviṣyanti kathaṃ śuddhirbhavet tava 
upāyaṃ kathayiṣyāmi taṃ kartuṃ yadi manyase  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
upāyaḥ kathyatāṃ me 'dya yaste manasi vartate 
kariṣye tamahaṃ sarvaṃ yatnenāpi mahāmune  RKV 
ṛkṣaśṛṅga uvāca
pṛcchāmi tvāṃ kathaṃ ko vā kutastvamiha cāgataḥ 
brahmakṣatraviśāṃ madhye ko bhavānuta śūdrajaḥ  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
nāhaṃ śūdro 'smi bhostāta na vaiśyo brāhmaṇo na vā 
na cāntyajo 'smi viprendra kṣatriyo 'smi mahāmune  RKV 
dharmajñaśca kṛtajñaśca sarvasattvahite rataḥ 
akāmāt pātakaṃ jātaṃ kathaṃ śuddhirbhaviṣyati  RKV 
ṛkṣaśṛṅga uvāca
māṃ gṛhītvā āśramaṃ gaccha yatra tau pitarau mama 
āvedayasva cātmānaṃ putraghātinam āturam  RKV 
te dṛṣṭvā māṃ kariṣyanti kāruṇyaṃ ca tavopari 
upāyaṃ kathayiṣyanti yena śāntirbhaviṣyati  RKV 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā citraseno nṛpottama 
skandhe kṛtvā tu taṃ vipraṃ jagāmāśramasannidhau  RKV 
na śaknoti yadā voḍhuṃ viśrāmyati punaḥpunaḥ 
tāvat paśyati taṃ vipraṃ mūrchitaṃ vikalendriyam  RKV 
mumoca citrasenas taṃ chāyāyāṃ vaṭabhūruhaḥ 
vastraṃ caturguṇaṃ kṛtvā cakre vātaṃ muhurmuhuḥ  RKV 
paśyatas tasya rājendra ṛkṣaśṛṅgo mahātapāḥ 
pañcatvamagamacchīghraṃ dhyānayogena yogavit  RKV 
dāhayāmāsa taṃ vipraṃ vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā 
snānaṃ kṛtvā sa śokārto vilalāpa muhurmuhuḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śūlabhedamāhātmye ṛkṣaśṛṅgasvargagamanavarṇanaṃ nāma  
tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
īśvara uvāca
tataścānantaraṃ rājā jagāmodvegam uttamam 
kathaṃ yāmi gṛhaṃ tvadya vārāṇasyām ahaṃ punaḥ  RKV 
brahmahatyāsamāviṣṭo juhomyagnau kalevaram 
athavā tasya vākyena taṃ gacchāmyāśramaṃ prati  RKV 
kathayāmi yathāvṛttaṃ gatvā tasya mahāmuneḥ 
evaṃ saṃcintya rājāsau jagāmāśramasannidhau  RKV 
ṛkṣaśṛṅgasya cāsthīni gṛhītvā sa nṛpottamaḥ 
dṛṣṭimārge sthitastasya maharṣer bhāvitātmanaḥ  RKV 
dīrghatapā uvāca
āgaccha svāgataṃ te 'stu āsane 'tropaviśyatām 
arghaṃ dadāmyahaṃ yena madhuparkaṃ saviṣṭaram  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
arghasyāsya na yogyo 'haṃ maharṣe nāsmi bhāṣaṇe 
mṛgamadhyasthito vipras tava putro mayā hataḥ  RKV 
putraghnaṃ viddhi māṃ vipra tīvradaṇḍena daṇḍaya 
mṛgabhrāntyā hato vipra ṛkṣaśṛṅgo mahātapāḥ  RKV 
iti matvā muniśreṣṭha kuru me tvaṃ yathocitam 
mātā tadvacanaṃ śrutvā gṛhān niṣkramya vihvalā  RKV 
hā hatāsmītyuvācedaṃ papāta dharaṇītale 
vilalāpa suduḥkhārtā putraśokena pīḍitā  RKV 
hā hatā putra putreti karuṇaṃ kurarī yathā 
vilalāpāturā mātā kva gato māṃ vihāya vai 
mukhaṃ darśaya cātmīyaṃ mātaraṃ māṃ hi mānaya  RKV 
śrutādhyayanasampannaṃ japahomaparāyaṇam 
āgataṃ tvāṃ gṛhadvāre kadā drakṣyāmi putraka  RKV 
lokoktyā śrūyate caitaccandanaṃ kila śītalam 
putragātrapariṣvaṅgaścandanād api śītalaḥ  RKV 
kiṃ candanena pīyūpabindunā kiṃ kimindunā  RKV 
putragātrapariṣvaṅgapātraṃ gātraṃ bhavedyadi  RKV 
pariṣvajitum icchāmi tvāmahaṃ putra supriya 
pañcatvam anuyāsyāmi tvadvihīnādya duḥkhitā  RKV 
evaṃ vilapatī dīnā putraśokena pīḍitā 
mūrchitā vihvalā dīnā nipapāta mahītale  RKV 
bhāryāṃ ca patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā putraśokena pīḍitām 
cukopa sa munistatra citrasenāya bhūbhṛte  RKV 
dīrghatapā uvāca
yāhi yāhi mahāpāpa mā mukhaṃ darśayasva me 
kiṃ tvayā ghātito vipro hyakāmācca suto mama  RKV 
brahmahatyā bhaviṣyanti bahvyaste vasudhādhipa 
sakuṭumbasya me tvaṃ hi mṛtyureṣa upasthitaḥ  RKV 
evamuktvā tato vipro vicintya ca punaḥpunaḥ 
parityajya tadā krodhaṃ munibhāvājjagāda ha  RKV 
dīrghatapā uvāca
udvegaṃ tyaja bho vatsa duruktaṃ gadito mayā 
putraśokābhibhūtena duḥkhataptena mānada  RKV 
kiṃ karoti naraḥ prājñaḥ preryamāṇaḥ svakarmabhiḥ 
prāgeva hi manuṣyāṇāṃ buddhiḥ karmānusāriṇī  RKV 
anenaiva vidhānena pañcatvaṃ vihitaṃ mama 
hatyāstava bhaviṣyanti pūrvamuktā na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
brahmakṣatraviśāṃ madhye śūdracaṇḍālajātiṣu 
kastvaṃ kathaya satyaṃ me kasmācca nihato dvijaḥ  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
vijñāpayāmi viprarṣe kṣantavyaṃ te mamopari 
nāhaṃ vipro 'smi vai tāta na vaiśyo na ca śūdrajaḥ  RKV 
na vyādhaścāntyajāto vā kṣatriyo 'haṃ mahāmune 
kāśīrājo mṛgān hantum āgato vanamuttamam  RKV 
bhrāntyā nipātito hyeṣa mṛgarūpadharo muniḥ 
idānīṃ tava pādānte saṃśritaḥ pātakānvitaḥ  RKV 
kiṃ kartavyaṃ mayā vipra upāyaṃ kathayasva me  RKV 
dīrghatapā uvāca
brahmahatyā na śakyetāpyekā nistarituṃ prabho 
daśaikā ca kathaṃ śakyāstāḥ śṛṇuṣva nareśvara  RKV 
catvāro me sutā rājan sabhāryā mātṛpūrvakāḥ 
mayā saha na jīvanti ṛkṣaśṛṅgasya kāraṇe  RKV 
upāyaṃ śobhanaṃ tāta kathayiṣye śṛṇuṣva tam 
śakro 'pi yadi taṃ kartuṃ sukhopāyaṃ nareśvara  RKV 
sakuṭumbaṃ samastaṃ māṃ dāhayitvānale nṛpa 
asthīni narmadātoye śūlabhede vinikṣipa  RKV 
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle śūlabhedaṃ hi viśrutam 
sarvapāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvaduḥkhaghnamuttamam  RKV 
śucirbhūtvā mamāsthīni tatra tīrthe vinikṣipa 
mokṣyase sarvapāpais tvaṃ mama vākyānna saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
rājovāca
ādeśo dīyatāṃ tāta kariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ 
samastaṃ me 'sti yatkiṃcidrājyaṃ kośaḥ suhṛtsutāḥ  RKV 
tavādhīnaṃ mahāvipra prayacchāmi prasīda me 
parasparaṃ vivadatorvipra rājñostadā nṛpa  RKV 
sphuṭitvā hṛdayaṃ śīghraṃ munibhāryā mṛtā tadā 
putraśokasamāviṣṭā nirjīvā patitā kṣitau  RKV 
putrāśca mātṛśokena sarve pañcatvamāgatāḥ 
snuṣāścaiva tadā sarvā mṛtāśca saha bhartṛbhiḥ  RKV 
pañcatvaṃ ca gatāḥ sarve munimukhyā nṛpottama 
viprān āhvāpayāmāsa ye tatrāśramavāsinaḥ  RKV 
tebhyo nivedayāmāsa yathāvṛttaṃ nṛpottamaḥ 
sa taistadābhyanujñātaḥ kāṣṭhānyādāya yatnataḥ  RKV 
dāhaṃ saṃcayanaṃ cakre citraseno mahīpatiḥ 
ṛkṣaśṛṅgādisarveṣāṃ gṛhītvāsthīni yatnataḥ  RKV 
yāmyāśāṃ prasthito rājā pādacārī mahīpate 
na śaknoti yadā gantuṃ chāyāmāśritya tiṣṭhati  RKV 
viśramya ca punar gacched bhārākrānto mahīpatiḥ 
sacailaṃ kurute snānaṃ muktvāsthīni pade pade  RKV 
pibejjalaṃ nirāhāraḥ sa gacchan dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ 
acireṇaiva kālena saṃgato narmadātaṭam  RKV 
āśramasthān dvijān dṛṣṭvā papraccha pṛthivīpatiḥ  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
kathyatāṃ śūlabhedasya mārgaṃ me dvijasattamāḥ 
yena yāmi mahābhāgāḥ svakāryārthasya siddhaye  RKV 
munaya ūcuḥ 
itaḥ krośāntarād arvāk tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam 
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle tato drakṣyasi nānyathā  RKV 
ṛṣivākyena rājāsau śīghraṃ gatvā nareśvaraḥ 
sa dadarśa tataḥ śīghraṃ bahudvijasamākulam  RKV 
bahudrumalatākīrṇaṃ bahupuṣpopaśobhitam 
ṛkṣasiṃhasamākīrṇaṃ nānāvratadharaiḥ śubhaiḥ  RKV 
ekapādāsthitāḥ kecidapare sūryadṛṣṭayaḥ 
ekāṅguṣṭha sthitāḥ kecid ūrdhvabāhusthitāḥ pare  RKV 
dinaikabhojanāḥ kecit kecit kandaphalāśanāḥ 
trirātrabhojanāḥ kecitparākavratino 'pare  RKV 
cāndrāyaṇaratāḥ kecit kecit pakṣopavāsinaḥ 
māsopavāsinaḥ kecit kecidṛtvantapāraṇāḥ  RKV 
yogābhyāsaratāḥ kecit keciddhyāyanti tatpadam 
śīrṇaparṇāśinaḥ kecit kecicca kaṭukāśanāḥ  RKV 
śaivālabhojanāḥ kecit kecinmārutabhojanāḥ 
gārhasthye ca sthitāḥ kecit keciccaivāgnihotriṇaḥ  RKV 
evaṃvidhān dvijān dṛṣṭvā jānubhyāmavaniṃ gataḥ 
praṇamya śirasā rājanrājā vacanam abravīt  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
kasmindeśe ca tat tīrthaṃ satyaṃ kathayata dvijāḥ 
yenābhivāñchitā siddhiḥ saphalā me bhaviṣyati  RKV 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ 
dhanvantaraśataṃ gaccha bhṛgutuṅgasya mūrdhani 
kuṇḍaṃ drakṣyasi tatpūrṇaṃ vistīrṇaṃ payasā śivam  RKV 
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā gataḥ kuṇḍasya sannidhau 
dṛṣṭvā caiva tu tat tīrthaṃ bhrāntirjātā nṛpasya vai  RKV 
tato vismayamāpannaścintayanvai muhurmuhuḥ 
ākāśasthaṃ dadarśāsau sāmiṣaṃ kuraraṃ nṛpaḥ  RKV 
bhramamāṇaṃ gṛhītāhiṃ vadhyamānaṃ nirāmiṣaiḥ 
parasparaṃ ca yuyudhuḥ sarve 'pyāmiṣakāṅkṣayā  RKV 
hataścañcuprahāreṇa sa tataḥ patito 'ṃbhasi 
śūlena śūlinā yatra bhūbhāgo bheditaḥ purā  RKV 
tattīrthasya prabhāveṇa sa sadyaḥ puruṣo 'bhavat 
vimānasthaṃ dadarśāsau pumāṃsaṃ divyarūpiṇam  RKV 
gandharvāpsaraso yakṣāstaṃ yāntaṃ tuṣṭuvur divi 
apsarogīyamāne tu gate sūryasya mūrdhani 
citrasenas tatastasminnāścaryaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ  RKV 
ṛṣiṇā kathitaṃ yadvattadvattīrthaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
hṛṣṭaromābhavad dṛṣṭvā prabhāvaṃ tīrthasambhavam  RKV 
mamādya divaso dhanyo yasmād atra samāgataḥ 
asthīni bhūmau nikṣipya snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi  RKV 
tilamiśreṇa toyenātarpayat pitṛdevatāḥ 
gṛhyāsthīni tato rājā cikṣepāntarjale tadā  RKV 
kṣaṇamekaṃ tato vīkṣya rājorddhvavadanaḥ sthitaḥ 
tān dadarśa punaḥ sarvān divyarūpadharāñchubhān  RKV 
divyavastraiśca saṃvītān divyābharaṇabhūṣitān 
vimānair vividhair divyair apsarogaṇasevitaiḥ  RKV 
pṛthagbhūtāṃśca tān sarvān vimāneṣu vyavasthitān 
utpattivatsamālokya rājā saṃharṣī so 'bhavat  RKV 
ṛṣirvimānam ārūḍhaścitrasenam athābravīt 
bhobhoḥ sādho mahārāja citrasena mahīpate  RKV 
tvatprasādānnṛpaśreṣṭha gatirdivyā mamedṛṣī 
jāteyaṃ yattvayā kāryaṃ kṛtaṃ paramaśobhanam  RKV 
svasuto 'pi na śaknoti pitḥṇāṃ kartumīdṛśam 
madīyavacanāt tāta niṣpāpastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi  RKV 
phalaṃ prāpsyasi rājendra kāmikaṃ manasepsitam 
āśīrvādāṃs tato dattvā citrasenāya dhīmate 
svargaṃ jagāma sasutas tato dīrghatapā muniḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcamāvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe dīrghatapasaḥ svargārohaṇavarṇanaṃ nāma catuḥpañcāśattamo  
'dhyāyaḥ

uttānapāda uvāca
māhātmyaṃ tīrthajaṃ dṛṣṭvā citraseno nareśvaraḥ 
kiṃ cakāra kva vā vāsaṃ kimāhāro babhūva ha  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
bhṛgutuṅgaṃ samāruhya aiśānīṃ diśamāśritaḥ 
tapaścacāra vipulaṃ kuṇḍe tatra nṛpottamaḥ  RKV 
sarvān devān hṛdi dhyātvā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarān 
vicikṣepa yadātmānaṃ pratyakṣau rudrakeśavau 
kare gṛhītvā rājānaṃ rudro vacanam abravīt  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
prāṇatyāgaṃ mahārāja mā kāle tvaṃ kṛthā vṛthā 
adyāpyasi yuvā tvaṃ vai na yuktaṃ maraṇaṃ tava  RKV 
svasthānaṃ gaccha śīghraṃ tvaṃ bhuktvā bhogānyathepsitān 
kuru niṣkaṇṭakaṃ rājyaṃ nāke śakra ivāparaḥ  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
na rājyaṃ kāmaye deva na putrān na ca bāndhavān 
na bhāryāṃ na ca kośaṃ ca na gajān na turaṃgamān  RKV 
muñca muñca mahādeva mā vighnaḥ kriyatāṃ mama 
svargaprāptir mamādyaiva tvatprasādānmaheśvara  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
yasyāgrato bhaved brahmā viṣṇuḥ śambhus tathaiva ca 
svargeṇa tasya kiṃ kāryaṃ sa gataḥ kiṃ kariṣyati  RKV 
tuṣṭā vayaṃ trayo devā vṛṇīṣva varamuttamam 
yathepsitaṃ mahārāja satyam etad asaṃśayam  RKV 
citrasena uvāca
yadi tuṣṭāstrayo devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ 
adyaprabhṛti yuṣmābhiḥ sthātavyam iha sarvadā  RKV 
gayāśiro yathā puṇyaṃ kṛtaṃ yuṣmābhir eva ca 
tathaivedaṃ prakartavyaṃ śūlabhedaṃ ca pāvanam  RKV 
yatrayatra sthitā yūyaṃ tatratatra vasāmyaham 
gaṇānāṃ caiva sarveṣām ādhipatyam athāstu me  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
adyaprabhṛti tiṣṭhāmaḥ śūlabhede nareśvara 
trikālāṃ hi trayo devāḥ kalāṃśena vasāmahe  RKV 
nandisaṃjño gaṇādhīśo bhaviṣyati bhavāndhruvam 
matsamīpe tu bhavata ādau pūjā bhaviṣyati  RKV 
prakṣipya tāni cāsthīni yatra dīrghatapā yayau 
sakuṭumbo vimānasthaḥ svargatas tvaṃ tathā kuru  RKV 
evaṃ devā varaṃ dattvā citrasenāya pārthiva 
kuṇḍamūrdhani yāmyāyāṃ trayo devās tadā sthitāḥ  RKV 
parasparaṃ vadantyevaṃ puṇyatīrthamidaṃ param 
yathā hi gayāśiraḥ puṇyaṃ pūrvameva paṭhyate 
tathā revātaṭe puṇyaṃ śūlabhedaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
idaṃ tīrthaṃ tathā puṇyaṃ yathā puṇyaṃ gayāśiraḥ 
sakṛtpiṇḍodakenaiva naro nirmalatāṃ vrajet  RKV 
ekaṃ gayāśiro muktvā sarvatīrthāni bhūpate 
śūlabhedasya tīrthasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  RKV 
kuṇḍam udīcyāṃ yāmyāyāṃ daśahastapramāṇataḥ 
raudravāruṇakāṣṭhāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ caikaviṃśati  RKV 
etatpramāṇaṃ tattīrthaṃ piṇḍadānādikarmasu 
nādharmaniratā dātuṃ labhante dānamatra hi  RKV 
viṣṇustu pitṛrūpeṇa brahmarūpī pitāmahaḥ 
prapitāmaho rudro 'bhūdevaṃ tripuruṣāḥ sthitāḥ  RKV 
kadā paśyati tīrthaṃ vai kadā nastārayiṣyati 
iti pratīkṣāṃ kurvanti putrāṇāṃ satataṃ nṛpa 
śūlabhede naraḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā śūladharaṃ sakṛt  RKV 
nāputro nādhano rogī saptajanmasu jāyate 
ekaviṃśatiṃ pituḥ pakṣe mātuśvaivekaviṃśatim  RKV 
bhāryāpakṣe daśaiveha kulānyetāni tārayet 
śūlabhedavane rājañchākamūlaphalairapi  RKV 
ekasminbhojite vipre koṭīr bhavati bhojitā 
pañcasthāneṣu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute bhaktimān naraḥ  RKV 
kulāni pretabhūtāni sarvāṇyapi hi tārayet 
dvijadevaprasādena pitḥṇāṃ ca prasādataḥ  RKV 
śrāddhado nivaset tatra yatra devo maheśvaraḥ 
syurātmaghātino ye ca gobrāhmaṇahanāśca ye  RKV 
daṃṣṭribhir jalapāte ca vidyutpāteṣu ye mṛtāḥ 
na yeṣām agnisaṃskāro nāśaucaṃ nodakakriyā  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yasteṣāṃ śrāddhaṃ kurvīta bhaktitaḥ 
mokṣāvāptir bhavet teṣāṃ yugamekaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
ajñānād yatkṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bālabhāvācca yatkṛtam 
tatsarvaṃ nāśayet pāpaṃ snānamātreṇa bhūpate  RKV 
rajakena yathā dhautaṃ vastraṃ bhavati nirmalam 
tathā pāpo 'pi tattīrthe snāto bhavati nirmalaḥ  RKV 
saṃnyāsaṃ kurute yo 'tra tīrthe vidhisamanvitam 
dhyāyan nityaṃ mahādevaṃ sa gacchet paramaṃ padam  RKV 
krīḍitvā sa yathākāmaṃ svecchayā śivamandire 
vedavedāṅgatattvajño jāyate 'sau śubhe kule  RKV 
rūpavānsubhagaścaiva sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ 
rājā vā rājaputro vācārasamanvitaḥ  RKV 
etatte kathitaṃ rājaṃstīrthasya phalamuttamam 
yacchrutvā mānavo nityaṃ mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
ya idaṃ śrāvayen nityamākhyānaṃ dvijapuṃgavān 
śrāddhe devakule vāpi paṭhetparvṇi parvṇi  RKV 
gīrvāṇāstasya tuṣyanti manuṣyāḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha 
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva naśyate sarvapātakam  RKV 
likhitvā tīrthamāhātmyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo dadāti yaḥ 
jātismaratvaṃ labhate prāpnotyabhimataṃ phalam  RKV 
rudraloke vaset tāvad yāvad akṣaram anvitam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śūlabhedamāhātmye kāśīrājamokṣagamanaṃ nāma pañcapañcāśattamo  
'dhyāyaḥ
