tyaktvā rājyaṃ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ jagāma tapa uttamam 
putradāragṛhaṃ rājyaṃ vasūni vividhāni ca  RKV 
phalānyetāni dharmasya śobhayanti janeśvaram 
phalaṃ dharmasya bhuñjeti suhṛtsvajanabāndhavāḥ  RKV 
paśyatāṃ sarvam eteṣāṃ pāpamekena bhujyate 
paraṃ hi sukhamutsṛjya karśayanvai kalevaram  RKV 
devarājo jagāmāsau tīrthānyāyatanāni ca 
gaṅgātīrtheṣu sarveṣu yāmuneṣu tathaiva ca  RKV 
sārasvateṣu sarveṣu sāmudreṣu pṛthakpṛthak 
nadīṣu devakhāteṣu taḍāgeṣu saraḥsu ca  RKV 
pāpaṃ na muñcate sarve paścāddevasamāgame 
revāprabhavatīrtheṣu kūlayor ubhayor api  RKV 
pūjayanvai mahādevaṃ skandatīrthaṃ samāsadat

ārdravāsāstu hemante cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ 
evaṃ tu tapatastasya indrasya viditātmanaḥ  RKV

tatastvekādaśe prāpte varṣe tu nṛpasattama  RKV

tathā brahmarṣayaḥ siddhā brahmaviṣṇupurogamāḥ  RKV 
tatrājagmuḥ surāḥ sarve yatra devaḥ śatakratuḥ 
dṛṣṭvā samāgatān devān ṛṣīṃścaiva mahāmatiḥ  RKV

viditaṃ sarvameteṣāṃ yathā vṛtravadhaḥ kṛtaḥ  RKV

tathāpyevaṃ brahmahaṇaṃ matvā pāpasya kāriṇam  RKV 
bhramantaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu brahmahatyā na muñcati

yathā vihīnacandrārkaṃ tathā rājyamanāyakam

kurvantu śakraṃ nirdoṣaṃ tathā sarve maharṣayaḥ 
bṛhaspatimukhodgīrṇaṃ śrutvā tadvacanaṃ śubham  RKV

avagāhya tataḥ peyā āpo vai nānyathā budhaiḥ 
dharāyāmakṣipadbhāgaṃ dvitīyaṃ padmasaṃbhavaḥ  RKV

indratīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ 
mahāpātakayukto 'pi mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
indratīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram 
so 'śvamedhasya yajñasya puṣkalaṃ phalam aśnute  RKV 
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam 
śrutamātreṇa yenaiva mucyante pātakair narāḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe indratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśottaraśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra kahloḍītīrtham uttamam 
revāyāścottare kūle sarvapāpavināśanam  RKV 
hitārthaṃ sarvabhūtānām ṛṣibhiḥ sthāpitaṃ purā 
tapasā tu samuddhṛtya narmadāyāṃ mahāmbhasi  RKV 
snātvā tu kapilātīrthe kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati 
śrutvā cākhyānakaṃ divyaṃ brāhmaṇāñchṛṇu yatphalam  RKV 
sarveṣāmeva dānānāṃ kapilādānamuttamam

sadyaḥ prasūtāṃ kapilāṃ śobhanāṃ yaḥ prayacchati

sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā 
dattā caiva mahābāho pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV

tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati 
mṛto viṣṇupuraṃ yāti gīyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ  RKV

yatkṛtvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe kahloḍītīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kambukeśvaramuttamam 
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityo dānavo baladarpitaḥ  RKV 
avadhyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ 
tasya putro mahātejāḥ prahlādo nāma nāmataḥ  RKV

kamburuvāca

tasyāhaṃ saṃyuge sādhyo yenopāyena śaṅkara 
bhavāmi na sadā kālaṃ taṃ vadasva varaṃ mama  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
mama saṃnihito yatra tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi dānava 
tatra viṣṇubhayaṃ nāsti vasātra vigatajvaraḥ  RKV 
tasya devādhidevasya vedagarbhasya saṃyuge 
śaṅkhacakradharasyeśā nāhaṃ sarve surāsurāḥ  RKV 
kiṃ punaryo dviṣatyenaṃ lokālokaprabhuṃ harim

vasiṣyasi ciraṃ kālam ityuktvādarśanaṃ gataḥ  RKV

sthāpayāmāsa deveśaṃ śivaṃ śāntamanāmayam  RKV

tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ

tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca candrahāse śubhāśubham

te dhanyāste mahātmānas teṣāṃ janma sujīvitam

vācikaṃ mānasaṃ pāpaṃ karmajaṃ yatpurākṛtam

candrahāsaṃ na jānanti ye revāyāṃ vyavasthitam  RKV 
candrahāse tu yaḥ kaścitsaṃnyāsaṃ kurute dvijaḥ 
anivartikā gatistasya somalokānna saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe somatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ayanaṃ cottaraṃ cāpi bhāskareṇa vinā nṛpa  RKV 
snānaṃ dānaṃ japo homaḥ svādhyāyo devatārcanam 
na vartate vinā sūryaṃ tena pūjyatamo raviḥ  RKV 
śabdagāḥ śrutimukhyāśca brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ 
pratyakṣo bhagavāndevo dṛśyate lokapāvanaḥ  RKV 
utpattiḥ pralayasthānaṃ nidhānaṃ bījamavyayam 
hetureko jagannātho nānyo vidyeta bhāskarāt  RKV 
evamātmabhavaṃ kṛtvā jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam 
lokānāṃ tu hitārthāya sthāpayed dharmapaddhatim  RKV 
narmadātaṭamāśritya sthāpayitvātmanas tanum 
sahasrāṃśuṃ nidhiṃ dhāmnāṃ jagāmākāśamavyayam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram 
sahasrakiraṇaṃ devaṃ nāmamantravidhānataḥ  RKV 
tena taptaṃ hutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam 
tena samyagvidhānena samprāptaṃ paramaṃ padam  RKV 
te dhanyāste mahātmānasteṣāṃ janma sujīvitam 
snātvā ye narmadātoye devaṃ paśyanti bhāskaram  RKV 
tathā devasya rājendra ye kurvanti pradakṣiṇam 
ananyabhaktyā satataṃ trirakṣarasamanvitāḥ  RKV 
tena pūtaśarīrāste mantreṇa gatapātakāḥ 
yatpuṇyaṃ ca bhavet teṣāṃ tadihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu  RKV 
sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā 
pradakṣiṇīkṛtā sarvā pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
mantramūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
tena mantravihīnaṃ tu kāryaṃ loke na sidhyati  RKV 
yathā kāṣṭhamayo hastī yathā carmamayo mṛgaḥ 
kāryārthaṃ naiva sidhyeta tathā karma hyamantrakam  RKV 
bhasmahutaṃ pārtha yathā toyavivarjitam 
niṣphalaṃ jāyate dānaṃ tathā mantravivarjitam  RKV 
kāṣṭhapāṣāṇaloṣṭeṣu mṛnmayeṣu viśeṣataḥ 
mantreṇa loke pūjāṃ tu kurvanti na hyamantrataḥ  RKV 
dvādaśābdānnamaskārādbhaktyā yallabhate phalam 
mantrayuktanamaskārātsakṛttallabhate phalam  RKV 
saṃkrāntau ca vyatīpāte ayane viṣuve tathā 
narmadāyā jale snātvā yastu pūjayate ravim  RKV 
dvādaśābdena yat pāpam ajñānajñānasaṃcitam 
tatkṣaṇānnaśyate sarvaṃ vahninā tu tuṣaṃ yathā  RKV 
candrasūryagrahe snātvā sopavāso jitendriyaḥ 
tatrādityamukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
māghamāse tu samprāpte saptamyāṃ nṛpasattama 
sopavāso jitakrodha uṣitvā sūryamandire  RKV 
prātaḥ snātvā vidhānena dadātyarghaṃ divākare 
vidhinā mantrayuktena sa labhet puṇyamuttamam  RKV 
pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ kṛtvā hyudakatarpaṇam 
mandire devadevasya tataḥ pūjāṃ samācaret  RKV 
gandhaiḥ puṣpaistathā dhūpairdīpanaivedyaśobhanaiḥ 
pūjayitvā jagannāthaṃ tato mantramudīrayet  RKV 
viṣṇuḥ śakro yamo dhātā mitro 'tha varuṇastathā 
vivasvānsavitā pūṣā caṇḍāṃśurbharga eva ca  RKV 
iti dvādaśanāmāni japankṛtvā pradakṣiṇām 
yatphalaṃ labhate pārtha tadihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu  RKV 
daridro vyādhito mūko badhiro jaḍa eva ca 
na bhavetsapta janmāni ityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt  RKV 
evaṃ jñātvā vidhānena japanmantraṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ 
ārādhayed raviṃ bhaktyā ya icchetpuṇyamuttamam  RKV 
mantrahīnāṃ tu yaḥ kuryād bhaktiṃ devasya bhārata 
sa viḍambati cātmānaṃ paśukīṭapataṅgavat  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścit tyajate dehamuttamam 
sa gatastatra devaistu pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ  RKV 
svecchayā suciraṃ kālamiha loke nṛpo bhavet  RKV 
putrapautrasamāyukto hastyaśvarathasaṅkulaḥ 
dāsīdāsaśatopeto jāyate vipule kule  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe ravitīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra paraṃ tīrthamayonijam 
snātamātro narastatra na paśyed yonisaṅkaṭam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā pūjayed devamīśvaram 
ayonijo mahādeva yathā tvaṃ parameśvara  RKV 
tathā mocaya māṃ deva sambhavād yonisaṅkaṭāt 
gandhapuṣpādidhūpaiśca sa mucyet sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
tasya devasya yo bhaktyā kurute liṅgapūraṇam 
sa vaseddevadevasya yāvatsikthasya saṃkhyayā  RKV 
ayonije mahādevaṃ snāpayed gandhavāriṇā 
madhukṣīreṇa dadhnā vā sa labhed vipulāṃ śriyam  RKV 
aṣṭabhyāṃ ca site pakṣe asitāṃ vā caturdaśīm 
pūjayitvā mahādevaṃ prīṇayed gītavādyakaiḥ  RKV 
vasetsa ca śive loke ye kurvanti manoharam 
te vasanti śive loke yāvad ābhūtasamplavam  RKV 
tasya devasya bhaktyā tu yaḥ karoti pradakṣiṇām 
vijñāpayaṃśca satataṃ mantreṇānena bhārata  RKV 
tasya yatphalamuddiṣṭaṃ pāramparyeṇa mānavaiḥ 
sakāśāddevadevasya tacchṛṇuṣva samādhinā  RKV 
ayonijo mahādeva yathā tvaṃ parameśvara 
tathā mocaya māṃ śarva sambhavādyonisaṅkaṭāt  RKV 
kiṃ tasya bahubhirmantraiḥ kaṃṭhaśoṣaṇatatparaiḥ 
yenauṃnamaḥ śivāyeti proktaṃ devasya saṃnidhau  RKV 
tenādhītaṃ śrutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam 
yenauṃnamaḥ śivāyeti mantrābhyāsaḥ sthirīkṛtaḥ  RKV 
na tatphalamavāpnoti sarvadeveṣu vai dvijaḥ 
yatphalaṃ samavāpnoti ṣaḍakṣara udīraṇāt  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayecchivayoginam 
dvijānāmayutaṃ sāgraṃ sa labhet phalamuttamam  RKV 
athavā bhaktiyuktastu teṣāṃ dānte jitendriye 
saṃskṛtya dadate bhikṣāṃ phalaṃ tasya tato 'dhikam  RKV 
yatihaste jalaṃ dadyād bhikṣāṃ dattvā punarjalam 
sā bhikṣā meruṇā tulyā tajjalaṃ sāgaropamam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe ayoniprabhavatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra agnitīrthamanuttamam 
tatra snātvā tu pakṣādau mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kanyāṃ dadyāt svayamalaṃkṛtām 
tasya yatphalamuddiṣṭaṃ tacchṛṇuṣva narottama  RKV 
agniṣṭomātirātrābhyāṃ śataṃ śataguṇīkṛtam 
prāpnoti puruṣo dattvā yathāśaktyā hyalaṃkṛtām  RKV 
tasyāḥ putraprapautrāṇāṃ yā bhaved romasaṃgatiḥ 
sa yāti tena mānena śivaloke parāṃ gatim  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe agnitīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra bhṛkuṭeśvaram uttamam 
yatra siddho mahābhāgo bhṛguḥ paramakopanaḥ  RKV 
tena varṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ tapaścīrṇaṃ purānagha 
putrārthaṃ varayāmāsa putraṃ putravatāṃ varaḥ  RKV 
varo datto mahābhāga devenāndhakaghātinā 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet parameśvaram  RKV 
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ labhet 
bhṛkuṭeśaṃ tu yaḥ kaścid ghṛtena madhunā saha  RKV 
putrārthī snāpayed bhaktyā sa labhet putramīpsitam 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā dadyād viprāya kāñcanam  RKV 
godānaṃ vā mahīṃ vāpi tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  RKV 
sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā 
dattā pṛthvī na sandehas tena sarvā nṛpottama  RKV 
tena dānena sa svarge krīḍayitvā yathāsukham 
martye bhavati rājendro brāhmaṇo vā supūjitaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe bhṛkuṭeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāviṃśatyuttaraśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchen mahīpāla brahmatīrthamanuttamam 
anyeṣāṃ caiva tīrthānāṃ parātparataraṃ mahat  RKV 
tatra tīrthe suraśreṣṭho brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
caturṇāmapi varṇānāṃ narmadātaṭamāśritaḥ  RKV 
vācikaṃ mānasaṃ pāpaṃ karmajaṃ yatpurākṛtam 
tatkṣālayati deveśo darśanād eva pātakam  RKV 
śrutismṛtyuditānyeva tatra snātvā dvijarṣabhāḥ 
prāyaścittāni kurvanti teṣāṃ vāsastriviṣṭape  RKV 
ye punaḥ śāstramutsṛjya kāmalobhaprapīḍitāḥ 
prāyaścittaṃ vadiṣyanti te vai nirayagāminaḥ  RKV 
snātvādau pātakī brahmannatvā tu kīrtayed agham 
tasya tannaśyate kṣipraṃ tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayet pitṛdevatāḥ 
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya sa labhet phalamuttamam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yad dānaṃ brahmoddiśya prayacchati 
tadakṣayaphalaṃ sarvamityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt  RKV 
gāyatrīsāramātro 'pi tatra yaḥ kriyate japaḥ 
ṛgyajuḥsāmasahitaḥ sa bhavennātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā tyajeddehaṃ sudustyajam 
anivartikā gatistasya brahmalokān na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
yāvadasthīni tiṣṭhanti brahmatīrthe ca dehinām 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi devaloke mahīyate  RKV 
avatīrṇastato loke brahmajño jāyate kule 
uttamaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ devānāmiva devatā  RKV 
vidyāsthānāni sarvāṇi vetti vedāṅgapāragaḥ 
jāyate pūjito loke rājabhiḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
putrapautrasamopetaḥ sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ 
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ brahmatīrthaprabhāvataḥ  RKV 
etatpuṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ jñānavatāṃ varam 
ye paśyanti mahātmāno hyamṛtatvaṃ prayānti te  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe brahmatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśadadhikaśatatamo

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle devatīrthamanuttamam 
tatra devaiḥ samāgatya toṣitaḥ parameśvaraḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ 
sa labhennātra sandeho gosahasraphalaṃ dhruvam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe devatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma triṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle nāgatīrthamanuttamam 
yatra siddhā mahānāgā bhaye jāte tato nṛpa  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
mahābhayānāṃ lokasya nāgānāṃ dvijasattama 
kathaṃ jātaṃ bhayaṃ tīvraṃ yena te tapasi sthitāḥ  RKV 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca yatsurāsuramānave 
tāta te viditaṃ sarvaṃ tena me kautukaṃ mahat  RKV 
mama saṃtāpajaṃ duḥkhaṃ duryodhanasamudbhavam 
tava vaktrāmbujaughena plāvitaṃ nirvṛtiṃ gatam  RKV 
śrutvā tava mukhodgītāṃ kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśanīm 
bhūyo bhūyaḥ smṛtirjātā śravaṇe mama suvrata  RKV 
na kleśatvaṃ dvije yuktaṃ na cānyo jānate phalam 
vidyādānasya mahataḥ śrāvitasya sutasya ca  RKV 
evaṃ jñātvā yathānyāyaṃ yaḥ praśnaḥ pṛcchito mayā 
kathā tu kathyatāṃ vipra dayāṃ kṛtvā mamopari  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
yathā yathā tvaṃ nṛpa bhāṣase ca tathā tathā me sukhameti bhāratī 
śaithilyabhāvājjarayānvitasya tvatsauhṛdaṃ naśyati naiva tāta  RKV 
kathayāmi yathāvṛttam itihāsaṃ purātanam 
kathitaṃ pūrvato vṛddhaiḥ pāramparyeṇa bhārata  RKV 
dve bhārye kaśyapasyāstāṃ sarvalokeṣvanuttame 
garutmato vai vinatā sarpāṇāṃ kadrureva ca  RKV 
aśvasaṃdarśanāt tābhyāṃ kalirūpaṃ vyavasthitam 
prabhātakāle rājendra bhāskarākāravarcasam  RKV 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā vinatā rūpam aśvaṃ sarvatra pāṇḍuram 
atha tāṃ kadrūmavocatsā paśya paśya varānane  RKV 
uccaiḥśravasaḥ sādṛśyaṃ paśya sarvatra pāṇḍuram 
dhāvamānam aviśrāntaṃ javena pavanopamam  RKV 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā yāntam īrṣyābhāvena mohitā 
kṛṣṇaṃ matvā tathājalpattayā saha nṛpottama  RKV 
vinate tvaṃ mṛṣā loke nṛśaṃse kulapāṃsani 
kṛṣṇaṃ cainaṃ vada śvetaṃ narakaṃ yāsyase param  RKV 
vinatovāca
satyānṛte tu vacane paṇo 'yaṃ te mamaiva tu 
sahasraṃ vatsarāndāsī bhaveyaṃ tava veśmani  RKV 
tatheti te pratijñāya rātrau gatvā svakaṃ gṛham 
parityajya ubhe te tu krodhamūrchitamūrchite  RKV 
bandhugarvasya gatvā tu kathayāmāsa taṃ paṇam 
kadrūrvinatayā sārddhaṃ yadvṛttaṃ pramadālaye  RKV 
tacchrutvā bāndhavāḥ sarve kadrūputrāstathaiva ca 
na manyante hitaṃ kāryaṃ kṛtaṃ mātrā vigarhitam  RKV 
akṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇatām amba kathaṃ gaccheddhayottamaḥ 
dāsatvaṃ prāpsyase tvaṃ hi paṇenānena suvrate  RKV 
kadrūruvāca
bhaveyaṃ na yathādāsī tatkurudhvaṃ hi satvaram 
viśadhvaṃ romakūpeṣu tasyāśvasya matirmama  RKV 
kṣaṇamātraṃ kṛte kārye sā dāsī ca bhavenmama 
tataḥ svasthoragāḥ sarve bhaviṣyatha yathāsukham  RKV 
sarpā ūcuḥ 
yathā tvaṃ jananī devi pannagānāṃ matā bhuvi 
tathāpi sā viśeṣeṇa vañcitavyā na karhicit  RKV 
kadrūruvāca
mama vākyamakurvāṇā ye kecidbhuvi pannagāḥ 
havyavāhamukhaṃ sarve te yāsyantyavicāritāḥ  RKV 
etacchrutvā tu vacanaṃ ghoraṃ mātṛmukhodbhavam 
kecitpraviṣṭā romāṇi tathānye girisaṃsthitāḥ  RKV 
kecitpraviṣṭā jāhnavyāmanye ca tapasi sthitāḥ  RKV 
tato varṣasahasrānte tutoṣa parameśvaraḥ 
mahādevo jagaddhātā hyuvāca parayā girā  RKV 
bho bhoḥ sarpā nivartadhvaṃ tapaso 'sya mahatphalam 
yamicchatha dadāmyadya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
sarpā ūcuḥ 
kadrūśāpabhayādbhītā devadeva maheśvara 
tava pārśve vasiṣyāmo yāvadābhūtasamplavam  RKV 
devadeva uvāca
ekaścāyaṃ mahābāhurvāsukirbhujagottamaḥ 
mama pārśve vasennityaṃ sarveṣāṃ bhayarakṣakaḥ  RKV 
anyeṣāṃ caiva sarpāṇāṃ bhayaṃ nāsti mamājñayā 
āplutya narmadātoye bhujagāste ca rakṣitāḥ  RKV 
nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ teṣāṃ vasadhvaṃ yatra cepsitam 
kadrūśāpabhayaṃ nāsti hyeṣa me vistaraḥ paraḥ  RKV 
evaṃ dattvā varaṃ teṣāṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ 
jagāmākāśamāviśya kailāsaṃ dharaṇīdharam  RKV 
gate cādarśanaṃ deve vāsukipramukhā nṛpa 
sthāpayitvā tathā jagmurdevadevaṃ maheśvaram  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścit pañcamyāmarcayecchivam 
tasya nāgakulānyaṣṭau na hiṃsanti kadācana  RKV 
mṛtaḥ kālena mahatā tatra tīrthe nareśvara 
śivasyānucaro bhūtvā vasate kālamīpsitam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe nāgeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikatriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra uttare narmadātaṭe 
sarvapāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ vārāhaṃ nāma nāmataḥ  RKV 
tatra devo jagaddhātā vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ 
sthito lokahitārthāya saṃsārārṇavatārakaḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed dharaṇīdharam 
gandhamālyaviśeṣaiśca jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ  RKV 
upavāsaparo bhūtvā dvādaśyāṃ nṛpasattama 
vṛṣalāḥ pāpakarmāṇas tathaivāndhapiśācinaḥ  RKV 
ālāpād gātrasaṃparkān niḥśvāsāt sahabhojanāt 
pāpaṃ saṃkramate yasmāt tasmāt tān parivarjayet  RKV 
brāhmaṇān pūjayed bhaktyā yathāśaktyā yathāvidhi 
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kāryaṃ kathāyāṃ tatra bhārata  RKV 
prabhāte vimale snātvā tatra tīrthe jagadgurum 
ye paśyanti jitakrodhāste muktāḥ sarvapātakaiḥ  RKV 
yathā tu dṛṣṭvā bhujagāḥ suparṇaṃ naśyanti muktvā viṣamugratejaḥ 
naśyanti pāpāni tathaiva śīghraṃ dṛṣṭvā mukhaṃ śūkararūpiṇastu  RKV 
nabhogataṃ naśyati cāndhakāraṃ dṛṣṭvā raviṃ devavaraṃ tathaiva 
naśyanti pāpāni sudustarāṇi dṛṣṭvā mukhaṃ pārtha dharādharasya  RKV 
kiṃ tasya bahubhir mantrair bhaktir yasya janārdane 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ  RKV 
eko 'pi kṛṣṇasya kṛtaḥ praṇāmo daśāśvamedhāvabhṛthena tulyaḥ 
daśāśvamedhī punareti janma kṛṣṇapraṇāmī na punarbhavāya  RKV 
dhyāyamānā mahātmāno rūpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ hareḥ 
ye tyajanti svakaṃ dehaṃ tatra tīrthe jitendriyāḥ  RKV 
te gacchantyamalaṃ sthānaṃ yatsurair api durlabham 
kṣarākṣaravinirmuktaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe ādivārāhatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ

tato gacchenmahīpāla paraṃ tīrthacatuṣṭayam

kauberaṃ vāruṇaṃ yāmyaṃ vāyavyaṃ tu tataḥ param 
yatra siddhā mahāprājñā lokapālā mahābalāḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kimarthaṃ lokapālaiśca tapaścīrṇaṃ purānagha 
narmadātaṭamāśritya hyetanme vaktumarhasi  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca

varadaṃ prārthayāmāsur devaṃ varam anuttamam  RKV 
kubera uvāca

krīḍeyaṃ vāruṇe loke yādogaṇasamanvitaḥ  RKV 
jagādāśu tato vāyuḥ praṇamya tu maheśvaram 
vyāpakatvaṃ trilokeṣu prārthayāmāsa bhārata  RKV

gate maheśvare deve yathāsthānaṃ tu te sthitāḥ 
sthāpanā ca kṛtā sarvaiḥ svanāmnaiva pṛthakpṛthak  RKV 
kuberaśca kubereśaṃ yamaścaiva yameśvaram

tarpaṇaṃ vidadhuḥ sarve mantraiśca vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ

āhvayāmāsus tān viprānsarve sarveśvarā iva 
kṣāntadāntajitakrodhānsarvabhūtābhayapradān  RKV 
vedavidyāvratasnātān sarvaśāstraviśāradān 
ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃyuktāṃs tathātharvavibhūṣitān  RKV

tatra sthāne dadus teṣāṃ bhūmidānam anuttamam 
yāvaccandraśca sūryaśca yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī  RKV 
tāvaddānaṃ tu yuṣmākaṃ paripanthī na kaścana

śoṣayeddhanado vittaṃ tasya pāpasya bhārata  RKV

āyurnayati tasyāśu yamaḥ saṃyamano mahān  RKV 
niḥśeṣaṃ bhasmasāt kṛtvā hutabhugyāti bhārata 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira 
bhaktiḥ kāryā nṛpaiḥ sarvair icchadbhiḥ śreya ātmanaḥ  RKV 
rājā vṛkṣo brāhmaṇāstasya mūlaṃ bhṛtyāḥ parṇā mantriṇastasya śākhāḥ

ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi svarge tiṣṭhati bhūmidaḥ

svadattā paradattā vā pālanīyā vasuṃdharā

devatājñāmanusmṛtya rājāno ye 'pi tāṃ nṛpa

svadattā paradattā vā yatnādrakṣyā yudhiṣṭhira 
mahī mahīkṣitā nityaṃ dānācchreyo 'nupālanam  RKV 
āyuryaśo balaṃ vittaṃ saṃtatiścākṣayā nṛpa

evamuktvā tu tān sarvāṃllokapālān dvijottamān

alabdhagrāsamarddhārdhaṃ niryayur nagarādbahiḥ  RKV

daridrāḥ satataṃ mūrkhā bhaveyuśca yayurgṛhān  RKV 
tadāprabhṛti te sarve brāhmaṇā dhanavarjitāḥ

gandhadhūpanamaskāraiḥ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  RKV

sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyeta saptajanmāntarārjitaiḥ  RKV

yaḥ karoti tilaiḥ snānaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  RKV 
sutṛptāstena toyena pitaraśca pitāmahāḥ

vājapeyasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti puṣkalam  RKV

nityaṃ vasanti kaurilyāṃ lokapālānnimantrya ye  RKV 
etatpuṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyamāyurvivardhanam 
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe kuberāditīrthacatuṣṭayamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma trayastriṃśadadhikaśatatamo

kṛtaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ māsaṃ kṛcchraṃ cānyaṃ tataḥ param

jagāmādarśanaṃ bhūyo reme comāpatiściram

bahavastaṃ na jānanti kāmarāgasamanvitāḥ 
narmadāyā hradaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapātakanāśanam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā nandāṃ devīṃ prapūjayet 
kiṃ tasya himavanmadhyagamanena prayojanam  RKV 
paramārthamavijñāya paryaṭanti tamovṛtāḥ 
teṣāṃ samāgame pārtha śrama eva hi kevalam  RKV 
pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ snānadānena yatphalam 
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti snātvā nandāhrade nṛpa  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe nandāhradatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchen mahīpāla tāpeśvaramanuttamam 
yatra sā hariṇī siddhā vyādhabhītā nareśvara  RKV 
jale prakṣipya gātrāṇi hyantarikṣaṃ gatā tu sā 
vyādho vismitacittastu tāṃ mṛgīmavalokya ca  RKV 
vimucya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ prārebhe tapa uttamam 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu vyādhenācaritaṃ tapaḥ  RKV 
atīte tu tataḥ kāle parituṣṭo maheśvaraḥ 
varaṃ brūhi mahāvyādha yatte manasi rocate  RKV 
vyādha uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si deveśa yadi deyo varo mama 
tava pārśve mahādeva vāso me pratidīyatām  RKV 
īśvara uvāca
evaṃ bhavatu te vyādha yastvayā kāṅkṣito varaḥ 
daivadevo mahādeva ityuktvāntaradhīyata 
gate cādarśanaṃ deve sthāpayitvā maheśvaram  RKV 
pūjayitvā vidhānena gato vyādhastato divam 
tadāprabhṛti tattīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam  RKV 
vyādhānutāpasaṃjātaṃ tāpeśvaramiti śrutam 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā sampūjayati śaṅkaram  RKV 
śivalokamavāpnoti māmuvāca maheśvaraḥ 
ye snātā narmadātoye tīrthe tāpeśvare narāḥ  RKV 
tāpatrayavimuktāste nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  RKV 
snānaṃ samācaren nityaṃ sarvapātakaśāntaye  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe tāpeśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja rukmiṇītīrthamuttamam 
yatraiva snānamātreṇa rūpavānsubhago bhavet  RKV 
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
snānaṃ samācaret tatra na ceha jāyate punaḥ  RKV 
yaḥ snātvā rukmiṇītīrthe dānaṃ dadyāttu kāṃcanam 
tattīrthasya prabhāvena śokaṃ nāpnoti mānavaḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
tīrthasyāsya kathaṃ jāto mahimedṛṅmunīśvara 
rūpasaubhāgyadaṃ yena tīrtham etad bravīhi me  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
kathayāmi yathāvṛttamitihāsaṃ purātanam 
kathitaṃ pūrvato vṛddhaiḥ pāramparyeṇa bhārata  RKV 
taṃ te 'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikāgramānasaḥ 
nagaraṃ kuṇḍinaṃ nāma bhīṣmakaḥ paripāti hi  RKV 
hastyaśvarathasampanno dhanāḍhyo 'ti pratāpavān 
strīsahasrasya madhyasthaḥ kurute rājyamuttamam  RKV 
tasya bhāryā mahādevī prāṇebhyo 'pi garīyasī 
tasyāmutpādayāmāsa putramekaṃ ca rukmakam  RKV 
dvitīyā tanayā jajñe rukmiṇī nāma nāmataḥ 
tadāśarīriṇī vācā rājānaṃ tamuvāca ha  RKV 
caturbhujāya dātavyā kanyeyaṃ bhuvi bhīṣmaka 
evaṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā jaharṣa priyayā saha  RKV 
brāhmaṇaiḥ saha vidvadbhiḥ praviṣṭaḥ sūtikāgṛham 
svastikaṃ vācayitvāsyāścakre nāmeti rukmiṇī  RKV 
yataḥ suvarṇatilako janmanā saha bhārata 
tataḥ sā rukmiṇīnāma brāhmaṇaiḥ kīrtitā tadā  RKV 
tataḥ sā kālaparyāyādaṣṭavarṣā vyajāyata 
pūrvoktaṃ caiva tadvākyamaśarīriṇyudīritam  RKV 
smṛtvā smṛtvātha nṛpatiścintayāmāsa bhūpatiḥ 
kasmai deyā mayā bālā bhavitā kaścaturbhujaḥ  RKV 
etasminnantare tāvadraivatātparvatottamāt 
mukhyaścedipatistatra damaghoṣaḥ samāgataḥ  RKV 
praviṣṭo rājasadanaṃ yatra rājā sa bhīṣmakaḥ 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā cāgataṃ gehe pūjayāmāsa bhūpatiḥ  RKV 
āsanaṃ vipulaṃ dattvā sabhāṃ gatvā niveśitaḥ 
kuśalaṃ tava rājendra damaghoṣa śriyāyuta  RKV 
puṇyāhamadya saṃjātamahaṃ tvaddarśanotsukaḥ 
kanyā madīyā rājendra hyaṣṭavarṣā vyajāyata  RKV 
caturbhujāya dātavyā vāguvācāśarīriṇī 
bhīṣmakasya vacaḥ śrutvā damaghoṣo 'bravīd idam  RKV 
caturbhujo mama sutastriṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ 
tasyeyaṃ dīyatāṃ kanyā śiśupālasya bhīṣmaka  RKV 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā damaghoṣasya bhūmipa 
bhīṣmakena tato dattā śiśupālāya rukmiṇī  RKV 
prārabdhaṃ maṅgalaṃ tatra bhīṣmakeṇa yudhiṣṭhira 
dikṣu deśāntareṣveva ye vasanti svagotrajāḥ  RKV 
nimantritāstu te sarve samājagmur yathākramam 
tato yādavavaṃśasya tilakau balakeśavau  RKV 
nimantritau samāyātau kuṇḍinaṃ bhīṣmakasya tu 
bhīṣmakeṇa yathānyāyaṃ pūjitau tau yadūttamau  RKV 
tataḥ pradoṣasamaye rukmiṇī kāmamohinī 
sakhībhiḥ sahitā yātā pūrbahiścāmbikārcane  RKV 
sāpaśyat tatra deveśaṃ gopaveṣadharaṃ harim 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā mohamāpannā kāmena kaluṣīkṛtā  RKV 
keśavo 'pi ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃkarṣaṇam uvāca ha 
strīratnapravaraṃ tāta hartavyamiti me matiḥ  RKV 
keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā saṃkarṣaṇa uvāca ha 
gaccha kṛṣṇa mahābāho strīratnaṃ cāśu gṛhyatām  RKV 
ahaṃ ca tava mārgeṇa hyāgamiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhataḥ 
dānavānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kurvaṃśca kadanaṃ mahat  RKV 
saṃkarṣaṇamataṃ prāpya keśavaḥ keśisūdanaḥ 
yayau kanyāṃ gṛhītvā tu rathamāropya satvaram  RKV 
nirgataḥ sahasā rājanvegenaivānilo yathā 
hāhākāras tadā jāto bhīṣmakasya pure mahān  RKV 
nirgatā dānavāḥ kruddhā velā iva mahodadheḥ 
garjantaḥ sāyudhāḥ sarve dhāvanto rathavartmani  RKV 
baladevaṃ tataḥ prāptā rathamārgānugāminam 
teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ balasyāsīt sarvalokakṣayaṃkaram  RKV 
yathā tārāmaye pūrvaṃ saṅgrāme lokaviśrute 
gadāhasto mahābāhus trailokye 'pratimo balaḥ  RKV 
halenākṛṣya sahasā gadāpātairapātayat 
aśakyo dānavairhantuṃ balabhadro mahābalaḥ  RKV 
babhañja dānavānsarvāṃstasthau giririvācalaḥ 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā ca balaṃ kruddhaṃ durdharṣaṃ tridaśairapi  RKV 
bhīṣmaputro mahātejā rukmīnām mahayaśāḥ 
narāṇāmatiśūrāṇām akṣauhiṇyā samanvitaḥ  RKV 
balabhadramatikramya tato yuddhe nirākarot 
tadyuddhaṃ vañcayitvā tu rathamārgeṇa satvaram  RKV 
keśavo 'pi tadā devo rukmiṇyā sahito yayau 
vindhyaṃ tu laṅghayitvāgre trailokyagururavyayaḥ  RKV 
narmadātaṭamāpede yatra siddhaḥ purā punaḥ 
ajeyo yena saṃjātastīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ  RKV 
etasmāt kāraṇāt tāta yodhanīpuram ucyate 
rukmo 'pi dānavendro 'sau prāptaḥ  RKV 
pratyuvācācyutaṃ kruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti mā vraja 
adya tvāṃ niśitairbāṇairneṣyāmi yamasādanam  RKV 
evaṃ parasparaṃ vīrau jagarjaturubhāvapi 
tayoryuddhamabhūdghoraṃ tārakāgnijasannibham  RKV 
cikṣepa śarajālāni keśavaṃ prati dānavaḥ 
nānucintya śarāṃs tasya keśavaḥ keśisūdanaḥ  RKV 
tato viṣṇuḥ svayaṃ kruddhaścakraṃ gṛhya sudarśanam 
sampraharatyamuṃ yāvadrukmiṇyātra nivāritaḥ  RKV 
tvāṃ na jānāti deveśaṃ caturbāhuṃ janārdanam 
darśayasva svakaṃ rūpaṃ dayāṃ kṛtvā mamopari  RKV 
evamuktastu rukmiṇyā darśayāmāsa bhārata 
devā dṛṣṭvāpi tadrūpaṃ stuvantyākāśasaṃsthitāḥ 
divyaṃ cakṣus tadā devo dadau rukmasya bhārata  RKV 
rukma uvāca
yanmayā pāpaniṣṭhena mandabhāgyena keśava 
sāyakairāhataṃ vakṣastatsarvaṃ kṣantumarhasi  RKV 
pūrvaṃ dattā svayaṃ deva jānakī janakena vai 
mayā pradattā deveśa rukmiṇī tava keśava  RKV 
udvāhaya yathānyāyaṃ vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā 
rukmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā tatastuṣṭo jagadguruḥ  RKV 
babhāṣe devadeveśo rukmiṇaṃ bhīṣmakātmajam 
gaccha svakaṃ puraṃ mā bhaiḥ kuru rājyamakaṇṭakam  RKV 
keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā rukmo dānavapuṃgavaḥ 
taṃ praṇamya jagannāthaṃ jagāma bhavanaṃ pituḥ  RKV 
gate rukme tadā kṛṣṇaḥ samāmantrya dvijottamān 
marīcimatryaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum  RKV 
vasiṣṭhaṃ ca mahābhāgamityete sapta mānasāḥ 
ityete brāhmaṇāḥ sapta purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ  RKV 
kṣamāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharṣibhir alaṃkṛtāḥ 
ityevaṃ brahmaputrāśca satyavanto mahāmate  RKV 
narmadātaṭamāśritya nivasanti jitendriyāḥ 
tapaḥsvādhyāyaniratā japahomaparāyaṇāḥ  RKV 
nimantritāstu rājendra keśavena mahātmanā 
śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ brahmoktavidhinā tataḥ  RKV 
haristānpūjayāmāsa saptabrahmarṣipuṃgavān 
pradadau dvādaśa grāmāṃstebhyastatra janārdanaḥ  RKV 
yāvaccandraśca sūryaśca yāvattiṣṭhati medinī 
tāvaddānaṃ mayā dattaṃ paripanthī na kaścana  RKV 
maddattaṃ pālayiṣyante ye nṛpā gatakalmaṣāḥ 
tebhyaḥ svasti kariṣyāmi dāsyāmi paramāṃ gatim  RKV 
yāvaddhi yānti lokeṣu mahābhūtāni pañca ca 
tāvatte divi modante maddattaparipālakāḥ  RKV 
yastu lopayate mūḍho dattaṃ vaḥ pṛthivītale 
narake tasya vāsaḥ syād yāvadābhūtasamplavam  RKV 
svadattā paradattā vā pālanīyā vasuṃdharā 
yasya yasya yadā bhūmis tasya tasya tadā phalam  RKV 
svadattāṃ paradattāṃ vā yo hareta vasuṃdharām 
sa viṣṭhāyāṃ kṛmirbhūtvā pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati  RKV 
anyāyena hṛtā bhūmiranyāyena ca hāritā 
hartā hārayitā caiva viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ  RKV 
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi svarge tiṣṭhati bhūmidaḥ 
ācchettā cānumantā ca tānyeva narake vaset  RKV 
yānīha dattāni purā narendrair dānāni dharmārthayaśaskarāṇi 
nirmālyarūpapratimāni tāni ko nāma sādhuḥ punarādadāti  RKV 
evaṃ tānpūjayitvā tu samyaṅ nyāyena pāṇḍava 
rukmiṇyā vidhivatpāṇiṃ jagrāha madhusūdanaḥ  RKV 
muśalī ca tataḥ sarvāñjitvā dānavapuṃgavān 
svasthānam agamat tatra kṛtvā kāryaṃ suśobhanam  RKV 
prayātau dvāravatyāṃ tau kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇāvubhau 
gacchamānaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā keśavaṃ kleśanāśanam  RKV 
brāhmaṇāḥ satyavantaśca nirgatāḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ 
āgacchamānāṃs tau vīkṣya rathamārgeṇa brāhmaṇān  RKV 
muhūrtaṃ tatra viśramya keśavo vākyam abravīt 
kimāgamanakāryaṃ vo brūta sarvaṃ dvijottamāḥ  RKV 
kurvāṇāḥ svīyakarmāṇi mama kṛtyaṃ tu tiṣṭhate 
devasya vacanaṃ śrutvā munayo vākyam abruvan  RKV 
kalpakoṭisahasreṇa satyabhāvāttu vanditaḥ 
duṣprāpyo 'si manuṣyāṇāṃ prāptaḥ kiṃ tyajase hi naḥ  RKV 
brāhmaṇānāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān idam abravīt 
mathurāyāṃ dvāravatyāṃ yodhanīpura eva ca  RKV 
trikālamāgamiṣyāmi satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ 
evaṃ te brāhmaṇāḥ śrutvā yodhanīpuramāgatāḥ  RKV 
avatīrṇastribhāgena prādurbhāve tu māthure 
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tīrthasyotpattikāraṇam  RKV 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca vartamānaṃ tathāparam 
yaṃ śrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed balakeśavau 
tena devo jagaddhātā pūjitastriguṇātmavān  RKV 
upavāsī naro bhūtvā yastu kuryāt pradakṣiṇam 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu ye vṛkṣāstānpaśyantyapi ye narāḥ 
te 'pi pāpaiḥ pramucyante bhrūṇahatyāsamair api  RKV 
prātarutthāya ye kecitpaśyanti balakeśavau 
tena te sadṛśāḥ syur vai devadevena cakriṇā  RKV 
te pūjyāste namaskāryās teṣāṃ janma sujīvitam 
ye namanti jagannāthaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaddānaṃ snānaṃ devārcanaṃ nṛpa 
tatsarvamakṣayaṃ tasya ityevaṃ śaṅkaro 'bravīt  RKV 
praviśyāgnau mṛtānāṃ ca yatphalaṃ samudāhṛtam 
tacchṛṇuṣva nṛpaśreṣṭha procyamānamaśeṣataḥ  RKV 
vimānenārkavarṇena kiṃkiṇījālamālinā 
āgneye bhavate tatra modate kālamīpsitam  RKV 
jale caivā mṛtānāṃ tu yodhanīpuramadhyataḥ 
vasanti vāruṇe loke yāvadābhūtasamplavam  RKV 
anāśake mṛtānāṃ tu tatra tīrthe narādhipa 
anivartikā gatir nṛṇāṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yo dadyāt kapilādānamuttamam 
vidhānena tu saṃyuktaṃ śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam  RKV 
yāvanti tasyā romāṇi tatprasūteśca bhārata 
tāvanti divi modante sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitāḥ  RKV 
yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti dhenvāstāvanti varṣāṇi mahīyate saḥ 
svargāc cyutaścāpi tatastrilokyāṃ kule samutpatsyati gomatāṃ saḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yo dadyād rūpyaṃ kāñcanameva vā 
kāñcanena vimānena viṣṇuloke mahīyate  RKV 
tasmiṃstīrthe tu yo dadyāt pāduke vastram eva ca 
dānasyāsya prabhāvena labhate svargamīpsitam  RKV 
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedānāṃ paṭhanād yatphalaṃ bhavet 
tatra tīrthe tu rājendra gāyatryā tatphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
prayāge yadbhavetpuṇyaṃ gayāyāṃ ca tripuṣkare 
kurukṣetre tu rājendra rāhugraste divākare  RKV 
someśvare ca yatpuṇyaṃ somasya grahaṇe tathā 
tatphalaṃ labhate tatra snānamātrān na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
dvādaśyāṃ tu naraḥ snātvā namaskṛtya janārdanam 
uddhṛtāḥ pitarastena avāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam  RKV 
saṃkrāntau ca vyatīpāte dvādaśyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayed ekaṃ koṭirbhavati bhojitā  RKV 
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni hyāsamudrāṇi pāṇḍava 
tāni sarvāṇi tatraiva dvādaśyāṃ pāṇḍunandana  RKV 
kṣayaṃ yānti ca dānāni yajñahomabalikriyāḥ 
na kṣīyate mahārāja tatra tīrthe tu yatkṛtam  RKV 
yadbhūtaṃ yadbhaviṣyacca tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam 
kathitaṃ te mayā sarvaṃ pṛthagbhāvena bhārata  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe rukmiṇītīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvicatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja yojaneśvaram uttamam 
yatra siddhau purā kalpe naranārāyaṇāvṛṣī  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tapastaptvā saṅgrāme devadānavaiḥ 
jayaṃ prāptau mahātmānau naranārāyaṇāvubhau  RKV 
punastretāyuge prāpte tau devau rāmalakṣmaṇau 
tatra tīrthe punaḥ snātvā rāvaṇo durjayo hataḥ  RKV 
punaḥ pārtha kalau prāpte tau devau balakeśavau 
vasudevakule jātau duṣkaraṃ karma cakratuḥ  RKV 
narakaṃ kālanemiṃ ca kaṃsaṃ cāṇūramuṣṭikau 
śiśupālaṃ jarāsaṃdhaṃ jaghnatur balakeśavau  RKV 
tatastatra ripūnsaṃkhye bhīṣmadroṇapuraḥsarān 
karṇaduryodhanādīṃśca nihaniṣyati sa prabhuḥ  RKV 
dharmakṣetre kurukṣetre tatra yudhyanti te kṣaṇam 
bhīmārjunanimittena śiṣyau kṛtvā parasparam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe punargatvā tapaḥ kṛtvā suduṣkaram 
pūjayitvā dvijānbhaktyā yāsyete dvārakāṃ punaḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed balakeśavau 
tena devo jagaddhātā pūjitastriguṇātmavān  RKV 
upavāsī naro bhūtvā yastu kuryāt prajāgaram 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo gāyaṃstasya śubhāṃ kathām  RKV 
yāvatastatra tīrthe tu vṛkṣān paśyanti mānavāḥ 
brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ tāvad eṣāṃ praṇaśyati  RKV 
prātarutthāya ye kecit paśyanti balakeśavau 
tenaiva sadṛśāḥ sarve devadevena cakriṇā  RKV 
te pūjyāste namaskāryāsteṣāṃ janma sujīvitam 
ye namanti jagatpūjyaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaddānaṃ snānaṃ devārcanaṃ nṛpa 
kriyate tatphalaṃ sarvamakṣayāyopakalpate  RKV 
agnerapatyaṃ prathamaṃ suvarṇaṃ bhūrvaiṣṇavī sūryasutāśca gāvaḥ 
lokāstrayastena bhavanti dattā yaḥ kāñcanaṃ gāṃ ca bhuvaṃ ca dadyāt  RKV 
etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam 
atītaṃ ca bhaviṣyacca vartamānaṃ mahābalam  RKV 
śrutvā vāpi paṭhitvedaṃ śrāvayipatvātha dhārmikān 
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe yojaneśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahārāja dvādaśītīrthamuttamam 
kṣaranti sarvadānāni japahomabalikriyāḥ  RKV 
na kṣīyate tu rājendra cakratīrthe tu yatkṛtam 
yadbhūtaṃ yadbhaviṣyacca tīrthamāhātmyamuttamam  RKV 
kathitaṃ tanmayā sarvaṃ pṛthagbhāvena bhārata  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe dvādaśītīrthamahātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma catuścatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gaccheddharāpāla śīvatīrthamanuttamam 
darśanādyasya devasya mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ  RKV 
śivatīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ 
pūjayeta mahādevaṃ so 'gniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā sopavāso 'rcayecchivam 
anivartikā gatistasya rudralokād asaṃśayam  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe śivatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
asmāhakaṃ tato gacchet pitṛtīrthamanuttamam 
pretatvādyatra mucyante piṇḍenaikena pūrvajāḥ  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
asmāhakasya māhātmyaṃ kathayasva mamānagha 
snānadānena yatpuṇyaṃ tathā piṇḍodakena ca  RKV 
śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
purā kalpe nṛpaśreṣṭha ṛṣidevasamāgame 
praśnaḥ pṛṣṭo mayā tāta yathā tvamanupṛcchasi  RKV 
ekatra sāgarāḥ sapta saprayāgāḥ sapuṣkarāḥ 
nāsya sāmyaṃ labhante te nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  RKV 
somanāthaṃ tu vikhyātaṃ yatsomena pratiṣṭhitam 
tatra somagrahe puṇyaṃ tatpuṇyaṃ labhate naraḥ  RKV 
māsānte pitaro nṛṇāṃ vīkṣante santatiṃ svakām 
kaścid asmatkule 'smākaṃ piṇḍamatra pradāsyati  RKV 
prapitāmahāstathādityāḥ śrutireṣā sanātanī 
evaṃ bruvanti devāśca ṛṣayaḥ satapodhanāḥ  RKV 
sakṛtpiṇḍodakenaiva śṛṇu pārthiva yatphalam 
dvādaśābdāni rājendra yogaṃ bhuktvā suśobhanam  RKV 
yuge yuge mahārāja asmāhake pitāmahāḥ 
sarvadā hyavalokanta āgacchantaṃ svagotrajam  RKV 
bhaviṣyati kim asmākam amāvāsyāpyamāhake

te sarvapāpanirmuktāḥ sarvānkāmāṃllabhati vai 
jalamadhye 'tra bhūpāla agnitīrthaṃ ca tiṣṭhati  RKV

śuklāmbaradharo nityaṃ niyataḥ sa jitendriyaḥ 
ekakālaṃ tu bhuñjāno māsaṃ tīrthasya sannidhau  RKV 
suvarṇālaṃkṛtānāṃ tu kanyānāṃ śatadānajam

koṭivarṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate

suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhye kule jāyeta rūpavān 
kṛtvābhiṣekavidhinā hayamedhaphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
dhanāḍhyo rūpavāndakṣo dātā bhavati dhārmikaḥ 
caturvedeṣu yatpuṇyaṃ satyavādiṣu yatphalam  RKV 
tatphalaṃ labhate nūnaṃ tatra tīrthe 'bhiṣecanāt 
tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ nirmitaṃ śambhunā purā  RKV 
hṛdayeśaḥ svayaṃ viṣṇur japeddevaṃ maheśvaram 
gandharvāpsarasaścaiva maruto mārutāstathā  RKV 
viśvedevāśca pitaraḥ sacandrāḥ sadivākarāḥ 
marīciratryaṅgirasau pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ  RKV 
pracetāśca vasiṣṭhaśca bhṛgurnārada eva ca 
cyavano gālavaścaiva vāmadevo mahāmuniḥ  RKV 
vālakhilyāśca gandhārāstṛṇabinduśca jājaliḥ 
uddālakaścarṣyaśṛṅgo vasiṣṭhaśca sanandanaḥ  RKV 
śukraścaiva bharadvājo vātsyo vātsyāyanastathā 
agastirmitrāvaruṇau viśvāmitro munīśvaraḥ  RKV 
gautamaśca pulastyaśca paulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ 
sanātanastu kapilo vāhniḥ pañcaśikhastathā  RKV 
anye 'pi bahavastatra munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ 
krīḍanti devatāḥ sarva ṛṣayaḥ satapodhanāḥ  RKV 
manuṣyāścaiva yogīndrāḥ pitaraḥ sapitāmahāḥ 
asmāhake 'tra tiṣṭhanti sarva eva na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
pitaraḥ pitāmahāścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahāḥ 
yeṣāṃ dattamupasthāyi sukṛtaṃ vāpi duṣkṛtam  RKV 
akṣayaṃ tatra tatsarvaṃ yatkṛtaṃ yodhanīpure 
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ tyaktvā sarvabandhusuhṛjjanān  RKV 
dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ priyānputrāṃs tathā dehaṃ nṛpottama 
gacchate vāyubhūtastu śubhāśubhasamanvitaḥ  RKV 
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ paramātmā mahattaraḥ 
śubhāśubhagatiṃ prāptaḥ karmaṇā svena pārthiva  RKV 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śubhāśubhaṃ na bandhūnāṃ jāyate kena hetunā 
ekaḥ prasūyate jantureka eva pralīyate  RKV 
eko hi bhuṅkte sukṛtameka eva hi duṣkṛtam  RKV 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
eṣa tvayokto nṛpate mahāpraśnaḥ smṛto mayā  RKV 
pitāmahamukhodgītaṃ śrutaṃ te kathayāmyaham 
yanme pitāmahātpūrvaṃ vijñātam ṛṣisaṃsadi  RKV 
na mātā na pitā bandhuḥ kasyacinna suhṛtkvacit 
kasya na jñāyate rūpaṃ vāyubhūtasya dehinaḥ  RKV 
yadyevaṃ na bhavettāta lokasya tu nareśvara 
amaryādaṃ bhavennūnaṃ vinaśyati carācaram  RKV 
evaṃ jñātvā pūrā rājansamastairlokakartṛbhiḥ 
maryādā sthāpitā loke yathā dharmo na naśyati  RKV 
dharme naṣṭe manuṣyāṇām adharmo 'bhibhavet punaḥ 
tataḥ svadharmacalanānnarake gamanaṃ dhruvam  RKV 
loko niraṅkuśaḥ sarvo maryādālaṅghane rataḥ 
maryādā sthāpitā tena śāstraṃ vīkṣya maharṣibhiḥ  RKV 
snānaṃ dānaṃ japo homaḥ svādhyāyo devatārcanam 
piṇḍodakapradānaṃ ca tathaivātithipūjanam  RKV 
pitaraḥ pitāmahāścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahāḥ 
trayo devāḥ smṛtāstāta brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  RKV 
pūjitaiḥ pūjitāḥ sarve tathā mātāmahāstrayaḥ 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena śrutismṛtyarthanoditān  RKV 
dharmaṃ samācarannityaṃ pāpāṃśena na lipyate 
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ manasāpi na laṅghayet  RKV 
iha loke pare caiva yadīcchecchreya ātmanaḥ 
pitāputrau sadāpyekau bimbādbimbamivoddhṛtau  RKV 
vibhaktau vāvibhaktau vā śrutismṛtyarthatastathā 
uddharedātmanātmānam ātmānam avasādayet  RKV 
piṇḍodakapradānābhyāmṛte pārtha na saṃśayaḥ 
evaṃ jñātvā prayatnena piṇḍodakaprado bhavet  RKV 
āyurdharmo yaśastejaḥ santatiścaiva vardhate 
pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ pitṛkṣetrāṇi yāni ca  RKV 
tāni te sampravakṣyāmi yeṣu dattaṃ mahāphalam 
gayāyāṃ puṣkare jyeṣṭhe prayāge naimiṣe tathā  RKV 
saṃnihatyāṃ kurukṣetre prabhāse kurunandana 
piṇḍodakapradānena yatphalaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ  RKV 
asmāhake tadāpnoti narmadāyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
tatra brahmā murāriśca rudraśca umayā saha  RKV 
indrādyā devatāḥ sarve pitaro munayastathā 
sāgarāḥ saritaścaiva parvatāśca balāhakāḥ  RKV 
tiṣṭhanti pitaraḥ sarve sarvatīrthādhikaṃ tataḥ 
sthitā brahmaśilā tatra gajakumbhanibhā nṛpa  RKV 
kalau na dṛśyā bhavati pradhānaṃ yadgayāśiraḥ 
vaiśākhe māsi samprāpte 'māvāsyāṃ nṛpottama  RKV 
vyāpya sā tiṣṭhate tīrthaṃ gajakumbhanibhā śilā 
tacca gavyūtimātraṃ hi tīrthaṃ tataḥ pravakṣate  RKV 
tasmindine tatra gatvā yastu śrāddhaprado bhavet 
pitḥṇām akṣayā tṛptirjāyate śatavārṣikī  RKV 
anyasyāmapyamāvāsyāṃ yaḥ snātvā vijitendriyaḥ 
karoti manujaḥ śrāddhaṃ vidhivanmantrasaṃyutam  RKV 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yatsyāt tacchṛṇuṣva narādhipa 
agniṣṭomāśvamedhābhyāṃ vājapeyasya yatphalam  RKV 
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti yathā me śaṅkaro 'bravīt 
rauravādiṣu sarveṣu narakeṣu vyavasthitāḥ  RKV 
pitā pitāmahādyāśca pitṛke mātṛke tathā 
piṇḍodakena caikena tarpaṇena viśeṣataḥ  RKV 
krīḍanti pitṛlokasthā yāvad ābhūtasamplavam 
ye karmasthā vikarmasthā ye jātāḥ pretakalmaṣāḥ  RKV 
piṇḍenaikena mucyante te 'pi tatra na saṃśayaḥ 
asmāhake śilā divyā tiṣṭhate gajasannibhā  RKV 
brahmaṇā nirmitā pūrvaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī 
uparyasyā yathānyāyaṃ pitḥn uddiśya bhārata  RKV 
dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu dadyātpiṇḍānvicakṣaṇaḥ 
bhūmau cānnena siddhena śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi  RKV 
śrāddhibhyo vastrayugmāni chatropānatkamaṇḍalu 
dakṣiṇā vividhā deyā pitḥn uddiśya bhārata  RKV 
yo dadāti dvijaśreṣṭha tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu 
tasya te dvādaśābdāni tṛptiṃ yānti na saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
asmāhake mahārāja pitaraśca pitāmahāḥ 
vāyubhūtā nirīkṣante āgacchantaṃ svagotrajam  RKV 
atra tīrthe suto 'bhyetya snātvā toyaṃ pradāsyati 
śrāddhaṃ vā piṇḍadānaṃ vā tena yāsyāma sadgatim  RKV 
snāne kṛte tu ye kecij jāyante vastravipluṣaḥ 
prīṇayennarakasthāṃstu taiḥ pitḥn nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
keśodabindavas tasya ye cānye lepabhājinaḥ 
tṛpyantyanagninasaṃskārā yaṃ mṛtāḥ syuḥ svagotrajāḥ  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu ye kecic chrāddhaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ 
narakāduddharantyāśu japantaḥ pitṛsaṃhitām  RKV 
vanaspatigate some yadā somadinaṃ bhavet 
akṣayāllabhate lokānpiṇḍenaikena mānavaḥ  RKV 
akṣayaṃ tatra vai sarvaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
narakāduddharantyāśu japante pitṛsaṃhitām  RKV 
tasmiṃstīrthe tvamāvāsyāṃ pitḥn uddiśya bhārata 
nīlaṃ sarvāṅgasampūrṇaṃ yo 'bhiṣicya samutsṛjet  RKV 
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ na tu vācaspatiḥ kṣamaḥ 
asmāhake vṛṣotsargādyatpuṇyaṃ samavāpyate  RKV 
tava śuśrūṣaṇāt sarvaṃ tatpravakṣyāmi bhārata 
rauravādiṣu ye kiṃcit pacyante tasya pūrvajāḥ  RKV 
vṛṣotsargeṇa tānsarvāṃstārayedekaviṃśatim 
lohito yastu varṇena mukhe pucche ca pāṇḍuraḥ  RKV 
piṅgaḥ khuraviṣāṇābhyāṃ sa nīlo vṛṣa ucyate 
yastu sarvāṅgapiṅgaśca śvetaḥ pucchakhureṣu ca  RKV 
sa piṅgo vṛṣa ityāhuḥ pitḥṇāṃ prītivardhanaḥ 
pārāvatasavarṇaśca lalāṭe tilako bhavet  RKV 
taṃ vṛṣaṃ babhrumityāhuḥ pūrṇaṃ sarvāṅgaśobhanam 
sarvāṅgeṣv ekavarṇo yaḥ piṅgaḥ pucchakhureṣu ca  RKV 
khurapiṅgaṃ tamityāhuḥ pitḥṇāṃ sadgatipradam 
nīlaṃ sarvaśarīreṇa svāraktanayanaṃ dṛḍham  RKV 
tameva nīlamityāhurnīlaḥ pañcavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ 
yastu vaiśyagṛhe jātaḥ sa vai nīlo viśiṣyate  RKV 
na vāhayedgṛhe jātaṃ vatsakaṃ tu kadācana 
tenaiva ca vṛṣotsarge pitḥṇām anṛṇo bhavet  RKV 
jātaṃ tu svagṛhe vatsaṃ dvijanmā yastu vāhayet 
patanti pitarastasya brahmakokagatā api  RKV 
yathāyathā hi pibati pītvā dhūnāti mastakam 
pibanpitḥn prīṇayati narakāduddhared dhunan  RKV 
yathā pucchābhighātena skandhaṃ gacchanti bindavaḥ 
narakāduddharantyāśu patitān gotriṇas tathā  RKV 
garjanprāvṛṣi kāle tu viṣāṇābhyāṃ bhuvaṃ likhan 
khurebhyo yā mṛdudbhūtā tayā saṃprīṇayed ṛṣīn  RKV 
pibanpitḥn prīṇayate khādanollekhane surān 
garjannṛṣimanuṣyāṃśca dharmarūpo hi dharmaja  RKV 
bhūtairvāpi piśācairvā cāturthikajvareṇa vā 
gṛhīto 'smāhakaṃ gacchet sarveṣām ādhināśanam  RKV 
snātvā tu vimale toye darbhagranthiṃ nibandhayet 
mastake bāhumūle vā nābhyāṃ vā galake 'pi vā  RKV 
gatvā devasamīpaṃ ca prādakṣiṇyena keśavam 
tataḥ samuccaran mantraṃ gāyatryā vātha vaiṣṇavam  RKV 
nārāyaṇaṃ śaraṇyeśaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam 
namo yajñāṅgasambhūta sarvavyāpinnamo 'stu te  RKV 
namo namaste deveśa padmagarbha sanātana 
dāmodara jayānanta rakṣa māṃ śaraṇāgatam  RKV 
tvaṃ kartā tvaṃ ca hartā ca jagat yasmiṃścarācare 
tvaṃ pālayasi bhūtāni bhuvanaṃ tvaṃ bibharṣi ca  RKV 
prasīda devadeveśa suptamaṅgaṃ prabodhaya 
tvaddhyānanirato nityaṃ tvadbhaktiparamo hare  RKV 
iti stuto mayā deva prasādaṃ kuru me 'cyuta 
māṃ rakṣa rakṣa pāpebhyastrāyasva śaraṇāgatam  RKV 
evaṃ stutvā ca deveśaṃ dānavāntakaraṃ harim 
punaruktena vai snātvā tato viprāṃstu bhojayet  RKV 
vedoktena vidhānena snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi 
piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kṛtvā vācayetsvastikaṃ tataḥ  RKV 
evaṃ stutvā ca deveśaṃ dānavāntakaraṃ harim 
punaruktena vai snātvā tato viprāṃstu bhojayet  RKV 
vedoktena vidhānena snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi 
evaṃ tānvācayitvā tu tato viprānvisarjayet  RKV 
yattatroccaritaṃ kiṃcittadviprebhyo nivedayet 
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā nārī vā bhaktitatparā 
śaktito dakṣiṇāṃ dadyātkṛtvā śrāddhaṃ yathāvidhi  RKV 
tatra tīrthe naro yāvat snāpayed vidhipūrvakam 
kṣīreṇa madhunā vāpi dadhnā vā śītavāriṇā  RKV 
tāvatpuṣkarapātreṣu pibanti pitaro jalam 
ayane viṣuve caiva yugādau sūryasaṃkrame  RKV 
puṣpaiḥ sampūjya deveśaṃ naivedyaṃ yaḥ pradāpayet 
so 'śvamedhasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti puṣkalam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yo rājan sūryagrahaṇam ācaret 
sūryatejonibhairyānairviṣṇuloke mahīyate  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pitṛbhyaḥ samprayacchati 
satputreṇa ca tenaiva samprāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam  RKV 
iti śrutvā tato devāḥ sarve śakrapurogamāḥ 
brahmaviṣṇumaheśāśca sthāpayāṃcakrur īśvaram  RKV 
sarvarogopaśamanaṃ sarvapātakanāśanam 
yastu saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇamamāvāsyāṃ tu bhāvitaḥ  RKV 
pitṛbhyaḥ piṇḍadānaṃ ca kuryādasmāhake nṛpa 
tripuṣkare gayāyāṃ ca prabhāse naimiṣe tathā  RKV 
yatpuṇyaṃ śrāddhakartḥṇāṃ tadihaiva bhaveddhruvam 
tilodakaṃ kuśairmiśraṃ yo dadyāddakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  RKV 
manvādau ca yugādau ca vyatīpāte dinakṣaye 
yo dadyāt pitṛmātṛbhyaḥ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
asmāhake naro yastu snātvā sampūjayeddharim 
brahmāṇaṃ śaṅkaraṃ bhaktyā kuryāj jāgaraṇakriyām  RKV 
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śakrātithyamavāpnuyāt 
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā yaḥ paśyati janārdanam  RKV 
viśeṣavidhinābhyarcya praṇamya ca punaḥpunaḥ 
saputreṇa ca tenaiva pitḥṇāṃ vihitā gatiḥ  RKV 
ekamūrtistrayo devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ 
satkāryakāraṇopetāḥ susūkṣmāḥ sumahāphalāḥ  RKV 
etatte kathitaṃ rājanmahāpātakanāśanam 
asmāhakasya māhātmyaṃ kimanyat paripṛcchasi  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe asmāhakatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ  
RKV adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla siddheśvaramanuttamam 
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā pūjayed vṛṣabhadhvajam 
sarvapāpavinirmukto gatiṃ yātyaśvamedhinām  RKV 
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā śrāddhaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ 
pitḥṇāṃ prīṇanārthāya sarvaṃ tena kṛtaṃ bhavet  RKV 
tatra tīrthe mṛtānāṃ tu jantūnāṃ nṛpasattama 
garbhavāse matisteṣāṃ na jāyeta kadācana  RKV 
garbhavāso hi duḥkhāya na sukhāya kadācana 
tattīrthavāriṇā snātur na punarbhavasambhavaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe siddheśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma saptacatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo  
'dhyāyaḥ

śrīmārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchenmahīpāla tīrthamaṅgārakaṃ śivam 
uttare narmadākūle sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram  RKV

pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ vācayetpāṇḍunandana  RKV

prīyatāṃ bhūmijo devaḥ sarvadaivatapūjitaḥ  RKV 
vipraṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya patnīputrasamanvitaḥ 
pitṛmātṛsuhṛtsārddhaṃ kṣamāpya ca visarjayet  RKV

aṅgārakapuraṃ yāti devagandharvapūjitaḥ  RKV

surūpaḥ subhagaścaiva sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ 
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ  RKV 
  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇe ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe maṅgaleśvaratīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭācatvāriṃśadadhikaśatatamo

tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snānaṃ kṛtvā devaṃ namasyati

paramāpadgatasyāpi jantoreṣā pratikriyā

tā niśāste ca divasāste māsāste ca vatsarāḥ 
narāṇāṃ saphalā yeṣu cintito bhagavānhariḥ  RKV 
paramāpadgatasyāpi yasya devo janārdanaḥ 
nāvasarpati hṛtpadmātsa yogī nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
te bhāgyahīnā manujāḥ suśocyāste bhūmibhārāya kṛtāvatārāḥ 
acetanāste paśubhiḥ samānā ye bhaktihīnā bhagavatyanante  RKV 
te pūrṇakāryāḥ puruṣāḥ pṛthivyāṃ te svāṅgapātādbhuvanaṃ punanti

sa eva sukṛtī tena labdhaṃ janmataroḥ phalam

etattīrthavaraṃ puṇyaṃ liṅgo yatra janārdanaḥ 
vañcayitvā ripūnsaṃkhye krodho bhūtvā sanātanaḥ  RKV

  iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe liṅgavārāhatīrthamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonapañcāśadadhikaśatatamo

devā ūcuḥ

jagāmākāśamāviśya stūyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ  RKV

sthāpayāmāsa rājendra kusumeśvarasaṃjñitam  RKV

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca

so 'vadhīttava sāmarthyādvadhārthaṃ duṣṭabhūbhṛtām
