etacca kathitaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa dvijottamāḥ 
narmadācaritaṃ puṇyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu durlabham  RKV 
kimanyaiḥ saritāṃ toyaiḥ sevitais tu sahasraśaḥ 
yadi saṃsevyate toyaṃ revāyāḥ pāpanāśanam  RKV 
mekalājalasaṃsevī muktimāpnoti śāśvatīm  RKV 
yathā yathā bhajenmartyo yadyadicchati tīrthagaḥ 
tattadāpnoti niyataṃ śraddhayāśraddhayāpi ca  RKV 
idaṃ brahmā hariridamidaṃ sākṣātparo haraḥ 
idaṃ brahma nirākāraṃ kaivalyaṃ narmadājalam  RKV 
tāvadgarjanti tīrthāni nadyo hṛdayaphalapradāḥ 
yāvanna smaryate revā sevāhevā kalau naraiḥ  RKV 
dhruvaṃ loke hitārthāya śivena svaśarīrataḥ 
śaktiḥ kāpi saridrūpā reveyamavatāritā  RKV 
tāvadgarjanti yajñāśca vanakṣetrādayo bhṛśam 
yāvanna narmadānāmakīrtanaṃ kriyate kalau  RKV 
garimā gāṇyate tāvattapodānavratādiṣu 
narairvā prāpyate yāvadbhuvi bhargabhavā dhunī  RKV 
ye vasantyuttare kūle rudrasyānucarā hi te 
vasanti yāmyatīre ye lokaṃ te yānti vaiṣṇavam  RKV 
dhanyāste deśavaryāste yeṣu deśeṣu narmadā 
narakāntakarī śaśvatsaṃśritā śarvanirmitā  RKV 
kṛtapuṇyāśca te lokāḥ śokāya na bhavanti te 
ye pibanti jalaṃ puṇyaṃ pārvatīpatisindhujam  RKV 
idaṃ pavitramatulaṃ revāyāścaritaṃ dvijāḥ 
śṛṇoti yaḥ kīrtayate mucyate sarvapātakaḥ  RKV 
yatphalaṃ sarvavedaiśca saṣaḍaṅgapadakramaiḥ 
śrutaiśca paṭhitaistasmātphalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet  RKV 
satrayājī phalaṃ yacca labhate dvādaśābdikam 
śrutvā sakṛcca revāyāścaritaṃ tatphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
sarvatīrthāvagāhācca yatphalaṃ sāgarādiṣu 
sakṛcchrutvā ca māhātmyaṃ revāyās tatphalaṃ labhet  RKV 
etaddharmyamupākhyānaṃ sarvaśāstreṣvanuttamam 
deśe vā maṇḍale vāpi nagare grāmamadhyataḥ  RKV 
gṛhe vā tiṣṭhate yasya likhitaṃ sārvavārṇikam 
sa brahmā sa śivaḥ sākṣātsa ca devo janārdanaḥ  RKV 
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ mārge 'yaṃ devasevitaḥ 
gurūṇāṃ ca guruḥ śāstraṃ paramaṃ siddhikāraṇam  RKV 
yaścedaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ purāṇaṃ devabhāṣitam 
brāhmaṇo vedavānbhūyātkṣatriyo vijayī bhavet  RKV 
dhanāḍhyo jāyate vaiśyaḥ śūdro vai dharmabhāg bhavet  RKV 
saubhāgyasantatiṃ nārī śrutvaitatsamavāpnuyāt 
śriyaṃ saukhyaṃ svargavāsaṃ janma caivottame kule  RKV 
rasabhedī kṛtaghnaśca svāmidhruṅ mitravañcakaḥ 
goghnaśca garadaścaiva kanyāvikrayakārakaḥ  RKV 
brahmaghnaśca surāpī ca steyī ca gurutalpagaḥ 
narmadācaritaṃ śṛṇvaṃstāmabdaṃ yo 'bhiṣevate  RKV 
sarvapāpavinirmukto jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
pākabhedī vṛthāpākī devabrāhmaṇanindakaḥ  RKV 
parīvādī guroḥ pitroḥ sādhūnāṃ nṛpatestathā 
te 'pi śrutvā ca pāpebhyo mucyante nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
ye punarbhāvitātmānaḥ śastraṃ śṛṇvanti nityaśaḥ 
pūjayanti ca tacchāstraṃ nārmadaṃ vastrabhūṣaṇaiḥ  RKV 
puṣpaiḥ phalaiś candanādyair bhojanair vividhair api 
śāstre 'sminpūjite devāḥ pūjitā guravastathā  RKV 
iha loke pare caiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena gandhavastrādibhūṣaṇaiḥ  RKV 
pūjayetparayā bhaktyā vācakaṃ śāstrameva ca 
vedapāṭhaiśca yatpuṇyamagnihotraiśca pālitaiḥ  RKV 
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti narmadācarite śubhe 
kurukṣetre ca yatpuṇyaṃ prabhāse puṣkare tathā  RKV 
rudrāvarte gayāyāṃ ca vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame  RKV 
evamādiṣu tīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ jāyate nṛṇām 
narmadācaritaṃ śrutvā tatpuṇyaṃ sakalaṃ labhet  RKV 
ādimadhyāvasāneṣu narmadācaritaṃ śubham 
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā śṛṇudhvaṃ tatphalaṃ mahat  RKV 
samāpya śivasaṃsthānaṃ devakanyāsamāvṛtaḥ 
rudrasyānucaro bhūtvā śivena saha modate  RKV 
dharmākhyānamidaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvākhyāneṣvanuttamam 
gṛhe 'pi paṭhyate yasya caturvarṇasya sattamāḥ  RKV 
dhanyaṃ tasya gṛhaṃ manye gṛhasthaṃ cāpi tatkulam 
pustakaṃ pūjayedyastu narmadācaritasya tu  RKV 
narmadā pūjitā tena bhagavāṃśca maheśvaraḥ 
vācake pūjite tadvaddevāśca ṛṣayo 'rcitāḥ  RKV 
lekhayitvā ca sakalaṃ revācaritamuttamam 
bhūṣaṇaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ yo dadāti dvijanmane  RKV 
narmadāsarvatīrtheṣu snānadānena yatphalam 
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti sa naro nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKV 
etatpurāṇaṃ rudroktaṃ mahāpuṇyaphalapradam 
svargadaṃ putradaṃ dhanyaṃ yaśasyaṃ kīrttivardhanam  RKV 
dharmyamāyuṣyamatulaṃ duḥkhaduḥsvapnanāśanam 
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ cāpi sarvakāmārthasiddhidam  RKV 
yatpradattamidaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vācyate dvijaiḥ 
śivaloke sthitis tasya purāṇākṣaravatsarī  RKV 
iti nigaditametannarmadāyāścaritraṃ pavanagaditamagryaṃ śarvavaktrādavāpya 
tribhuvanajanavandyaṃ tvetadādau munīnāṃ kulapatipuratas tat sūtamukhyena sādhu  RKV 
 iti śrīskānde mahāpurāṇa ekāśītisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ pañcama āvantyakhaṇḍe revākhaṇḍe
revākhaṇḍasamāptirevākhaṇḍapustakadānādimāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśadadhikadviśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
